Let Us Become God's Victorious Elite Soldiers

2 Timothy 2:1-13
<Prayer (I)> Heavenly Father, please allow this one hour to be a time when the life of the original nature that we possessed before the Fall is infused into us. Please allow this to be an altar of life overflowing with Heavenly Father's love.
Please allow us to feel the blocking wall of death with our minds and bodies at this hour. Thus, by receiving the grace of resurrection, let us build an altar of glory and become those who can go forth with new candles on all the scattered altars. Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
Is there anyone with a wounded heart? Please look upon them with compassion. Are there any traces left on their bodies from being captured by Satan? Please remove them. And so, please allow them to be able to take on the original form before the Fall. Loving Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
Heavenly Father, please appear with words of power. Please remold all of us and bring about the work of re-creation. Loving Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
You have called each and every one of us from difficult circumstances, so now we will cross the hill of trials and difficulties. The time has come when we must raise a song of victory in the remaining battle of reality. Therefore, Heavenly Father, please add strength to our strength, add ability to our ability, and appear with the authority of resurrection.
April 8, 1956 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church.

8

Let Us Become God's Victorious Elite Soldiers

Please allow the spirits that were trapped in darkness to be liberated, and resurrect them with the flames of hope. Please grant us the flames of Heavenly Father's life that can more than illuminate the blocked garden of truth, this world ruled by evil, and the foundation of Heavenly Father's 6,000-year resentment. My Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
We know that the new history begins with Heavenly Father at the center. And we also know that it was a historical fact that if the standard of history was not placed in heaven, it could not become the standard of the entire history.
Heavenly Father! Since you have established us, please allow us to accomplish the new history, and establish us as the heavenly elite soldiers of the new era, so that we can build a new garden and return the glory of joy to Heavenly Father. Please grant us this grace. Loving Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
We have entered the same path that the prophets and saints went, breaking through the barriers of battle. We have entered the path that is said to be difficult. We have entered a path from which we cannot turn back. We know that the time has come when we must fight with autonomous courage toward a one-sided goal. Please allow us to become the heavenly elite soldiers who can, by pouring out all our final passion, make a bold decision against Satan, stand at the forefront, raise the flag before others, and charge toward Satan.
Heavenly Father, until we can gather the remaining altar of battle as an altar of victory and settle it as Heavenly Father's altar of rest and glory, please protect the path we are going, and consecrate the place where we stay, so that we can plant the white flag of joyful victory before this nation and the 2.4 billion people of humankind and have more to spare. Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
Father, at this hour, even if it is a small number of family members, we have gathered to immerse ourselves in Father's love with one mind. Therefore, please allow us to be immersed in the Father's love that has been hidden, even for just this one hour.
Please reveal the love of heaven and the history of truth that have been hidden for 6,000 years, and reveal the history of resurrection, and allow us to receive the liberation of freedom from our minds and bodies and become the true sons and daughters of the Father. Please establish us as children who can face the Father with a song of victory and face the Father with the glory of victory. Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
This is a holy day. To the altars gathered on behalf of the 30 million people, Heavenly Father, please work. If there is a dead altar, please show the work of life. Regardless of the time, the environment, or the place, Heavenly Father, please work.
Please raise the beacon of life that has been sleeping, and allow us to go forth with a new flag of life through the conscientious children, the children who follow the Father, and please allow there to be many children who can protect the hidden altars. Loving Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
We have gathered at this hour, so Heavenly Father, please consecrate our spirits, and if there are any self-centered ideas or elements of sin, or any unclean dark roots remaining, please appear with the work of the Holy Spirit like a flame of fire and lead us. Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
We earnestly ask and desire that you allow us to become sons and daughters who fulfill our mission, who carry out the mission entrusted to us without any shortcomings, and who can save face before the tens of thousands of saints and the family members of that land by dedicating our minds and bodies to this one will.
Please protect us so that no one is caught in the conditions of Satan's accusation from the beginning to the end of this hour, and allow even one more life to be moved by the grace of resurrection, to taste the joy of new life, and to receive the grace of new life. And so, please allow this hour to be a time of returning the glory of the resurrection of new life to Heavenly Father. Loving Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
Now I entrust everything to you, so please allow the fundamental work of the living life to appear from the beginning to the end of the hour, and please allow only the will of joy to be revealed. I have prayed in the name of the Lord. Amen.
<Prayer (II)> Heavenly Father, on this day too, though we are lacking and sinful, a small number of family members have prostrated themselves before the Father's holy temple.
Until now, you have commanded through the prophets you have raised, you have commanded through the Holy Spirit, and you have commanded through Christ, but we know that you, Heavenly Father, have not yet commanded in person.
10

Let Us Become God's Victorious Elite Soldiers

Please allow the words of the Father's command, which you have not been able to give in person, to appear here. And so, please allow the Father's will, which you intended to accomplish through the Holy Spirit and through Jesus Christ, to appear here.
We know that the Father desires to fulfill the will of joy. Before the Father's will, we want to pour out all of our lacking devotion, we want to offer all of our lacking loyalty, and we want to offer all of our lacking bodies, so Heavenly Father, please extend your hand of compassion.
On our hands and feet, there are marks of Satan's arrows, and on our bodies, we have the wounds of battle. Father of compassion! Please allow your hand to hold our hands and feet that have the marks of Satan's arrows, and hold our wounded bodies, and apply the oil of life, and wrap us with the new bandage of resurrection. We desire a single word of new exhortation, so Heavenly Father, please exhort us. I earnestly ask and desire this.
Please remove all worldly minds and all natures that belonged to sin, and allow us to cherish only the original nature that can admire the Father.
Heavenly Father, now that you have called and gathered us, please command us. Please allow us to find what is the center of the providence that the Father wants to find, and please allow us to find what is the center of the heavenly law that the Father wants to find.
Heavenly Father, please descend at this hour. We have prostrated ourselves meekly and humbly to repay the words that the Father has given us. We know nothing, and our bodies are wounded, but we want to be offered to the Father, so please accept us. Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
At this hour, Heavenly Father, please take charge of everything. We who have now come before the will, know that we must bear fruit with life, so at this time when the end is approaching, Heavenly Father, please grant us your hand of life.
We know that even if the world and history may change, the Father's life does not change, so please allow us to run toward the eternal life, the unchanging standard.
11

At this hour, if there are any children who are not worthy of that one standard, please command them one by one, and grant them your hand of power, and work so that they may resemble the Father's divine image. Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this.
We have gathered before the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit, so please remove their subjective ideas and grant them the work of life. May the Father alone become the center of their minds and bodies, the center of the entire gathering, and the shield of victory, and please allow this to be a joyful hour.
Please establish them as children who will not be wounded even if they have a head-on collision with Satan, by forming the flesh and blood of eternal life and creating the shield of eternal victory with the elements of life found from this day on. Heavenly Father, I earnestly ask and desire this. I entrust everything to you, so please take charge. I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen.
<Sermon> The words I want to give you today are, "Let Us Become God's Victorious Elite Soldiers." I will speak for a moment on this topic.
We Are the Ones Responsible for the Battle and the Embodiment of Hope
The term "elite soldier" is not a word that has existed from the beginning. It is a word that came into being because human beings fell, and it was a word that could not but come out. In other words, because the battle remains, and because sons and daughters were needed who could take charge of the battle on behalf of God, this word came into being.
Unless these sons and daughters are established and go through the course of battle until a certain time, God's will cannot be completed, so He chose these sons and daughters, and God Himself has been fighting Satan on earth for the long period of 6,000 years, repeating the changing history.
However, who are the responsible ones who must take responsibility for this history of God's battle and come to the forefront to fight the actual battle?
It is not God who fights directly, nor is it Jesus Christ who fights directly, nor is it the Holy Spirit who fights directly. You all know well that the saints who believe well with God, Jesus Christ, and the Holy Spirit in the background are in charge of the direct responsibility for this battle.
12

Let Us Become God's Victorious Elite Soldiers

This battle must be concluded by all means. However, 2,000 years have passed since Jesus Christ came and went, but this battle has not yet been concluded. Now we must expand the ground of this battle and create the foundation for victory, but who are the beings who will take on this responsibility? It is none other than us, who are insignificant and worthless.
When we think about this, we can see that God's hope is not in God Himself. And the hope of Jesus Christ is not in Jesus Christ himself, and the hope of the Holy Spirit is not in the Holy Spirit itself, and the hope that the prophets and saints desire is not in themselves. It is in none other than us, who are insignificant and remain on this earth today.
Then, if heaven is calling you who are on the earth, what standard are they using to call you? God's 6,000-year providence as a whole
is setting the standard and calling you.
Therefore, you must be well aware that you have the responsibility to conclude with victory the 6,000 years, and furthermore, the countless eons of human history. And you must know well that Father is calling us in this way. Not only that, but you must become the true elite soldiers of Heaven who take responsibility for the age, for history, and for the eternal providence.
Pioneering the great destiny of the providence directly is not something for Jesus Christ to do, not something for the Holy Spirit to do, and not something for God to do, but it is precisely what we must do.

To Become Heavenly Elite Soldiers

We must be able to look at ourselves, who carry such a great mission, and criticize ourselves from a third-person perspective. We must consider whether we have become people who can answer with dignity even if the Father Himself appears and questions us. Have I become a heavenly elite soldier equipped with the courage, pride, and conviction to take responsibility for the entire providence and fight? Even if the Father asks, have I become someone who can answer without hesitation, “Yes! That is correct.”… Heaven is looking for such beings who can answer with dignity.
Then what are the conditions to become such elite soldiers? Within ourselves, we cannot find the conditions to become heavenly elite soldiers. If so, how can we become heavenly elite soldiers?
For us to become heavenly elite soldiers, we must emulate the one who has already appeared as the representative heavenly elite soldier, that is, Jesus Christ, in whom we believe. From the background of Jesus Christ’s coming, his life and his entire ideal are contents that we can boast about to Satan. And they are the contents and conditions that we must absolutely emulate to become heavenly elite soldiers. You must keep this in mind.
The same is true of his words, the same is true of the principle of the cross he showed as he passed away, and the same is true of the principle of the resurrection he left behind. All these things are the absolute conditions and laws that we must possess in order to conclude all historical battles and become heavenly elite soldiers. We must be equipped with these conditions.
However, what we need to know here is that Jesus Christ also prepared, made efforts, and suffered for some 30 years of his life until he was equipped with all the conditions that a heavenly elite soldier must have. It did not happen in a day, nor did it happen in a single moment. He had to go through a long course of trials for some 30 years.
Then what is the course that Jesus Christ walked when he came to this earth? As a heavenly elite soldier, he showed the conditions of trial, the course of trial, that must be overcome to win against Satan on earth.
Jesus said on the cross, “It is finished.” He did not say this because it was all finished on the cross. He said it because he had fulfilled all the conditions that a heavenly elite soldier must have before being hung on the cross. And he said it in the sense that he had fulfilled all the missions he had to do as a heavenly elite soldier.

Let Us Become Victorious Elite Soldiers of God

Because Jesus was a heavenly elite soldier who lacked nothing, Heaven was able to resurrect him after he passed away on the cross. Therefore, after Jesus’ resurrection, Jesus has been working in heaven and the Holy Spirit on earth, fighting against Satan for 2,000 years.

The Lesson from the Life of Jesus Christ

You must keep in mind that the course of trial that we, who have been called by Heaven, must now keep is none other than the path of Jesus Christ, who walked it for some 30 years of his life.
When we consider the course of Jesus Christ’s 30-odd years of life, he walked the 30-year course of his private life, went through the 3-year course of his public life, and concluded the trials during the 3-day period in the tomb.
Not only must my individual self follow the way of the cross and the path of resurrection, but all of humankind in the entire world must walk this path.
The fact that Jesus Christ received the grace of resurrection after he passed away on the cross was not as easy as you might think. It is not a principle that was accomplished in one day, nor is it a principle that was accomplished in a few hours. You must know that it is a principle that was accomplished through victory after walking a path of suffering for some 30 years, combining the heart of God who went through a long 4,000-year history and the heart of Jesus Christ.
We are living a life of faith and reading the Bible, but we should not interpret the Bible according to our own will. Believers often think that the way of the cross was accomplished only on the cross, but that is not the case. You must know that it is a principle that was accomplished at the end of a life of suffering that others did not know, without eating well or dressing well for some 30 years. And you must know that Jesus is the only-begotten Son of God who perfectly fulfilled the remaining conditions of a heavenly elite soldier.
Now we must analyze what the lesson from the life of Jesus Christ is and repeat the course of Christ’s suffering from the beginning of our faith in Jesus. You too must go through a course of trials. During the course of Jesus Christ’s trials, there will be battles. And you must emulate Christ who fought not for 10 years, not for 20 years, but for 30 years, and you must emulate the unchanging heart of Jesus Christ who was not afraid of death.
What you need to know now is that you yourselves are the ones who must bear the remaining path of suffering and the path of death, protect the cross, and keep the way of the cross.
After Jesus Christ came and went, the apostles had the responsibility to protect the fortress of the cross that Jesus had built on this earth and to take the first step of the fierce battle. You must know that the saints of the last days now have the responsibility to protect the remaining fortress of the cross.
The time has come when we must decide victory or defeat in the final decisive battle, and the crucial issue here is whether I have become an elite soldier who can remain, and whether I can bring about a second history of resurrection, a revival, just as Christ died and was resurrected.
Jesus is waging a battle even in the spirit world. He is fighting against Satan on behalf of countless good saints. The one who came to wage a battle on earth in imitation of Jesus who is fighting in the spirit world is the Holy Spirit. We have the responsibility to actually fight with the help of the Holy Spirit. In other words, we are the ones who must become the heavenly elite soldiers who actually take charge of that battle.

When We Must Resolve the 6,000 Years of Resentment

Now the final battle has begun, and you today must know that the battle you are fighting is not a battle for you alone. You must know that the battle is a battle connected to you from heaven through the Holy Spirit. And the purpose of that battle is to cast out Satan.
Therefore, we must now cross over the hill of battle and become the elite soldiers who take responsibility for the cross of Christ that remains, all the way to the original homeland, and sing a song of victory. We must become elite soldiers of victory who have resolved the 6,000 years of resentment and fulfilled the 6,000 years of desire.

Let Us Become Victorious Elite Soldiers of God

We must become elite soldiers of joy.
The group that appeared as the representative elite soldiers who took responsibility for the fortress of the cross left behind after Christ was the 12 apostles. The 12 apostles went beyond death to protect the walls of the cross, and they defended the walls of the cross without hesitation, offering their bodies and minds and shedding their blood and flesh. Heaven is looking for such elite soldiers.
The traces of blood shed by the prophets and saints as they walked the path of the gospel still remain on the walls of the cross. And this land is a land where the resentment and blood of our ancestors are pooled, and a land where the appeal of blood remains. The ones who will resolve this resentment are none other than us. The death of Jesus Christ is a resentful thing, but the deaths of the prophets and saints are also resentful. You must be able to feel resentment for the deaths of the prophets and saints as well as the death of Christ.
Now we must know that the time has come to have resentment. The time has come to resolve the resentment of heaven that has been endured and endured for 6,000 years. What is needed at this time is heavenly elite soldiers. What is required in this age is heavenly elite soldiers.
We must become the true sons and daughters of God who can say, “Father! Let the 6,000 years of resentment explode through me!” If there are many such true sons and daughters among the 30 million people, the way for the 30 million people to live will be opened. Also, if such people become priests and protect the walls of the cross and become fighting elite soldiers, this nation will not be destroyed. Today, we believers must become such heavenly elite soldiers.
Jesus Christ, who came to this earth and died on the cross, built a temple of victory in the spirit world and has been expanding that temple. If you look through the spirit world, you will know that the darkness of the fall had reached below the throne of God. As a result of repeating battles and adding toil to toil, a foundation was finally prepared after Jesus. The battle to expand this foundation even more has continued to this day, and the battle with Satan has continued on earth as well. Heaven is now hoping that heavenly elite soldiers will emerge who can finish this battle.
Now we must be aroused. Jesus Christ not only toiled and fought for some 30 years of his life on this earth until he crossed the hill of the cross of death, but he also continued to fight for 2,000 years. You ignorant people who do not know this battle…. You must appeal to yourselves. Before you appeal to the people, before you appeal to the family, society, the world, and the earth, you must appeal to yourselves.
You must fight for the will, emulating Jesus Christ who fought for the will for 2,000 years. Therefore, you must win in heaven and win on earth, so that heaven and earth can respond to each other, represent the heart of God, and reveal the beauty of the original creation. This is the purpose for which God has providentially worked for 6,000 years, and the will for which He sent Jesus Christ.

What Heavenly Elite Soldiers Must Know

Now we must become heavenly elite soldiers and protect the walls of the cross. You must become heavenly elite soldiers in this way, and you must be able to discern which corps of elite soldiers you belong to.
Because the history of the earth is a history that develops the history of heaven in a figurative way, just as there are 12 corps of elite soldiers in heaven centered on the 12 apostles, on earth there are 12 denominations of the Israelite 12-tribe type and countless peripheral corps.
These corps have been formed over the course of 2,000 years of history, and you must know which corps you belong to. You must know what kind of self you are, belonging to which unit of the heavenly army, which is systematically organized just like the armies of the world, which are organized into squads, platoons, companies, battalions, regiments, divisions, and so on.
And now you must know what kind of mission you are being commanded to focus on.
Now, after going through the process of battle, we must greet the time when the entire created world can rejoice, centered on one center. That center is none other than Jesus Christ and the Holy Spirit, in whom we believe.

Let Us Become Victorious Elite Soldiers of God

What is the ultimate purpose of the heavenly elite soldiers? It is to complete the battle with Satan and receive a reward from God and Christ. It is to win the battle and receive the reward of heaven on earth.
Now the battle is taking place on all fronts. It is taking place all over the world. Also, the will of the providence is unfolding throughout heaven and earth. You must become elite soldiers who win in the individual battle, win in the family battle, win in the social, national, and world battles, and win in the battle taking place in heaven and on earth.
Jesus Christ has not been able to conclude the battle that is taking place in heaven and on earth. Therefore, you must become the elite soldiers who protect the departments of each front and conclude the battles of each front. Only when you win as a limb with Christ as the head, and after your body and mind become one, and you offer worship before heaven, will all things in heaven and earth be in harmony.
You must now pass through the traces of blood left by the apostles, and you must take command and responsibility for the company if it is a company, or the battalion if it is a battalion, that the apostles commanded. Furthermore, you must take responsibility for the responsibilities that Jesus Christ and the Holy Spirit are bearing.

Ultimate Goal of the Heavenly Elite Soldiers
Heaven does not want a battlefield to remain on earth. Because resentment has been맺힌 on earth, the battle of Jesus Christ can be concluded and Christ can come again only when we win on earth and resolve the resentment. What does He do after He comes again? He concludes the battle that has been going on for 6,000 years and receives blessings from God. A banquet where God personally raises both hands to bless. The banquet of the Lamb is a banquet where the victorious elite soldiers gather and are all blessed together, and this banquet of the Lamb is to be held.

You must directly receive the words that God, the commander-in-chief, commands. You must go to the position of directly receiving God's command on behalf of Jesus.

In Revelation 14, it is written, "Then I looked, and behold, on Mount Zion stood the Lamb, and with him 144,000 who had his name and his Father's name written on their foreheads." (v. 1) As it is recorded, you must receive the seal of the Father.

Until now, you have been guided by the Holy Spirit and by Jesus Christ, but this is not all. You must receive the seal of the Father to become eternal elite soldiers not only on earth but also in the kingdom of heaven. Please keep in mind that you must go to that position.

After you individually become such elite soldiers, you must make all of humanity become such elite soldiers.

You must become not only the elite soldiers of Christ by winning all battles, but also the original human beings, the true sons and daughters who have completed the ideal of creation, with whom God can be pleased. The time must come when the triumphant cry of Hosanna returned by such heavenly elite soldiers shakes the whole earth, and then God's resentment against Satan will be resolved at once. You must know this for sure.

The battle still remains. Therefore, you must launch the final attack, cross the hill of battle, receive God's seal, and become elite soldiers who can make Satan surrender before God. Only then will the battle with Satan be concluded.

The battle does not end even if you make Satan surrender before the Holy Spirit and before Jesus Christ. The battle is concluded only when you make Satan surrender before God.

The Father has suffered through the 6,000-year history of the providence to create these victorious elite soldiers. Knowing this Father, you must become victorious heavenly elite soldiers. *

Jesus Christ, Who Became God's Pride

2 Corinthians 8:16-24

<Prayer (I)> Beloved Father, this is the day you have granted the gift of atonement to all people. Please allow us not to forget at this hour the bloody course of the Father who worked while leaving behind traces of labor in the course of the ever-changing history, and the traces of martyrdom of the pioneers who went before us.

Please allow this one hour of worship before the Father on this day to be a time of offering sacrifices as earnestly as Abel's appeal of blood. Please guide us so that we do not become a group centered on our perishable bodies, and allow us, though a small and insignificant group, to build an Abel-type altar on behalf of the 30 million people, just as Abel became a fragrant offering before the Father and all things on the altar of sanctification.

I earnestly hope and pray, my beloved Father, that you will not allow us to stand in a position of boasting of ourselves from Cain's position, seeing Abel shed his blood.

Please allow the heart of heaven and the heart of the appeal of blood to overflow. On this earth, the stains of the blood of the righteous still remain, this is a bloody land, a land with the lump of sighs of hundreds of millions of years, so please allow many children among the 30 million people to appear as offerings of joy before the Father for this and offer worship of gratitude. Please allow many among the 2.4 billion people of humankind.

May 16, 1956 (Wednesday), former headquarters church.

I earnestly hope and pray, beloved Father, that a multitude of children will appear in every corner of the country who can tear down the wall of sin accumulated over hundreds of millions of years, create a garden of joy, and attend the Father in joy and glory.

We have lived until today forgetting that the hand of heaven has labored for 6,000 years to find me and to establish me. Please allow us not to stand in a position of forgetting that the reason I can live comfortably and believe comfortably today is not because I am great, but because of the bloody and laborious hands of countless prophets and saints who are enshrined in the course of history until my own self came to be in this position today.

Please establish them as children who can worship the Father as one offering that prostrates itself in meekness and humility, as one offering that is given, as one offering of joy that is offered, Father, I earnestly hope and pray.

Father, please awaken this sleeping castle. Please have pity on this people who are wandering in the darkness, not knowing the direction. For this, please quickly establish the children you will establish, and please quickly call the children you will call. Please allow it to be quickly established as a beloved altar that can represent the whole by establishing a center toward heaven.

Please allow this entire nation to be victorious, and guide them to be grateful for the holy grace and to praise the holy light, beloved Father, I earnestly hope and pray.

Father, a small group has gathered in this place today, so please take charge. Please take control. Please have insight into the center of each individual's heart, and please do not allow the center of the heart that they have established themselves, the heart of the self, to stand in a place that begins with the self and ends with the self. Please do not allow them to stand in a place of forming their own ideology through the perception and concept of the self and being intoxicated with self-satisfaction.

Please allow them to be meek and humble offerings before the heart of parents, frankly laying out all their own concepts or assertions. I earnestly hope and pray, beloved Father, that you will allow this to be a time when we can deeply feel our own insufficiency before the majestic Father and fundamentally offer all of ourselves to the Father.

Jesus Christ, Who Became God's Pride

I earnestly hope and pray.

Father, since you have gathered them and established them and have already sounded a new alarm in this castle, you must take full responsibility, Father. You must complete the entire mission, and you must take charge of the entire work, so please allow them to quickly step up and rise above this age, and Father, please allow them to become heavenly elite soldiers who can stand at the forefront and go out to fight.

Please establish them as elite soldiers who can represent these 30 million people, so that they will not be lacking whether they stand before the tens of thousands of saints, before the angels in heaven, or before the saints on this earth, beloved Father, I earnestly hope and pray.

During the three days, there was much time when I thought only of myself, and there was much time when I lived to love only myself, and I wasted much time to make excuses for myself. However, please forgive me for not living in the position that the Father desires, where I cannot but go and cannot but move to find the Father, forgetting myself, to fulfill the Father's desire, forgetting myself, and to reveal the Father's overall value.

Please do not allow those who have come out to find the Father at this hour to be those who have come only with a conceptual attitude of faith and a mind to receive blessings, and please do not allow them to be those who have only a mind to receive grace. The history of the appeal, "Save me," has passed 6,000 years, so please allow this to be a time when we can pray, "Receive me, Father," as the cry of prayer, "I offer all of myself, so please receive me," is heard from the earth and reaches heaven.

Please allow us to ask ourselves whether we ourselves have become offerings worthy of the Father, and whenever we stand before the holy body of the manifested Father, to keenly feel our own insufficiency and to feel that we are sinners, and to bow our heads and worship the Father. Please awaken us at this hour so that a heart of repentance may arise, and that we may feel the original nature of goodness and the substance of goodness, and worship on behalf of the Father's glory.

We know that this work is the desire of heaven, and that heaven is being mobilized for this one will, so please let the Trinity move and the work of the Holy Spirit appear, and place the whole under your hand, and Father, please take charge of the entire event. I earnestly hope and pray, Father, that you will guide us to form an altar of saints who offer the whole to the Father, without having any concepts or perceptions that deviate from the Father's will.

Please bless every place where lonely groups are offering earnest pleas to heaven at this hour, and since they have set out under heaven's command that they cannot but go, please protect the children who have pledged to go without regard for the path of death, the path of battle, the path of refuge, the path of adversity, or the summit of Golgotha.

Those who follow behind those who go on a difficult path will also have difficulties, and I know that there will be many wounds from following that path, so Father, you must take responsibility for this. Please take them as offerings in place of the Father and grant them the heart and the gift of love of the Father that you will allow at the last day.

Please let the direct work of your dominion, where they can be immersed in joy and feel the Father's pleasure, be with each of their hearts, and in every place where they are, please come personally and comfort them so that they are not held by the cross of the environment, and please personally admonish them. The path of battle is not far and the remaining hill is not high, so I earnestly hope and pray, Father, that the direct work of admonition will be with them so that they can overcome it.

At this hour, we have come out with our hearts bound together to see the Father, and we wish to have a time of worship, so from the first hour to the last, please lead the entire meeting with the protection of your love and the gift of your love, and please bless us to become offerings of the gift that the Father desires, I have prayed in the beloved name of the Lord. Amen.

<Prayer (II)> We know that the Garden of Creation is a garden of goodness, a garden of love, a garden of oneness, and a garden of harmony. We know that it is our responsibility to be good according to God's love, it is our responsibility to become one, and it is our responsibility to be in harmony.

<Sermon> Therefore, show to them in the presence of the churches the proof of your love and of our boasting about you. (2 Cor. 8:24) Centering on these words, today I will speak on the topic, “Jesus Christ Who Became God's Pride.”
Adam and Eve, Who Should Have Become God's Pride
God, who created all things in heaven and earth, created Adam and Eve as the embodiment of God's pride in all things in heaven and earth. He also created Adam and Eve as the embodiment of God's pride in the angelic world. And when Adam and Eve stood before all things, all things had to bow down to Adam and Eve.
This garden of creation that was created in this way was broken due to the fall of man. That is, due to the fall of man, the value of all things, which should have been a source of pride before man, could not be properly manifested. Man, who could have appeared as the center of value in the formless world, lost that qualification, and the position of man, who should have received glory as the center of harmony, appearing before all things on behalf of God as the meaning of God's pride, was fundamentally broken.
Therefore, what was the standard that God has been seeking until today, six thousand years after the fall of man? He has been seeking one representative who can represent God's heart, represent His form, represent God's character, and represent the work of the heavenly law, a representative whom God can be proud of.
Also, until now, Jesus Christ has also been toiling for this one will. Then, what kind of person was Jesus Christ, who came to this earth four thousand years after the fall of Adam and Eve? He was the one who represented God's internal heart and external form. Therefore, God intended to reveal the “standard of pride” that He had established with His ideal of creation through Jesus Christ. This was the original mission that Jesus Christ had to carry out.
Therefore, we must know that Jesus Christ stood in the position of a great person in charge who had to appear as a child representing God's heart and form in every part or any one part of his life through his life.
In this way, Jesus had to appear as a substantial being whom God could be proud of. First, he had to be able to be proud before all things, and then he had to be able to be proud before Satan, and he had to be able to be proud before the tens of thousands of saints. And he had to greet the one day of restoring what God had intended to rejoice and receive glory centering on Adam and Eve. This was God's will in His work and providence, having established Jesus as the central being.
God had the people of Israel build the nation of Israel, and
In their midst, He sent Jesus Christ to be established before you. Therefore, if the people of Israel had united to praise Jesus Christ and had treated him with a heart of gratitude based on the standard that God had intended to boast of, this historical sorrow would not have been prolonged for six thousand years.

Jesus, the King of Faith, Established as God’s Boast

What was visible in the eyes of Jesus Christ, who appeared as God’s boast, and what the people of Israel were boasting of were vastly different. That is, the way the people of Israel, who came forth to fulfill God’s will for the providence of restoration, boasted of themselves as God’s chosen people was different from the way Jesus Christ, who fought to uphold God’s will for the providence of restoration, boasted for the sake of God’s will. Therefore, the people of Israel had to be in a position to abandon their national pride, which they had built up until then, before the words of Jesus, who could boast on behalf of God, and before the life of Jesus.

If they had abandoned their own pride and humbly bowed down before Jesus Christ, who appeared with a new boast to boast on behalf of God’s will, the difficult gate of the cross would not have remained before Jesus Christ. In the history of Christianity, there would have been no such thing as the way of the cross. There would have been the words that one is saved by listening to the words of Jesus, but there would have been no such words that one is saved by believing in the cross.

Today, we bless the death of Jesus Christ and believe that the cross has the authority of redemption, but that is not everything. Christians today have forgotten that the words Jesus Christ spoke during his lifetime had the authority of redemption. What we need to know is that, of course, spiritual redemption is possible by believing in the cross of Christ, but if we had believed in the words Jesus spoke during his lifetime and practiced them as he said, redemption of both spirit and body would have been achieved.

Then what should Jesus Christ have boasted of first when he came to this earth? Adam and Eve failed to establish God’s word because of their fall.

Jesus Christ, Who Became God’s Boast

They did not believe the word. Therefore, because human beings fell by not believing God’s word and the providential history was prolonged for four thousand years, the one center that Jesus Christ established before Satan to block this prolonged four-thousand-year history was faith. In other words, Jesus appeared on this earth as the king of faith.

What kind of person is Jesus? And where did Jesus establish the one standard of value by which he could stand as God’s boast? In the course of four thousand years of history, Jesus appeared as the king of faith before all people who could not believe anyone and could not face God’s will. Therefore, God was able to boast of the faith of Jesus Christ.

Many people said they believed in God, but with such faith, they could not establish an internal relationship of high and low through the heavenly heart of God. Also, numerous prophets and sages came and went, but through what they believed and followed, they could not know the principle of love that permeated God’s heart. Furthermore, Jesus Christ took charge of the entire historical process of faith that numerous saints had walked and tried to cut off all the history of Satan single-handedly. Jesus Christ, in the position of bringing to fruition the four thousand years of faith, came and went as the central figure of the universe, the protagonist of faith.

Because of this one standard, God established Jesus Christ as the king of faith. Jesus Christ represented God’s will and conveyed God’s word on His behalf, but the proclaimed word was not the Old Testament word as it was. He did not believe with the Old Testament faith. He did not believe within the limits of what the prophets and sages had spoken and prophesied. In other words, Jesus did not have the messianic idea within the realm of the Old Testament that the people of Israel had believed in.

What kind of faith did Jesus Christ have? He had a faith that was not in the Old Testament, a faith that had not existed in history until then, a new faith that had not appeared until then, a faith that had not appeared in any environment or anywhere in the world. He was the representative of faith. That is why the history of the Old Testament had to run before Jesus Christ.

Then what should we, who believe in Jesus Christ, the king of faith who was established as God’s boast, know? We must know that if we look at Jesus Christ within a certain limit, we cannot know his value that extends to the four-thousand-year history before his coming, his thirty-some years of life, and the eternal future. We must also know that even if billions of people stand in opposition because they do not know God’s will, I will hold on to that one will. I will believe what no one else can believe. We must know the fact that Jesus could stand as the savior of all people, the king of faith, only when the standard of faith was established.

Then did Jesus Christ, whom we believe in today, tell us all the words during his lifetime and leave? If he did not tell us all the words and leave, we need the words that the coming Lord will give us. Jesus was the king of faith who could be boasted of before Satan and all the created world after four thousand years since the fall of Adam and Eve, and the king of faith whom God sought, but because of the disbelief of the Jewish people, he had no choice but to hand him over to the enemy. Therefore, Jesus Christ is to come with a standard that can be boasted of before the created beings on this earth again and give you new words.

Jesus, as the representative of faith, the king of faith, announced new words that were not in the Old Testament. Those words are the words of the New Testament and have been handed down to us today.

Now, what we must possess is that today is a new era, and a glorious era will come in the future, and we must be able to have the faith to remain in that glorious era.

The hope and faith of Jesus Christ were not of the dimension that human beings had believed in for four thousand years. It was a faith that extended through his entire life to the distant future, that is, to eternity, a faith that could reveal a love and goodness that God had not thought of and that had not appeared at that time.

Therefore, Jesus Christ was the king of faith who had never existed in history, and he was the one whom God could boast of. Just like Jesus, you must also have this faith.

Jesus, the King of Victory Who Defeated Satan

Second, the reason God could boast of Jesus Christ was that although many people had fought against Satan for thousands of years, Jesus Christ was finally able to stand as the king of victory. That is why God boasted of Jesus Christ.

For four thousand years, numerous ancestors came to this earth and fought against Satan. Numerous prophets came and fought against Satan for the sake of God’s will to send the Messiah. However, they could not subdue Satan. They fought against Satan for four thousand years, but they could not conquer Satan and could not subdue him, but with the coming of Jesus Christ to this earth, Satan was finally conquered and subdued.

With what did Jesus subdue Satan? He subdued him with the principle of heavenly love. You must know that. What we Christians today must know is the fact that in subduing Satan, there is no other way than the principle of love.

What kind of principle is the principle of love? Jesus Christ died before all people. Also, although numerous people have come and gone on this earth, Jesus Christ is the only begotten Son whom God loved so dearly. That is why, when you look at the life of Jesus Christ for about thirty years, there is no part that is not the life of a filial son. A day’s life before God, whether day or night, was a life that was suitable for God’s heart, a life from which no time could be taken away. It was a life of a filial son to the extent that God would say, “On this earth, there is only you.”

Even if everything in his life were to disappear, Jesus’s heart was solely for God. Even if his own body was disregarded, he only had the heart to fulfill his mission as the savior of all people. Only, Father! I will disappear and become a filial son who can return the price of love as the object of Your love, whom You have been seeking for four thousand years, as the son who receives Your love. He had nothing but this one heart.

Therefore, even if tens of millions of people said that Jesus Christ was not the Son of God, God could not do so. The power of the heavenly principle of the parent-child relationship, which is connected to the center of heaven and earth and is related to God’s love, cannot be blocked by anyone. Jesus did not succumb to the environment in any difficulty. He carried the cross even in the lonely place on Golgotha. Jesus knew that God’s will was in that place, and he knew well the heart of the Father’s love that he had longed for for four thousand years.

Therefore, as long as the Father’s will does not change, the pride of being a son who can receive the Father’s love is eternal. God boasted of Jesus Christ as the only begotten Son, the embodiment of God’s unchanging love, before all created things. He boasted before the satanic world.

In the six-thousand-year history to this day, there are many people who have been filial to the parents who gave birth to them. There are many filial sons and daughters in Satan’s bosom. However, in order for God to be able to boast of Jesus Christ and to receive God’s love like Jesus, there must be a value and achievement that is more than the sum of all the filial sons and daughters in the satanic realm throughout history. Only then can God say, “This is my beloved Son,” and he can become the only filial son in heaven and on earth who represents the heavenly principle.

When Jesus looked at the numerous crowds with this standard, he was dumbfounded. Because of such a heart of Jesus, he felt that there was a difference between heaven and earth between his own value and their value. Therefore, Jesus was able to pray for them before heaven with dignity.

Also, he was able to destroy even Satan with the power that came from the parent-child relationship connected with God through love. What should we think about today? Humanity has been fighting against Satan for six thousand years until now, but you should think about how Jesus Christ was able to achieve a victory that was more valuable than the sum of all the victories of many prophets for four thousand years. Jesus, the prince who took responsibility for the entire will

Jesus' entire life was a life of fulfilling his own responsibility and mission. He completed on earth a responsibility that could remain for eternity. Jesus' life of over 30 years was a life that achieved on this earth an eternally unchanging record, a record of having fulfilled his responsibility. There was not a single person on this earth other than Jesus Christ who came forward to take responsibility for God's will. You must know that Jesus took responsibility all by himself.

While Jesus felt lonely about taking responsibility for the entire will by himself, he felt an even greater responsibility. Therefore, Jesus' daily life was a life of laying the foundation for fulfilling the entire responsibility. And during the 30-year preparation period, the 3-year practical period, and the 3-day completion period, Jesus' eyes were only on subjugating Satan and fulfilling God's will on that foundation. It was a life lived with a keen sense of this responsibility. Jesus never forgot this responsibility for a single moment.

Also, when he went to the top of Golgotha carrying the cross, even at the last moment when all the people slandered him and Satan mocked him, Jesus' heart to bear the responsibility of the heavenly law that he was entrusted with did not change. Because Jesus crossed the pass of the cross with the single-minded determination to fulfill his responsibility, he was able to bring about the history of resurrection. And because he had the responsibility to re-gather the disciples who remained on earth, Jesus was able to go to the kingdom of heaven, come down again, and bring about the history of resurrection by relying on God's power.

Even in death, Jesus was concerned about his scattered disciples, and during the three days in the tomb, he had the heart to protect these disciples forever, so after his resurrection, he went to the shore of the Sea of Galilee to look for his disciples.

Today, when we think about it from a human perspective, it is easy to think, "How could Jesus have done that to those who had no sense of responsibility?" Although they were disciples who rejected him in a difficult situation, Jesus went to Galilee first after his resurrection and began to carry out his responsibility. In this way, the character of Jesus Christ, who established them as unchanging disciples when crossing the pass of death, is the character that we today should emulate.

That's not all. You must know that he was responsible for the disciples of that time, the countless saints after that, and even us today, 2,000 years later. The history of salvation was the history of the whole. Since Heaven's will is to save the whole, Jesus is responsible for all of humanity.

Then what kind of responsibility does Jesus have? Jesus is not responsible for worldly affairs, nor is he responsible for a good life. He is responsible for our lives. Everyone, there are many difficult things in this world, but there is nothing more difficult than this. Because he took responsibility for the matter of life and death….

We who must bear the entire responsibility

Then, what should we do to serve this Jesus, the Jesus we believe in today? We should not always be the ones who place responsibility on Jesus.

And we ourselves should be able to say, "Abba, Father, I understand the difficulties of Jesus Christ who has been responsible for 2,000 years," and we should be able to feel sorry for Jesus who is taking responsibility for us and for the world today.

Whose fault were these things! It is because of us, who are insignificant. Therefore, we should think about this and become people who can bow our heads before Jesus. While calling out, "Lord!" we should feel a heart that feels like our bones are melting, a heart that feels like our flesh is melting.

God was finally able to hold on to Jesus Christ, who was trying to take responsibility for the 4,000-year will, and say, "You alone are taking the responsibility that I must take." Jesus Christ who became God's pride
