Therefore, the time has come for us to pray, "Please give us the responsibility that Jesus Christ pledged to God on the cross to take responsibility for history, for the present, and for the future."

In our lives until this day, there have been many times when we have passed the responsibility on to Heaven. But now, we must be able to pray, "Instead of the anxious heart of God for 4,000 years, I will fight with the responsibility of Jesus Christ, who has been working on earth as the king of responsibility, bearing all historical responsibilities. Even if the enemy Satan and tens of millions of people do not welcome me, I will take responsibility and fight." People who can pray like this must emerge. Only when such people emerge can Jesus rest in the garden of rest.

Today, in the last days, what we hear is the words, "Who is the one who will listen to my appeal for life?" But who is the person who will listen to the appeal for life of Jesus Christ, who inherited God's life? Heaven is looking for such a person.

Until now, Jesus has been praying at the right hand of God for all people. The reason Jesus cannot rest and is still praying is not because Jesus did something wrong. Nor is it because Jesus is in a position where he cannot stand before the Father. All of this is because of us.

41

Therefore, for the sake of Jesus who has been toiling for 2,000 years, you must try to fulfill the responsibility of life, even if it means cutting off your own life.

The responsibility of life remains on this earth because Jesus died on the cross. The time to fulfill this remaining responsibility of life is the time of the Second Advent. The time of the Second Advent begins with the appearance of a person who takes on this responsibility of life. He is a person who takes on the historical responsibility of life and the future responsibility of life, so you must fight with him in the final battle.

The beginning of the Second Advent

God established His beloved Jesus, and through the Jesus of faith, or through the Jesus of truth, He wants to love human beings. He wants to love you.

Today, when we are told to emulate the Jesus of faith, even in our hearts, we should be able to say, "Yes, that is so." When we are told to emulate the victorious Jesus, we should be able to say, "That is so," and when we are told to emulate the Jesus who is taking responsibility, we should be able to say, "Yes, that is so." If you cannot become such a person, how can Jesus Christ, who has not rested for a single moment, for a single hour, until now, rest?

Therefore, you must take on these conditions that God established as His pride. And you must become people who fulfill on this earth the conditions of pride of Jesus who went to the spirit world. So you must become people whom God can be proud of.

First, you must be proud of believing in a world that does not believe. And you must be proud of having won the fight against Satan. In this world where people cannot take responsibility, you must be proud of taking responsibility.

Through this, God's pride must reach us on earth through Jesus Christ in the spirit world, and through us on earth, that pride must also reach all things. Only then will God's ideal of creation, the will to set up human beings as the lords of all things and be proud of them before all things, be fulfilled.

42

Jesus Christ who became God's pride

Only then can human beings and all things offer thanks and worship to the God who is proud. We have this entire responsibility.

Today, we are so pathetic. The faith we have is also insignificant. Therefore, when human beings have to fight Satan in the future, we must pray, "Abba, Father, please give strength to all the people of this world so that they can fight and win against Satan. Please let all of humanity be able to bear its responsibility." And we must be able to fight the enemy of the whole alone, win, and say, "Father, be joyful."

By showing God the appearance of taking on all the responsibilities of the world, and through a person who can be proud of the center of taking responsibility before hundreds of millions of people, or tens of thousands of saints and the created world, God's resentment toward the earth can be resolved, and through such a person, God's will can be unfolded. You must know this for sure. Let us pray.

<Prayer> Father! I know that the life of Jesus Christ was one where tears did not cease when he saw the evil of the world, saying, "This way is my responsibility, and that way is my responsibility."

Today, we have no feeling even when we see evil, and we are unrighteous and inadequate, and we do not feel the responsibility with a painful heart for the will of heaven. I was the one who did not have a heart to defeat the enemy and a sorrow that was filled with resentment, and I was the one who did not have a record of fighting, and I was the one who did not believe in the almighty God. I did not know the loyalty of Jesus Christ to heaven.

Father, this evening I have admonished a small group. I have learned that Your will to establish Jesus Christ and be proud of him was connected to us today through the apostles and through history, and that You hope that will bear fruit in us, and I have learned that the central responsibility that tens of thousands of saints can welcome, in addition to the joy of having obtained life, has been entrusted to us today.

Now, please allow us to become a sacrifice to resolve the resentment of heaven and earth, all things, and Jesus Christ, and please allow us to become filial children who do our best with all our heart and soul.

43

Please allow it, Father, I earnestly hope and pray.
You established the ideal of the bridegroom and bride through the way of the cross, and now the problem we face is to what extent we can practice the love of Christ, to what extent we have fulfilled our responsibility centered on the love of Christ, and to what extent we can find the value of faith through the love of Christ.
As the Father has admonished us at this hour, please allow us to know that we ourselves today have been entrusted with the responsibility for resolving Heaven's sorrow, and that the situation is such that the battle to resolve Heaven's grief must be concluded through us. Having understood this, please allow us to have only the heart to practice it more than anyone else and the heart to be grateful to you, Father.
Allow us to be grateful even while carrying the cross, and please do not let us become cowardly before you, Father, even if we fight against tens of thousands of millions of satans. Even if we stand in a difficult position carrying the cross, Father! Please guide us to become children who can say, “Do not worry, for I am here.” Please allow us to become children who can comfort the Father, who is sorrowful as He looks upon His children who are in difficult positions. I earnestly hope and pray for this.
Please work so that the Word may become their life and their path, and please allow them to find a central point and standard to live by appealing to the center of their lives, and lead them so that they can go before the Father with a center of unchanging faith and life. I earnestly ask and desire that you allow the history of the creation of the Word to be so. I have prayed all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen. *

Thus, Jesus Is Seeking Us

Matthew 18:1-14
The content I would like to speak on at this hour is “Thus, Jesus Is Seeking Us.” I will speak under this title.
Jesus Christ is the one who came to the earth as the one person whom God prepared through 4,000 years of toil. This Jesus Christ came to save the countless multitudes of humanity left on earth, representing God's will and God's anxious heart.
Fallen People Are Like a Single Lost Sheep
Since the fall, where has our human race stood before God? We are in the position of a single lost sheep that has strayed, not among the ninety-nine sheep.
Even the myriads of angels and archangels in heaven are unable to offer joyful praise to God because of the loss of Adam and Eve, who were like one sheep. God has been repeating His toil until now to find again the humanity that has prevented the angels and archangels from offering joyful praise.
Jesus Christ was sent to the earth as the one being whom God had sought for 4,000 years. As the ancestor of goodness before all people, that Jesus is repeating a history of toil, standing in the position of True Parents to bring about the rebirth of us human beings who have entered into death.
May 20, 1956 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church.

Today, we simply know Jesus Christ as the one established as God's only begotten Son in the course of God's 4,000-year providential history, and as the central being who was victorious over Satan by carrying the cross to save humanity, which had fallen into sin.
Then what did God do to establish Jesus Christ as the one center? He entrusted to Jesus all the things He had been providing for the world's people. Thus, Jesus Christ was established as a new center and came to stand in the position of having to take responsibility for and save all people. When Jesus stood in this position, his mind and body must have been submerged in unspeakable sorrow.
Jesus Christ Who Came to Find Us
Then, through what course does Jesus Christ find us today? Through 4,000 years of history, God established the Word for human salvation, and through many prophets and sages, He announced to the multitudes that the Messiah would come.
Therefore, the believers of Judaism had been preparing to receive the Messiah through the words of testimony that many prophets had proclaimed. That is the history of the Old Testament. Jesus Christ, who came upon this prepared foundation, had to conclude the 4,000-year history of the Old Testament as a history of goodness before God. Therefore, the new words he spoke were words imbued with the sorrow intertwined in God's 4,000-year providential course of restoration, and at the same time, they were words that clarified the heavenly law that the multitudes of creation must possess as they walk the path of faith.
However, what must have been the heart of Jesus as he looked upon the crowd that could not believe, even though the many believers of Judaism should have listened carefully to and believed this new word that Jesus announced? You must know that Jesus appealed with a sorrowful heart.
Until today, Heaven has been toiling for a long time to find me, one person, and to find and re-establish our human race, which has fallen into sin.

Thus, Jesus Is Seeking Us

In the Old Testament Age, He gave the words of the Old Testament law to the Israelite people through the prophets. And to resolve the sorrowful 4,000-year history, He sent Jesus Christ and announced the new words of truth. However, because the Jewish people did not believe those words, they could not comfort God's sorrowful heart, and you must know that the result was that they instead intensified Heaven's sorrowful heart from within their own hearts.
Therefore, Jesus appeared before the crowd that did not know which way to go and was in the hands of Satan, and he presented the direction to go and taught them the way to live. However, the people of Israel did not listen to those words. Thus, our human race lost its direction in life, and the altar of 4,000 years of toil that God had established also collapsed. If the people of Israel had become one on the foundation of God's Word, they would have borne fruit by the Word God gave, and God would have embraced them again as His children.
The Jewish People Who Did Not Believe the Word Jesus Gave
Because the people of Israel, who were originally supposed to be the model, did not believe the new word that Jesus gave and could not become one, Jesus Christ left behind words of sorrow and departed. Therefore, what position did the people of Israel, who should have stood in the position of a hundred sheep, come to stand in? They were placed in the position of a single lost sheep, and we are also in the same situation.
We must know the heart of Jesus who dealt with the people of Israel, who were in the position of one lost sheep. To find and re-establish the lost people of Israel, Jesus cried out with a sad heart.
What we must know today is the fact that Heaven has been carrying on the providence for 4,000 years with a sorrowful heart to find me, one person, and that after that, Jesus Christ inherited God's sorrowful heart and is following behind us, calling out to us.

Then what course did Jesus go through during his thirty-some years of life? Jesus prepared for the 30 years of his private life, hoping for God's will to appear. After that period, when he appeared with a new word and began to preach, Jesus did not preach the word with a feeling of joy, but with Heaven's sorrow in his heart.
He spoke many words, such as, “Follow me,” and “Believe in me,” but the crowd that listened carefully to the voice appealing from that sad heart and followed him was extremely small.
In such an environment, Jesus spent his 30 years of life with a sorrowful heart, and you must know the fact that the earnest voice that Jesus cried out while he was alive is still appealing to you through the words of the Bible, and that even at this hour today, Jesus is pleading for you from the spirit world.
Therefore, you must now find the direction you must go by knowing what the content of the words that Jesus appealed with was.
If you yourselves are in the position of a lost sheep before Heaven, and yet you do not know the direction you should go, nor do you know what position you are in, and you think that the world will just continue as it is, you are greatly mistaken.
You yourselves may not know it well, but Jesus has been calling with a sad voice throughout the 2,000-year historical course from his birth until now, and that calling voice is becoming your hope.
God's Heart and Jesus' Voice
Will you turn away from this voice that calls so earnestly? If there is anyone who cannot hear, they should at least have the same heart of resentment. Is there anyone among you whose ears do not know how to long for the calling voice? You must strive to discern this voice. Or, even if you have heard the calling voice, when your body is not strong enough to move, you must become a self that can gather your heart toward that place.

Thus, Jesus Is Seeking Us

God's steps in seeking to find me today, an individual in the position of a lost sheep, were not for a day, not for a year, not for a hundred years; He came seeking for 6,000 years.
The 6,000-year history of striving to find the lost flock of sheep on heaven and earth was Heaven's history of great redemption.
Because we human beings could not hear God's calling voice, the words proclaimed by showing them through Jesus Christ, who was the God of substance, and by having Jesus, who was the substance, reveal God's formless heart, were the words of the gospel.
Because human beings do not know the heart of God who exists without form and cannot hear God's voice, Jesus appeared as the substance of God to resolve this. And when they heard the words and voice he preached, the people of Israel were in a position where they should have come to Jesus, known the true will of God that they had not known for 4,000 years, felt God's heart, and repented. Nevertheless, the people of Israel did not repent and instead distanced themselves from Jesus.
Therefore, you must now prepare to understand the sad voice of Jesus that you hear. To do so, what must you do? Just as you listen well to all worldly words, you must have a heart that can say, “I believe in Jesus, who appeared before all people on behalf of God's heart and on behalf of God's will.”
Jesus came on behalf of the formless God and walked the course of atonement on behalf of the ignorant human beings who had only brought sorrow to Heaven for 4,000 years. You must be able to fathom the heart of God who made Jesus re-determine himself by placing him in such a sad position.
If the people of Israel had broadened their hearts and known how to discern the voice that cried out on behalf of God's anxious internal heart, they would have understood without problem the words that the Jesus Christ who appeared in substance cried out, pierced with sorrow. But what were the people of Israel like? They tried to be satisfied with only the words that appeared in the Old Testament. They thought that all of God's final words were recorded in the Old Testament.

God's sorrow is not only this. The people of Israel did not realize that when God established Jesus Christ and showed and testified to God's internal heart in substance, if they did not attend him, Heaven's sorrow would be connected to the sorrow on earth.
Jesus Christ was supposed to resolve with joy on the earth the sorrow of the 4,000 years of toil of the formless God, but because of the people of Israel who did not know such a Jesus, you must know that God's sorrow was not resolved through Jesus Christ and remained as sorrow once again.
Jesus Christ, who came to the earth on behalf of God's will and on behalf of the 4,000-year history, went without being able to announce the words of joy. Therefore, although the 2,000-year history since Jesus has passed, when we look at it through the 6,000-year history today, the sorrow of God and the sorrow of Jesus Christ are still piercing the earth.
Today, we must know this sorrow of God and the sorrow of Jesus Christ, and now we must be able to fathom the words of God's joy and the words of Jesus Christ.
The purpose for which Jesus sought us was not always to convey only words of sorrow. In the process of toiling to find us, who are like a lost flock of sheep, he should not always speak only words of grief. Since he has spoken words of grief for 6,000 years, at the moment the lost flock of sheep is found, the 6,000 years of sorrow must be completely
The word of joy that can be forgotten must appear.
You think that the word of joy will appear from heaven, but that is a big misunderstanding.
Now, before the heart of Jesus Christ who has toiled for 2,000 years, we must become a flock that can run to the Lord who is coming to find us.
We must not be those who, even after hearing the cry of the sorrowful Jesus Christ, the wounded Jesus Christ, linger and fail to set a direction and run. When Jesus Christ suddenly comes and calls you with a voice of sorrow, you must not cower in that place.


This is how Jesus finds us

Then what should we do? Before the voice of Jesus Christ's sorrow is heard, you must first cry out with a voice of sorrow.
I must first cry out, 'My shepherd! Lord!' so that my voice fills the heavens and the earth.
Then Jesus, who is coming to find you, will listen to your cry and when he cries out again, he will not cry out with a sad voice but with a joyful voice. You must stand in such a position.
We who must testify to the sorrowful heart of Jesus
Today, we must testify to the sorrowful heart of Jesus Christ.
We should not just be sad about losing our shepherd, but we should know how to cry out to find the lost shepherd.
Only when we become beings who can take responsibility for the toiling steps left by Jesus who cried out like this, will we be able to offer satisfaction to this Jesus. You must know the fact that today Jesus is looking for us with a voice of sorrow, and is repeating a life of suffering to find us.
Jesus, who represented the 4,000-year history to save humanity, could not live a comfortable life due to the providence of salvation for all humanity. He is coming to us today through a life of suffering.
As you know, Jesus' 30-odd years of life were a life of suffering. His life during the 30-year preparation period as the son of Joseph the carpenter was a life of suffering both externally and internally.
He could not live as freely as you in a comfortable place. It is a great misunderstanding to think that he lived as befitting the savior of all people. In a position where he was criticized even by his stepfather Joseph, Mary, and his younger siblings, Jesus spent a life of suffering, unable to say all that he had to say.
Jesus' suffering was not for himself. Knowing that if it were not for him, there would be no one to find the lost family again on behalf of the heart of God who had toiled for 4,000 years, he was earnest with his heart toward heaven day and night.


And seeing the multitudes struggling in a miserable environment centered on their surroundings and themselves, Jesus entered a life course of difficulty and sorrow and fought by dedicating his life to realize the ideal world on behalf of the living word of God for 4,000 years.
Jesus, who was not treated properly from birth, lived a lonely and difficult life like a life in the wilderness until he died. This external suffering of Jesus was also suffering, but the hidden suffering in his internal heart that was not revealed externally is known only to God.
The people of Israel, who should have believed in and followed Jesus, did not recognize the person they should have known, but recognized the person they did not need to know. Among such people of Israel, Jesus longed for life in his hometown.
The life he ate, wore, and drank was not a life for himself, nor a life for his own comfort. All his eating, wearing, and drinking were for God, for the world's humanity, and for the nation, beyond Jesus himself, and his footsteps were also such footsteps.
However, there was not a single person who understood the circumstances of such a messiah.
There was no one who, embracing the lonely heart of Jesus Christ, would say, 'I know your heart, I know your heart, I will follow you wherever you go and be a friend to comfort your heart.' Even his disciples, who should have comforted him, could not comfort Jesus' hidden inner heart.
Therefore, the 30-odd years of Jesus Christ's life were marked by a life of suffering. From the day his three-year public ministry of preaching the gospel began, the words he preached were not private words. They were not words for his own benefit, nor were they words to establish any of his own power. They were words to fulfill God's will.
However, there was no one who, on behalf of the entire nation, recognized and wanted to be a friend to Jesus who came with such words and will. Therefore, Jesus was an object of contempt in the village and an object of contempt for the entire nation.
Today, you are in an environment where you can hear God's word in a comfortable place.


This is how Jesus finds us

You must not miss this time when you can face God in such a free environment.
The suffering Jesus
In Jesus' time, he had to preach the word secretly, and he had to listen to the word in hiding. That is why the place they went was the wilderness. Even in such circumstances, Jesus tried to lead a large crowd into the wilderness and preach the word of God. You must know the heart of Jesus Christ who tried to fulfill God's will by preaching the word of God even in that way.
In this way, Jesus preached the gospel to the multitudes in the course of his life, but there was not a single person who welcomed it. No matter how earnest his heart was in preaching the gospel, there were many who did not know. The more Jesus worked to fulfill the mission and responsibility he was given, the more people acted destructively towards it.
Looking at this, the pitiful Jesus Christ, who had been crying out in the wilderness to the multitudes all day long, went into the rugged path of the Mount of Olives to appeal to heaven again. You must think of the toil of Jesus who, with his disciples scattered, went before God alone to heal his wounded heart and to replenish his strength to fight Satan for the second time.
You must know that Jesus Christ lived a life of suffering among sufferings by burning his 30-odd years of life. Not only that. It is a great misunderstanding to think that Jesus' suffering ended with the suffering of his 30-odd years of life. Even today, in the spirit world of that country, Jesus Christ is in suffering.
Jesus Christ, who is acting on behalf of the will of the providence with the one purpose of fulfilling God's will as the 2,000-year history is extended, is living a life of suffering even at this hour today. That life of suffering is connected and continues to this day.


Then where will this one suffering be resolved? It is not all things on this earth today. It is absolutely not all things on this earth. The resentment that has been formed in that suffering and toil must be resolved through you who can take responsibility for today.
Therefore, Jesus revealed the suffering in the course of the providence of eternal life before you, regardless of the historical distance. If you know this fact, you yourselves must know how to hold the suffering hand of Jesus and comfort him. Thus, the responsibility to comfort by taking on the deep-seated resentment of Jesus Christ, who was hated and cursed, is on you today.
But if you have not been able to stand in such a position, what should you do? You must know how to feel the suffering of Jesus in your environment. You must become a person who knows how to analyze the life of suffering of Jesus Christ in your life.
Then what sin did Jesus have that he had to live a life of hardship and suffering for 30-odd years? If there was a sin, it is only the sin of being established as a savior who must save all people before God. You must know the story of this Jesus who suffered for all people and cried out earnestly for all people. We must have a heart of repentance for such a Jesus today.
In your life, too, there are traces of the suffering of Jesus Christ's 30-odd years of life. If you are to gather this, you must gather everything from the suffering at birth in a manger to the suffering on Golgotha, and even the traces of suffering for 2,000 years after the resurrection. You must know this overall will.
Jesus' sorrow did not end with his earnest cry. It did not end even after going through a life of hardship and toil. Today, people think that Jesus' sorrow ended with his death on the cross after a life of hardship, but because of that, the will was extended and Jesus' sorrow remained as a resentment that could not be resolved. Knowing this fact, you must save Jesus from sorrow at the risk of your life.


This is how Jesus finds us

In this way, Jesus Christ has toiled and walked a path full of resentment until today, after 6,000 years of history, to find us, and he has laid down his life and walked the path of the cross, so you must hold on to such a Jesus.
When Jesus was about to die on the path of death on the cross that concluded his 30-odd years of life, he cried out earnestly, 'Abba, Father...'

The bloody appeal of the numerous prophets and sages who had toiled for 4,000 years should have been resolved by the people of Israel, but since the people of Israel could not resolve it, how could they repay the bloody appeal of their ancestors? There was no way to repay it.
However, it was Jesus Christ who paid the price of the historical bloody appeal on behalf of the nation and made indemnity. When Abel's blood cried out, the condition that the numerous prophets and sages who shed their precious blood appealed to the torn and blood-stained land and to the people of Israel was resolved by Jesus. The sound of crying that had been appealing for 4,000 years, the purpose of the bloody appeal of numerous prophets and sages for 4,000 years, was fulfilled through the death of Jesus himself, and also through his resurrection after death.
Because of the resurrection of Jesus Christ, the resentment of the ancestors who shed their blood on this earth was gathered, and their will to resent the earth and demand the resolution of their resentment was fulfilled. Thus, only then could they worship before heaven with Jesus at the forefront.
We who must resolve the resentment of Jesus
What did Jesus, who completed the bloody appeal of the prophets and sages who were sacrificed because the people of Israel did not believe in and serve heaven, leave to posterity at the same time? Jesus left the blood of the death on the cross to posterity. That is why the blood of the death of Jesus Christ remains in your hearts today. Therefore, when you stand before Jesus, and when you look at your life, you will feel that there was a hill of blood in your life as well. You must know that this is a reward for the bloody appeal of the prophets and sages and at the same time a reward for the bloody appeal of Jesus Christ. That is why when Jesus, who came to us through the path of the cross, tells us to come, we must also go to Jesus through the path of the cross.
Now you must experience that the passion with which Jesus Christ appealed with his blood on the cross on the hill of Golgotha is beating in your pulse.
Even though Jesus Christ found you by hanging the cross, you have not known the toil of Jesus Christ who came to you in that way until now, and you have not called on Jesus by hanging the cross. Jesus Christ, who walked the path of death, Jesus Christ, who came to me carrying the cross, is still crying out for me, appealing infinitely for me, suffering, walking the path of death, and toiling for me.
Now we are facing Jesus with the cross in between, but who will resolve the resentment of this cross? We must resolve it today. Before resolving this, we cannot hold on to Jesus Christ and call him my bridegroom.
That is why when Mary Magdalene said, 'Oh, Lord!' right after the resurrection, Jesus stopped her. And that is why Mary Magdalene wanted to live a life in heaven from the day she met the resurrected Lord, but the life in heaven was blocked for 2,000 years. Knowing this remaining resentment of the cross, we who believe must now resolve this remaining resentment of the cross.
I will.
What did Jesus Christ, who crossed the hill of the cross over and over to find us, leave behind?
Jesus left the nouns bridegroom and bride on this earth. So now, in your prayers, the Lord will appear as the bridegroom. You are the bride and the Lord is the bridegroom; in that form He will appear to you. When you see the Lord appearing as the bridegroom, you must always think of the price of the blood of the cross.
Now, what is left? What is it that the Lord must find for us again? It is the way to abolish the cross and bless all generations.

<01456>

Thus Jesus finds us

He must find a way to get beyond the cross. If Jesus cannot freely hold onto us after crossing the hill of the cross, He must resolve this one resentment of taking down the cross. The history of the Second Advent will not be completed until a single, unchanging standard is established through my own body, through the altar, and through heaven and earth, by which the cross can be abolished.
The light, water, and oil that Jesus left behind
What did Jesus, who found us in this way, leave for us today?
What did He leave for us after finding me through a sad life, through a life of suffering, through death on the cross? Jesus left us the light of life. Jesus came to us at the risk of his life, and what gift did he bring? He brought the light that can brighten the dark world. That is why when we shed tears of gratitude for the death of Jesus Christ, we come to know the heart of Jesus Christ and the circumstances of Jesus Christ.
And what else did Jesus Christ leave for us? He left us water and oil. What did Jesus leave for us to heal us who have been afflicted as much as we have been and wounded as much as we have been? He left us water and oil.
Therefore, we must shine the light that Jesus left us to find our wounds and wash them with water and oil, and knowing that we are sinners and naked, we must put on the wedding garment. The time has come for this. In this way, after you have lit the lamp in your heart and mind, washed your sins clean, healed your wounds, and put on the wedding garment, you can fulfill the desire of Jesus who died 2,000 years ago today.
Now, after lighting the lamp of our hearts, washing our bodies clean with water, anointing our wounds with oil, and putting on the wedding garment He has permitted, we must cross the cross ourselves, without needing Jesus to cross it for us, and offer our worship to Jesus.

<01457>

This is what human beings must do on earth.
Do not hope for Jesus to cross the cross, but you must try to cross it. It is not that Jesus will cross over, but you must become beings who emit the light of life, and then, with all your strength, put on the wedding garment that can replace the light of eternal, unchanging value, cross the cross, and hold onto Jesus, saying, "Lord, may you rest in peace forever." You must become loving brides who can offer worship. God is hoping for such brides to emerge.
You must now untie the burden that Jesus left behind. Inherit the light of the heart from Jesus, receive the gift of water and oil from Jesus, and then put on the wedding garment... This wedding garment is not a garment that will remain with you as an individual. It is not to be fixed on you, but through you, many people must receive the light of life, receive the gift of water and oil, and by putting on the wedding garment, become brides before the Lord.
<Prayer> Father of love! As we feel how harsh the 6,000-year history has been, please allow us to become those who feel fear before that penetrating heart and that penetrating mind. We did not know what sin was the greatest among sins, but now we know that it is a great sin to consider the light given by the Lord as my own, it is a great sin to have water and oil and keep them only for myself, it is a great sin for me to be wearing the wedding garment and not have many people wear the wedding garment, and we have learned that this is a great sin representing 6,000 years, not to have made them believe when we had the responsibility to do so.
Today, the children of Yours who have gathered in this place, please allow them to realize that it is a greater sin to cause one life to sin than to sin themselves, and that it is a greater sin not to leave behind the light, water, oil, and wedding garment left by the labor of Jesus Christ.
Father, now through the words that have been conveyed, let the scattered children receive the image of Jesus Christ and hear the voice of the calling. We must take responsibility for the historical labor and suffering, even the suffering of the cross, but since they are in a position of insufficiency, do not know the will of heaven, and are in a position of not knowing the will that the Father desires, Father, please encourage them and first reveal the will to them, and allow them to hear the direct voice of the Father. As they desire to live a life of goodness, I earnestly hope and desire, loving Father, that you will guide them so that they can live as they have embraced.
I earnestly hope and desire, loving Father, that you will guide them to become children who can cross over all things and reveal the glory of heaven by adorning themselves as the bride of the Lord, and that you will have them take charge of a new historical work.
I entrust everything to you, so please take charge according to your will, appear upon the hearts of those who have gathered, and I earnestly hope that you will establish them as children who can represent the eternal glory of victory, and I have spoken in the name of the Lord. Amen. *

Jesus who comes and goes for the sake of heaven and earth,
and who will come and go

John 14:2-12
<Prayer (I)> The young children have come before the Father's knees again to find the way to live, so Father, please receive them. Jesus, Who Came and Is to Come for the Sake of Heaven and Earth

Please allow it, beloved Father, we earnestly hope and desire.
Please remove humanistic perceptions and humanistic concepts from the environment around us, and we pray in the name of the beloved Lord, earnestly hoping and desiring that You will allow the heart of the one who speaks and the heart of the one who receives to unite as one and become a joy and glory to the Father. <Sermon> The words I want to give today are, “Jesus, Who Came and Is to Come for the Sake of Heaven and Earth.” I will speak for a short time under this title.
The Position of Adam and Eve in the Cosmos
It is an undeniable fact that God created all things in the heavens and the earth so that God could receive glory. That is why He first created the formless world of angels, and next, He created the formless substantial world as a representation of the formless substantial world. And He created Adam and Eve as the center and representatives of the spirit world and the substantial world.
As long as the heavens and the earth do not change, this Adam and Eve had to share the same destiny as the heavens and the earth. In other words, they were Adam and Eve who had the destiny to move as the heavens and the earth moved. Therefore, if Adam and Eve change, the heavens and the earth also change, and if the center of Adam and Eve is scattered, the center of the entire heavens and the earth is also scattered. And they were Adam and Eve who were created with the inevitable condition that if the center of the entire cosmos is scattered, the center of the Creator is also scattered.
Because this Adam and Eve fell, the center of the cosmos went astray, and because the center of the cosmos went astray, the center of the Creator also went astray. Therefore, God is in the position of having to re-establish the center of heaven and earth, have the created world harmonize with that correct center, and make the center of the Creator and the center of the created beings not two, but one. If that happens, then again, if heaven is happy, the earth will also be happy, and if the earth is happy, heaven will also be happy. As heaven is eternal, the earth will also be eternal, and if heaven is immersed in joy of an infinite realm, the earth will also be immersed in joy of an infinite realm.

As long as the Creator's destiny does not go wrong, the destiny of the created world cannot change. Because Adam and Eve, the center of this created world, fell, all things were scattered, and the direction and center of all things went astray. The history to restore this again is the history of the providence of restoration, and through repeated history of the providence of restoration, the long 6,000 years have passed to this day.
Until this hour, God's providence of love was revealed through countless prophets and saints, and while symbolically revealing love through the prophets and saints, He showed the substantial providential love internally and externally through Jesus Christ, who appeared as the crystal of that entire love.
Therefore, his heart represented the center of the formless world, and his body represented the center of the formless substantial world. You must know the fact that because the people of Israel, who should have known that he was this kind of Jesus, did not know, they handed Jesus Christ over to the cross. Thus, the entire heaven and earth were plunged into darkness.
The Purpose of Jesus' Words and Practical Life
The one and only purpose for which Jesus Christ came was to establish an eternal, unchanging center in heaven and earth, equipped with the heart of the Father who created the heavens and the earth. Jesus Christ came to this earth to establish this kind of center.
Therefore, what he said was not to establish some center of his own. It was not to establish a partial center of some village in Jerusalem or a town in Israel, but to establish one center that could connect to the center of the entire spirit world, to the center of the Creator.
His actions were also not the actions of an individual, his hope was not the hope of an individual, and his fight was not a fight that ended with an individual. You must know that the goal he hoped for was to stand as an unchanging center that could embrace all things in the heavens and the earth, and to go beyond all things, through the formless world, to the position of representing the heart of God, the Creator.

Jesus, Who Came and Is to Come for the Sake of Heaven and Earth

You must know the words of Jesus Christ, the life of Jesus Christ, and the practical actions of Jesus Christ who had such a hope. His actions were actions as a new start to build heaven and earth anew, and the words he spoke were words that brought about the history of re-creation to accomplish that one Will.
After a 30-year preparation period, in his 3-year practical life course, he spoke to re-establish the unchanging center of heaven and earth that was lost at the time of Adam and Eve, but because the people of Israel did not believe the words he spoke, Jesus Christ, who should have been established as the center of the spirit world and the physical world, was only established as the center of the spirit world, and you must know that he went without being established as the center of the substantial physical world.
For what did Jesus Christ live until he crossed the hill of the cross? For what did he toil for some 30 years of his life after coming to this earth? Primarily, he toiled for the earth.
However, due to his merit of toiling for the earth, the purpose he intended to reap on the earth was to be fulfilled, and one center that should be achieved on the earth by uniting spirit and flesh was to be completed in one substance, but because the spirit and the flesh were divided, the body of Jesus Christ, the center of the substance to be achieved on the earth, was harmed. Thus, by representing the spiritual world, only the spirit of Jesus was perfected, and you must know that the 2,000-year history since the resurrection until today has been a period of carrying out the providence of restoration centered on the spirit world.
Jesus was resurrected after he died on the cross, and after being active on the earth for 40 days after his resurrection, he went to the spirit world again. In this way, the fact that Jesus died, was resurrected, and then ascended again symbolically shows the history of God's creation.
In the book of Genesis, there is the verse, “And there was evening and there was morning, the first day” (Gen. 1:5). Then there is the night time. The three-day period of Jesus in the tomb is a period like the night time. The 30-odd years of his life were the daytime, and Jesus toiled for 30-odd years to raise his disciples. After going through this course of toil, his resurrection is like passing through the night and greeting a new morning.
The resurrected Jesus toiled to set up a lamp on the earth, but he could not set up a lamp on the earth. However, it seems that he was resurrected to set up a lamp on the earth, but in reality, because he was resurrected as the center of the spirit world, Jesus Christ could not remain on the earth and went to the spirit world again. What does this mean? It means that Jesus Christ, who had passed through the night period and greeted the day period, again met the evening and went to the eternal world.
Jesus, Who Had to Say “I Know” to People Who Said “I Don’t Know”
Then what is left now? What is left is the night period. What should have become an eternal morning with the coming of Christ has again become a period like the evening due to the death of Jesus Christ, so the responsibility to take charge of this night period remains. Because we handed over Jesus Christ, we must bear that responsibility.
Just as Jesus Christ established the standard of victory by defeating Satan on the cross by completing the responsibility of this night period, today, the countless Christians remaining on this earth are in the destiny of having to cross the hill of the battle of the night period.
The era when you cross the hill of this night period, are resurrected in the likeness of Jesus, and enjoy the glory of the new morning with him is the era of the Second Advent of hope.
Jesus Christ came to this earth and lived for some 30 years for this earth. Because Jesus came for the earth, for this humanity of the earth, even if the people on the earth oppose him, even if the people on the earth say, “I don’t know,” Jesus had to stand in the position of saying, “I know.”
When Jesus went through the Garden of Gethsemane to the hill of Calvary, even the disciples who were following him abandoned Jesus. When Jesus was hung on the cross, there was no one who said they knew Jesus. Not a single disciple said, “I know Jesus.” In this way, although there was not a single person who said, “I know,” because Jesus came for the earth, he established the position of saying, “I know,” to the people on the earth who said, “I don’t know.” This is what he did when he was resurrected and went to the shore of the Sea of Galilee to find his disciples. In this way, Jesus left one way for the people on the earth to know, and after 40 days, he ascended again.
Now, even when we are in the position of saying, “We don’t know,” because Jesus Christ was in the position of saying, “I know you,” even if we live on an earth that does not recognize Jesus, we must stand in the position of saying, “I know Jesus.”
Therefore, for 2,000 years since Jesus came and went, human beings have been playing the game of seeking Jesus with their hearts. Just as Jesus sought out the apostles on the shore of the Sea of Galilee, in order to repay the grace of the Jesus who sought them out, believers for 2,000 years have been seeking toward the heaven where Jesus went.
It should not have been so. This kind of life has continued for 2,000 years until today.
Then for what purpose did Jesus go to the kingdom of heaven? Since what Jesus, who came for the sake of the earth, had to accomplish was the will of Heaven, he went to the spirit world and has been working for the will of Heaven until now.
Jesus, who came for the sake of the earth, established the standard of “I know” on the earth, but if he did not go to the spirit world, that is, the invisible world, and establish the standard of “I know,” human beings would not be able to remain in the world of “I know.” Therefore, for 2,000 years until today, he has been praying before God in the spirit world to establish the standard of “I know” from a position that you do not know.
Then, it is said that Jesus prays for human beings at the right hand of God, but what kind of prayer is he praying? He is praying a prayer of blood and sweat. If human beings on earth say they know Jesus, then Jesus goes to the spirit world and says that he knows them.
In this way, if Jesus does not create a position where he can say that he knows them before God, the spirit world where human beings can go will not be recognized before the Father. Therefore, Jesus has gone to the spirit world until today and is praying a prayer of toil before God, saying, “I know them.” You must know this well.

69

After this work, how will Jesus come when he comes again? When he comes, he will come with the work of the earth and the work of heaven combined. He will come taking responsibility for the work of the earth and the work of heaven. Therefore, we today must also follow and cross the hill that Jesus crossed until Jesus Christ, who was resurrected from the death of the cross, ascended to heaven and is in the heavenly world, comes again.
Also, at this time, which corresponds to the morning of resurrection after the 2,000-year period of night, when the Jesus who went away establishes a center of welcome in heaven and comes again, you must feel and know with your heart that Jesus is coming toward the earth.
Until now, the form of faith of us believers has been to long for Jesus while looking at heaven. This has been the motto and standard of our faith until today.
Today, when we must long for the Holy Spirit
Now, there is one thing left for us to long for, and what is that? We must long for the Holy Spirit, who is working on behalf of the earth. You must know this. Until now, countless people have longed for Jesus spiritually for 2,000 years, but today we must also long for the Holy Spirit. You must think that we are the saints and humanity who must do so. In this way, the time has come to long for the Holy Spirit, and the time has come to complete the body of the bride.
Since the Holy Spirit is the spirit of the bride, we must know how to long for her, taking on the appearance of the bride and forming the body of the bride. When this happens, Jesus Christ can go to the spirit world and rest. And after establishing a center in heaven and earth, we will find our way back, centering on this earth.
We who longed for the spirit world with our hearts must now long for the Holy Spirit who works in us. Therefore, we long for Jesus, the spiritual symbol, and the Holy Spirit, the physical symbol, and in our one individual,

Jesus who came and went, and will come and go, for the sake of heaven and earth

by the mind that longs for Jesus and the body that longs for the physical Holy Spirit becoming one, the center of heaven and the center of the earth can finally be united in my one mind and body. By doing so, Jesus can stand on my behalf, and the Holy Spirit can stand on my behalf, and I, in the midst of them, can appear representing all people on behalf of the will of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. You must know this.
Then, with what kind of will will the Lord who must come to this earth now come? You must establish the center of Jesus and the Holy Spirit in yourselves. You who have living physical bodies must be completed as a central substantial being that unites the spiritual and the physical, following the example of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, who symbolize the spirit world and the physical world. Otherwise, God’s entire ideal of creation will not be completed in you alone. The mission of this one center is the mission of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Jesus Christ is returning to establish this one center.
What the saints of the Second Advent era must do
Then, what must we do today to uphold this one will? We should not just think about Jesus Christ going to the shores of the Sea of Galilee to find his beloved disciples. Jesus Christ does not always come to find you. You yourselves must become a bride and attend Jesus Christ.
Since Jesus and the Holy Spirit are the center of heaven, you must establish this one standard of being able to face them as one by becoming the center of the earth by having a center where your mind and body can become one. This is not a time to always just long for Jesus. Now, we must have the body of the Holy Spirit and be able to find and attend Jesus on earth on his behalf. You must find and establish this one center.
Jesus Christ, who desires this one center, has established the Holy Spirit for you and has toiled for 2,000 years until today. Now you must

repay this toil. Although Heaven sent Jesus Christ to this earth as the center representing spirit and flesh and established the standard of being completed only spiritually, you yourselves must find and attend Jesus Christ and complete this remaining incomplete part of the flesh. Today, humanity must now go before Jesus, resemble the heart of Jesus Christ, resemble the body of Jesus Christ, resemble the heart of the Holy Spirit, and resemble the body of the Holy Spirit, and appear confidently before all things in heaven and on earth, and become a person who can establish his or her one individual before God and boast.
And I must become someone who can boast before Jesus and the Holy Spirit. And then, I must become someone who can boast before the apostles. Thus, standing before the Father, I must be able to confidently exclaim, “Father, who has toiled for 6,000 years until now! I will subjugate Satan, who has been the enemy for 6,000 years, in my own body, so, Father, from this hour on, please let go of your worries about Satan.”
And then, I must have the heart to be able to say, “And the groaning of sin that has permeated this entire garden of creation has all receded because of me, so, Father! Please resolve the groaning that has permeated heaven and earth with this.”
And then, for 6,000 years, God established his beloved sons and daughters but was never able to love them. Even today, although God has a heart that wants to love us, he cannot truly find and establish us and love us. Jesus and the Holy Spirit can come and love us, but God cannot love us until we believe in the word.
The responsibility of the believer
Therefore, today, we must have a center on behalf of Jesus Christ and become a being who can say, “Abba, Father! I will take responsibility for all the sins and groans of the people of this earth today, so, Father, who wanted to love humanity for 6,000 years,

Therefore, the responsibility of us believers today is….
Jesus came for this earth and toiled for heaven. In this way, only a being who can stand proudly as a central being representing the infinite spirit world before Jesus who toiled for heaven, Jesus Christ who appeared as the center of heaven and earth, can participate in the world of glory where Jesus Christ appears with the joy of heaven and earth, and you can live in a world of joy with God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit. You must keep this in mind.
<Prayer> Father of love! When we look at the 6,000-year history, in a broad sense, it has been a period of night until now, and we are now in a moment of admiring the dawn of the morning that must appear.

I have spoken briefly about this at this time.

Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.

Let Us Return the Glory of Resurrection to God Like Jesus

<Sermon> The title of the sermon I would like to contemplate with you at this hour is, "Let Us Return the Glory of Resurrection to God Like Jesus." I will speak for a short while under this title.

The Ideal of Creation and the Purpose of Jesus' Advent

The Garden of Eden is a garden where the eternal God can enjoy glory, and all of creation can offer joyful worship to God and live in gladness. Creating such a garden was God's purpose of creation. Also, human beings had to manifest the glory of God's desired hope on the earth. Thus, it was the responsibility of our ancestors, Adam and Eve, to manifest God's glory as a reality, but because they fell, that will could not be fulfilled.
The original garden where God intended to rejoice after achieving the ideal of creation was not realized due to the human fall. Therefore, all of humankind until now has been going through a path of struggle, confronting the forces of darkness while hoping for the glory of resurrection. This has been the course of six thousand years of history.
Throughout history, God has desired to greet the one day when He could achieve the total glory of resurrection and the total inheritance of resurrection, and not only the billions of created beings on this earth but also the myriads of angels in the spirit world and all things of creation could sing of God's glory and offer worship of gratitude. To greet that one day, God sent numerous prophets to this earth, and after four thousand years of history passed, the one whom God sent as the glorious substantial being, embodying His own internal heart and external reality, was the only-begotten son, Jesus Christ.
Since God's glorious being had appeared in this way, the people should have rejoiced and offered thanks. That is, the chosen people of Israel and the religion of Judaism, which was established to fulfill the will of the providence, should have manifested the glory of Jesus on his behalf, but they could not. Thus, you know well that Jesus had to leave behind laments of sorrow and resentment.
When we look at the words Jesus left behind today, his words were not cried out only to the unbelieving people. He spoke to all people.

01477

Jesus was prepared to die for God. He knew that the remaining path was a path of destiny that he could not but go, and knowing that fallen human beings had never, at any time or in any historical process, given their all in heart, character, and will for God, Jesus stepped forward with confidence and cried out. "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, and with all your soul, and with all your mind," he said with confidence. You should not think that this one phrase applies only to yourselves.

The Words Jesus Gave
Then what does this one phrase represent? Jesus keenly felt God's anxious internal heart that had permeated the four-thousand-year course of history. Thus, feeling the responsibility to attend God himself, he reaffirmed here that at any time, in any hour, he himself had to become the representative who gave his all in heart, which had not existed in the four-thousand-year course of history, the representative who gave his all in life, and the representative who gave his all in will.
Heaven's glory was to appear as Jesus' glory, Jesus' glory was to appear as the glory of all people, and the glory of all people was to extend to everything in all of creation. However, you must know that because Jesus and the nation were severed, the glory of resurrection and the glory of gratitude that were achieved in Jesus himself have remained as the hope of humankind today.
Jesus appeared as the incarnation of God's glory. One being who gave his all in heart, character, and will for God, the incarnation of victory that had not existed in the course of history, was Jesus. Therefore, you must know that God's heart is accumulated in Jesus himself. Furthermore, you must know that before Jesus gave his all in heart, God first gave His all in heart. You must know that before Jesus gave his all in will, God first gave His all in will. And you must know that before Jesus gave his all in character, God first gave His all in character. Thus, the one who appeared as a mediatorial being, as the incarnation of the gospel, was Jesus.

01478

Let Us Return the Glory of Resurrection to God Like Jesus

Therefore, this word of truth from Jesus was not a word spoken through what was felt nearby, but a word spoken through the ideal of human creation, a word established as an ideal of glory that could elevate the value of the whole, and a word that revealed the Father's hidden heart. You must know this.
Today, you should not think that the words God spoke were spoken because He loved only you. And Jesus spoke such words because he thought that he now had to substantially fulfill the will of God, who had worked hard to establish him. The word he testified to, that just as God gave His all for Jesus, human beings have the responsibility to give their all for God, has been passed down to this day unfulfilled.

God Who Has Been Seeking with All His Heart, Will, and Character
Therefore, we must now revere God with all our heart, will, and character, and we must know that God Himself first came seeking us with all His heart, will, and character.
For four thousand years, what kind of heart did God have toward human beings? He did not come with a heart for His own sake. Although they were human beings who deserved to die immediately and suffer, God walked the four-thousand-year course of history of patience from the position of giving His all in heart for human beings, and you must know that He also walked the course of struggle to discern Satan for four thousand years with all His will.
Thus, we must know the character of God, who has endured, fought, and loved for four thousand years with an unchanging heart of love.
Jesus, who appeared before such a God, gave his all in heart to establish the kingdom of God centered on the people of Israel. Therefore, the course of Jesus' thirty-some years of life was a period of sacrifice of giving his all in heart. In the course of his thirty-some years of life, he did not reveal himself before the nation but silently sought to experience the heart of Heaven, which had endured for four thousand years.
Thus, Jesus felt the twisted facts related to Satan in the four-thousand-year course of history and received internal testimony of them from the spirit world and revealed them. Furthermore, you must know that Jesus was the one who bore the responsibility to reveal the secrets of the heavenly law hidden in the four thousand years of history, to establish the substantial foundation of God's internal endurance, and to establish the external substantial foundation in his thirty-some years of life.
Therefore, the more difficult the situation Jesus was in, the more he was in a position to seek himself, but he could not even think of seeking himself. You must know that Jesus felt the one heart of God, who had endured while seeking Jesus himself through the four-thousand-year history, the heart of God who had endured to find each and every human being, and that he lived a life of preparation for thirty-some years to appear as the substance to resolve that heart.
Until this hour, God has not made excuses for His position to anyone. He could not make excuses to all people, nor did He make excuses to the enemy, Satan. Because Jesus was one who sought to experience this entire heart of God, he endured without making excuses to anyone, even when he was in a lonely position. You must emulate this life of endurance of Jesus.
However, God endured for Jesus, and Jesus did not endure for himself but for the Father. That is, Jesus felt that God had walked a course of hardship to find him, so he did not endure for himself but for God.
Thus, because Jesus left himself and endured for God for thirty-some years, he surpassed Satan's endurance. Satan has struggled until now to destroy the path that God has endured for four thousand years. However, Jesus, who knew that there was a Father's endurance that was greater than Satan's endurance, believed in that Father and endured like the Father, so he became the incarnation of endurance.
In this way, when Jesus himself stood on the foundation of the heart of God's four-thousand-year endurance, and using that as a victorious foothold, he fought against Satan with patience and won, but if he could not establish a substantial foundation of victory, you must know that the heart of God's four-thousand-year endurance would be destroyed.

01480

Let Us Return the Glory of Resurrection to God Like Jesus

Jesus Who Defeated Satan with a Heart of Endurance
Because Jesus, throughout his thirty-some years of life, endured for the sake of God's will even when he was in a situation where he could not endure, and because he endured in a position where Satan could not endure and upheld God's will, and because he was established as a model of one who endures, Jesus became the protagonist who could fight against Satan.
God went through a four-thousand-year course of shedding blood to find the one person, Jesus. Also, while human beings were struggling to fulfill their own individual desires, God walked the course of the history of struggle for the sake of human beings. In this way, although God fought with Satan for four thousand years, God did not fight centered on Himself.
However, what Satan has wanted while fighting until today was for his own glory. Also, he has been fighting with God centered on himself until now. However, God did not fight for Himself. The purpose of God's fight was for the pitiful human race in Satan's bosom, and it was to put forward the one person, Jesus, through the chosen people.
Then what kind of being did Jesus appear as? He appeared as the substantial substitute and incarnation of the victory that God had won by fighting with Satan for four thousand years. Jesus came to this earth as the protagonist of the fight on behalf of God in this way. Therefore, the course that Jesus practiced with the responsibility to inherit the will of God, who had established the standard of internal victory, and to establish the standard of external victory on the earth was the three-year public life course.
During this three-year public life period, Satan fought with Jesus for his own victory but was defeated, so he once again mobilized the nation to fight with Jesus.
However, during the three-year public life period, in any difficult place of battle...
never fought for his own sake. Jesus

1481

said that he did what he saw the Father doing. He walked the three-year public course as the incarnation of battle on God's behalf, as the substantial being who could express God's internal heart. Jesus did not fight to defend himself.
Just as God could not make excuses for Himself, Jesus also did not make excuses for himself in the position of fighting Satan before all people.
Jesus was one who served God with an unchanging heart for the toil of His providence that He had carried out for 4,000 years for His own sake.
Realizing the fact that God's will was manifested through the course of the providential battle, Jesus waged a fight to externally fulfill the entire will that God had established internally. However, in the fight between Jesus and Satan, Satan fought for himself, but Jesus fought for Heaven. This is where the standard of victory was established.
Then what is the reason for Satan's defeat? It is because he fought for himself. The purpose of Satan's fight was for himself. However, Jesus placed the purpose of his fight in Heaven. And because Jesus fought with all his will, with a heart that would not change to the end as long as God did not change, he established the standard of victory. Also, just as God gave His all with all His heart, all His will, and all His character, Jesus also showed such an attitude before humankind.

Jesus, the Substantial Embodiment of God

Thus, Jesus, on behalf of God's internal character, could inherit the heart of God, who loved while enduring all difficulties and sorrows. Therefore, wherever he was, Jesus fought against Satan only as the substantial embodiment of God's will and God's love.
In the course of fighting Satan, Jesus knew that when Satan attacked centered on his own purpose, the impact would not only be on Jesus himself but also on God. Therefore, no matter what

1482

Let Us Offer the Glory of Resurrection to God as Jesus Did

hardships he faced, just as God had endured for him (Jesus), and just as He had endured for all people, and just as God had fought against Satan in the providential course until that time, he fought against Satan, enduring alone for his thirty-some years of life. In this way, Jesus' life, up to the climactic moment of his death on the cross, was a life in which he, as the substantial embodiment of God, consistently practiced and manifested God's love. However, his life's course, that is, the course of practicing God's love, was a course of trial walked while fighting against Satan.
But why did God hand Jesus over to Satan to die on the cross? It is not because God did not love Jesus. Do you know to what extent God loved Jesus? You must know that God's highest love is actually received in a place beyond death. Therefore, in order to receive the love of Jesus, who came on behalf of God, you must have the earnest heart to be able to cross the hill of death. This is because Satan will inevitably surrender at that point.
For 4,000 years, God alone looked upon the entire world, grieving, worrying, and toiling, but with the establishment of one person, Jesus, on the earth, a new battle with Satan centered on him began. Thus, Jesus not only forgot all about himself and fought for God, but he also had no desire for himself even in the place of death, so he was able to manifest the power of resurrection. Today, we too must go through such a course of victory like Jesus.
Jesus offered everything he had to possess God's eternal life and to manifest God's glory. And he offered himself as a sacrifice for sinful human beings. We must know the love of Jesus, who raised his hands and prayed for humankind from a position where he could even forget Satan's opposition.
Because Jesus manifested a love that could not be manifested in the satanic world, Satan had no choice but to surrender to his love. Satan had his own will to seek, but through Jesus, he came to feel shame.

1483

Thus, because of the cross, not only did God, who had been providentially working for 4,000 years, begin to feel sorrow, but humanity also began to feel sorrow, and even Satan began to feel sorrow. You must know this.
It was not only God and humanity who grieved over Jesus' death. Satan also came to grieve over Jesus' death of love. Therefore, the greater Satan's sorrow becomes, the more the fruit of Jesus' love will be borne.
Through the victory of the cross that proved his love, Jesus formed an unchanging bond with God, who had been providentially working for 4,000 years, and became the substantial embodiment of unchanging victory and unchanging love. Because Jesus became one with God on behalf of heaven, earth, and humanity, as long as God does not change, Jesus Christ also could not change.
God had tried to manifest His glory for 4,000 years, but that will was not fulfilled. He intended to finally fulfill that will by establishing one person, Jesus. Therefore, Jesus sought to manifest that will on this earth through human beings. He was to appear as the evidential substantial being of God's 4,000-year providence, but because of the cross, that will was trampled by Satan. However, Jesus, as the eternal substantial being of God, showed the glory of God who had been providentially working for 4,000 years. What was that? It was the glory of resurrection. You must know this.

Jesus Who Manifested the Glory of Resurrection

That resurrection, for the first time in 4,000 years of history, represented the glory of heaven, and it represented the glory of victory in the 4,000-year battle with Satan. Because Jesus showed this victorious standard both spiritually and substantially, God raised the dead Jesus again and began to unfold a new providence. By being hung on the cross, Jesus took responsibility for the 4,000-year providential history and the responsibility of his ancestors, and his resurrection and ascension were his going to that land on behalf of the glory of heaven.

1484

Let Us Offer the Glory of Resurrection to God as Jesus Did

In this way, Jesus was the one who came to substantially fulfill the internal glory of God on this earth, that is, to manifest the complete glory of God. This is because complete glory can only be achieved when the internal glory and the external glory are united. Jesus came to fulfill this very mission.
For God's glory to be completely fulfilled, the only begotten Son, Jesus, who came as the substantial embodiment of God's internal glory, and the Jewish people should not have become distant but should have become one, so that the internal glory of God within Jesus could become the glory on earth. However, because Jesus, who was supposed to take charge of God's 4,000-year providential history and realize God's glory on earth, died on the cross due to the disbelief of the Jewish people, the internal glory of heaven became a spiritual glory. Therefore, Jesus ascended, having achieved an incomplete glory.
After his ascension, Jesus, in the spirit world, is fighting the battle of heaven that God had been waging against Satan for 4,000 years, the battle of truth to restore humanity, the providential battle to fulfill the will, and, on behalf of the Holy Spirit, the battle of love. In other words, Jesus went to the spirit world, took over this battle that God had been fighting, and is fighting on God's behalf.
Then, where is the foundation where Jesus Christ, who represented humanity, all things, and the love of heaven before God who had been providentially working for 4,000 years, must truly be victorious? It is none other than this earth.

The Holy Spirit Who Is Responsible for the Battle on Earth

Then who should be responsible for this course of battle remaining on earth? While Jesus has taken over and is fighting God's internal battle in the spirit world, the Holy Spirit and we on earth must cooperate together to be victorious in the battle of love to substantially complete the internal battle and the internal providence.

1485

This battle is not a battle fought only spiritually. It must be fought both spiritually and physically. And you must know that the destiny to win in that battle remains with us, human beings. In other words, it is our destiny to take over and win the internal battle of God that Jesus has been fighting in the spirit world until now, and the battle he fought for the salvation of humankind, sacrificing his thirty-some years of life on this earth.
Therefore, you must now pray and cry out, “Father! Jesus! Holy Spirit! Give me strength,” and do your utmost to fulfill the historical desire of heaven on earth.
Jesus came to this earth as the fruit of God's 4,000 years of toil, and he came as the first perfected being that God had hoped for. However, Jesus Christ had a course that he could not complete in his thirty-some years of life. And in the course of battle during his three-year public ministry, there remains the regret of not being able to fully fulfill God's glory, and the heart of love that shed blood on the cross remains on the earth.
For this reason, today we must take over the mission that Jesus could not complete on earth and fulfill it both spiritually and physically. And we must offer our entire life course to inherit and continue the path that Jesus Christ walked.
Then, what should I do today when I stand myself before the Father and criticize myself? Jesus fought against Satan to fulfill God's will, and for 2,000 years after Jesus' departure, he has been toiling together with the Holy Spirit. You must resemble such a Jesus. And you must know that the period in which Jesus stood himself before the Father and waged a victorious battle was not just one day, but a period of thirty-some years. You must know the heart of the Father who has been providentially working for 6,000 years, the anxious heart of Jesus to fulfill the will, and the heart of the Holy Spirit.
Thus, if you cannot endure with all your heart in the course you must endure today, then because of you, the will of God who has been grieving for 6,000 years, the will for which Jesus toiled his entire life, and the will for which the Holy Spirit has toiled for 2,000 years since Jesus' death will all be frustrated. You must know this for sure.

Therefore, you must now wage a battle for this will.

Our Mission

Jesus received much opposition from his enemies. When he was driven out of this town, he went to that town, and when he was treated with contempt in this place, he fled to that place. Even in such circumstances, Jesus did not know how to defend himself. He came with the entire life of heaven, but he could not show such value. Thus, he was a Jesus who went through a course of silent battle, and furthermore, a Jesus who, even on the summit of the cross, forgot himself and fought against Satan to testify centered on God's will and love.
Therefore, if you have any heart of love to find and establish Jesus himself, it will not make Jesus sad but will make him happy. Thinking of this fact, you must today take the place of Jesus' deeply felt thirty-some years of life, and you must take the place of the heart of God who has endured until today.
You must take the place of the hearts of the prophets who established altars and providentially worked through the nation to fulfill God's will for 4,000 years, and you must emulate the heart with which Jesus loved humanity. Thus, today you must do the same kind of work as Jesus did when he did not establish himself and made Satan sad by setting a standard of victory with a heart that did not love himself. You must conclude all the battles of the 6,000 years.
You must be victorious in all the battle courses of endurance. You must also be victorious in the battle of testifying to the will of heaven. You yourself must take the place of Jesus Christ. You must have the heart of victory of the will, glory, and love that God has endured for 4,000 years. Just as Jesus forgot himself and toiled only to fulfill the will of heaven, you too must forget yourself and bear the fruit of the entire glory that God desires. You must bear the fruit of victory with your heart and body.
