(6)

Let Us Fulfill God's Will of Love to Unify

The title of the words I would like to give today is, Let Us Fulfill God's Will of Love to
Unify. I will speak for a short time under this title.
These are words that you know well as the most important words in your life of faith,
memorize well, and regard as the center of your life for living well.

God's Hope in Providential History through the Prophets

Because God's will was not fulfilled due to Adam's fall, the providence of restoration
has been repeated throughout the course of history until today.
It was God's original will of creation for God and human beings to live in harmony in one love,
centered on one will, and for the whole heaven and earth to rejoice in God's love and live as one,
with that love established as the center of actual life. However, due to the fall of Adam and Eve,
God's love remained only as God's love. In other words, God's love, which was supposed to form a
relationship with human beings, could not form a relationship with them and departed from them,
and it departed from the entire created world.
Therefore, God has been going through 6,000 years of history until now, hoping for the one day
when He can gather all things centered on the love He intends to establish and enjoy that day together
with all things. However, the entire creation has not yet been unified as one centered on God's
love, and that ideal of God remains as an ideal, and the love of hope that must be found also
remains as it is. Therefore, God has been conducting the providence until now to surely fulfill
that will.
In this way, God has been conducting the providence for a long time to fulfill God's hope and to
find a heart that can believe in and love human beings, regardless of the era, since the human fall
until today, but He has not yet been able to achieve or find them.
When we look back at the history of Heaven's providence, we can see that God intended to establish
an unchanging standard of hope for human beings, an ideal for human beings, and love for human beings
by raising up one person, Abraham. Only when the day comes when this will of God is fulfilled, only
when the day comes when such a center of love is established, can a relationship between God and
human beings be formed, and based on that established relationship, God could enjoy the joy of a new
ideal, which is why He chose and raised up Abraham. However, because Abraham failed to establish the
center of love, God had been laying the foundation to establish the will of heavenly love until the
time of Jesus.
Therefore, the 4,000-year history up to Jesus was a period in which a single substantial being who
had fulfilled God's hope, faith, and love had to be established before the entire will of the
providence. If such a being was not established, God's hope, faith, and love would each be separated
and would be marked by a history in which unification could not be seen in any period, so God first
laid the foundation of hope. Then, on that foundation, He intended to lay the foundation of faith,
and on that foundation of faith, He intended to lay the foundation of love. Thus, in the end, He
wanted to greet the one day when He could present before heaven and earth a single incarnate being
who was the fruition of all these things, that is, the substantial self of the entire hope, the
substantial self of the entire faith, and the substantial self of the entire love. However, if such
a one day could not be greeted, the ideal of unification centered on God's love could not be
accomplished on this earth.

Let Us Fulfill God's Will of Love to Unify

is.
To establish that one day, God had been working hard, laying the foundation of hope by dividing the
4,000-year providential history from Abraham through Moses to John the Baptist into three stages.
Who was the one who appeared as a single substantial being on that foundation of hope? It was Jesus
Christ. Because Jesus Christ was a being who appeared as the one substantial being that God had hoped
for for 4,000 years, he was the total fruition of the 4,000 years of providence that God had conducted
with hope.
Then, what was it that Jesus planted when he came to this earth as such a fruition? It was the
gospel of the New Testament established through the course of faithfulness, that is, the gospel of
faith. After that, 2,000 years of history have passed centered on this gospel of faith.
You must know that the one being who appears as the substantial being of the entire love, representing
heaven and earth on the foundation where the gospel of faith has borne fruit, is the Lord of the
Second Advent who is to come. Then what does God intend to do in the age of the Second Advent? You
must know that the purpose of God's 6,000-year providential history is to plant a seed of life on the
foundation of faith that has been laid until now, centered on the coming Lord of the Second Advent,
and to bring it to fruition.

Central Elements of the Completed Testament Age

Today, we look to God as the protagonist of our hope, and we look to Him as the protagonist of our
faith. We also look to Him as the protagonist of our love. God, who is the protagonist of this hope,
faith, and love, had human beings go through the Old Testament Age, which represented hope, and the
New Testament Age, which represented faith, in the course of history, so in the future, they will
have to go through the Completed Testament Age, which represents love.
Then, what is it that can remain as the one eternal and unchanging central element in such a
Completed Testament Age, that is, the age of the Second Advent? It is God's love. It is the central
element of the whole and at the same time the element of the ideal of the whole.

is.
Therefore, until now, human beings have come through the providential course of hope and the
providential course of faith for this love. However, you must know that if you yourselves do not walk
the providential course of love, the foundation of unification that God must achieve on this earth
centered on love will collapse.
Jesus Christ, who appeared as the center of faith on the foundation of hope, spoke words to establish
faith on this earth. If the people of that time had embraced this Jesus Christ as the substantial
being of faith, that is, if they had known and served Jesus as the fruition of the hope of God's
4,000-year providential history, the central being of faith in the eternal course of faith, and a
single substantial being who could testify to and integrate the eternal love of God, then the people
of that time could have had the eternal hope of God, the eternal faith of God, and could have
experienced the eternal original love of God through the one person of Jesus.
However, due to the disbelief of the Jewish people, Jesus Christ died, and as a result, today in our
course of faith, we have come to complete only the spiritual substantial being of hope, only the
spiritual substantial being of faith, and only the spiritual substantial being of love.
Then, what is the standard of victory for God's love? Any being in heaven and on earth moves centered
on God's love. However, because Jesus Christ, who came as the incarnation of that love of God, died,
all that will was shattered.
Jesus was the being of hope accompanied by 4,000 years of God's labor, and he came as the master of
all things, hoping to become one with God. Originally, the human ancestors' hope to become one with
God was broken by the fall of Adam and Eve. Therefore, it was supposed to appear as a substantial
being of faith encompassing both spirit and body, united with God's ideal centered on Jesus Christ,
but it was completed only in the spiritual aspect.
Therefore, today we must inherit and fulfill the inheritance that Jesus left behind. Just as Jesus'
one body became a single substantial being of hope with spirit and body, I must become such a person
and be able to represent him, and just as Jesus was a substantial being of faith, I must become such
a person and be able to represent him. Also, just as he was a single substantial being centered on
love, I must become such a person. Thus, standing before God, I must represent the hope, faith, and
love of Jesus, and furthermore, as the substantial being of the Holy Spirit's hope, as the substantial
being of the Holy Spirit's faith, and as the substantial being of the Holy Spirit's love, I must
fulfill that mission.
This is the mission that human beings on this earth today must fulfill for the Father after Jesus
came and went. Therefore, when we complete that mission, we can see the conclusion of Jesus' hope and
the conclusion of the Holy Spirit's hope. Furthermore, we can see the conclusion of Jesus' faith and
the Holy Spirit's faith, and Jesus' love and the Holy Spirit's love. Thus, you must achieve the day
when you can conclude all those things, and only then can the Lord of the Second Advent appear on this
earth.

Human Beings Must Become the Substantial Beings of God's Faith, Hope, and Love

God's hope was not God's own, but a hope for human beings. God's faith was also not God's own, but a
faith for human beings. Also, God's love was not a love for God Himself, but a love for human beings.
Therefore, human beings must be able to represent that hope of God, represent that faith, and
represent that love. At that time, God can boast of that one human being before all things as a being
who represents the hope of the whole, the faith of the whole, and the love of the whole.
In other words, He can boast of that one being as the central body of hope that all these things
desire. Also, He can boast of him as the protagonist whom any being in the entire creation, that is,
in heaven and on earth, can believe in and live by. Furthermore, He can boast of him as a central
body of adoration whom all beings can love.
Just as Jesus Christ appeared as a mediatorial incarnation representing God's love, today we must
receive the hope, faith, and love of Jesus Christ and appear on this earth as a substantial proof of
hope, a substantial proof of faith, and a substantial proof of love before any evil person.
If one does not become such a being, one cannot establish the condition to pay indemnity for the
standard of Jesus Christ's hope, the standard of faith, and the standard of love anywhere. Therefore,
today we must repay Jesus Christ, who appeared as the substantial being of God's hope, God's faith,

<Sermon> The title I would like to speak on for a short time today is "Let Us Become People Who Repay Their Debts." I will speak on the title, "Let Us Become People Who Repay Their Debts."
Human Beings Who Owe a Debt of Sin and a Debt of Toil
Originally, when God created the heavens, the earth, and all things, He did not establish the principle of being in debt. It was God's purpose of creation to form a relationship of oneness with human beings as one substantial proof, having the form of two but being able to give and receive with each other, where yours is mine and mine is yours.
Because Adam and Eve, who were created for this purpose, failed to fulfill God's will and fell, the billions of human beings from then until now have become beings who owe an infinite debt to heaven. The one who was sent as a representative being to establish a way for fallen human beings to be able to repay their debts again was none other than Jesus Christ. Therefore, we are living a life of repaying debts through the historical course through Jesus Christ. Also, through this life, we are looking forward to eternal life.
You may think that you as an individual are qualified to be presented before the whole universe, but you must know that in your body, without your knowledge, there remains a debt of sin received through the fallen lineage over thousands of years of history.
Also, we must know that in addition to the debt of sin, we have a debt of the toil of God's providence for us human beings, and in addition to that, we have a debt of the toil of the tens of thousands of prophets, saints, and legions of angels who have carried out the history of restoration.
When we think about these things, we come to know that I, as one individual today, am a human being who cannot repay the debt owed to the heavenly law, no matter how much I try, and who cannot save face, no matter how much I try. The one who was established to represent us in order to save the face of such human beings and establish them before the heavenly law was none other than Jesus Christ.
The Debt of Eternal Life, the Debt of Life, the Debt of Love, the Debt of Relationship
We were human beings who should have had eternal life centered on God from the time we were born. We were beings who should have represented God's love from the time we were born through our parents. Also, we were beings who should have had a love that represented our parents, centered on the couple. We were human beings who should have formed a relationship of love with all things.
However, because we failed to become such human beings, you must know that human beings owe a debt of eternal life to God, a debt of life to their parents, a debt of love in the couple, and a debt of relationship to all things.
Where was the purpose of God in creating Adam and Eve as the masters of all things after creating the heavens, the earth, and all things? It was to give human beings an eternal responsibility. Therefore, we were given the responsibility to love eternally. That is, because Adam and Eve failed to follow God's will and were drawn into the bosom of Satan, the debt of life centered on the eternal love of God...

has come to stay with each of us today.

Jesus, Who Came to Repay Humankind’s Debt in Their Stead

After passing through this era of nature worship and the era of worshipping children, we entered an era of worshipping the bridegroom and bride, and now the era of worshipping the bridegroom and bride is also passing.
Then, what is the remaining era? It is the era of worshipping parents. An era in which parents can be established more completely must surely appear. Therefore, we must now form a relationship between our bodies and God. Although we have felt nothing until now, if we center on Jesus, we can feel new things and form a new relationship of heart with all things. We can also form a relationship centered on God's principle of ownership.
After that, I can enjoy all things and at the same time be drawn into the realm of God's love, and I come to live a life where that love can be drawn into my heart.

To Repay the Debt to All Things

God established this one standard as the purpose of creation, established human beings as the representatives to fulfill that purpose, and had human beings rule over all things, but today human beings are in a position where they cannot save face before all things. Those Qualified to Repay the Debt of Love
Jesus and the Holy Spirit are working today to give you new birth. Thus, human beings receive the elements of Jesus and the Holy Spirit and are heading toward a certain standard, passing through the position of children and heading toward the standard of the position of bridegroom and bride. Today, we believe in Jesus, receive grace, are moved by the Holy Spirit, and are moving forward relying on those powers.
But what is it that must be accomplished in me today? Even if there is no grace from Jesus, even if there is no inspiration from the Holy Spirit, I myself, instead of receiving the grace of Jesus and the inspiration of the Holy Spirit, must be perfected as a bridal body.
This is not being realized in Christianity today. Even we today feel the love of a bride only when the Holy Spirit works. Now that we have grown as children through the work of the Holy Spirit, we must know how to long for Jesus as our bridegroom even without receiving the work of the Holy Spirit. If it must continue to be accomplished with the help of the Holy Spirit, you will have no way to repay the debt of love between husband and wife on earth.
Therefore, you must know that only when I, as an individual, go to the position of a bride who knows how to attend Jesus as the bridegroom without receiving the inspiration of the Holy Spirit, can I become a qualified person to repay the debt of love of the couple, the couple that was established in the original position before the heavenly law.
After the fallen human beings are restored to the position of bridegroom and bride through the providence of restoration, passing through the position of children from all things, what should they do? Next, because we have not formed a relationship with the love of the True Parents who have taken responsibility for our lives and loved us, we must pay by indemnity the debt of love of the True Parents whom God established with the will of creation. You must repay, with your spirit and body combined, the debt of heavenly love in which the True Parents established by God care for your entire life.
In other words, after we are restored as bridegroom and bride through Jesus Christ, passing through the position of children from all things, what should we look for? We must find the True Parents. However, all of humanity in the world today does not know this. For the sake of the fallen parents, they must find the unfallen True Parents, but they do not know when these True Parents will appear. The True Parents appear at the time of the Second Advent.
When the Debt to True Parents Must Be Repaid
In Christianity, they say they will hold the marriage supper of the Lamb through the ideal of the bridegroom and bride. Then, what kind of people are the bridegroom and bride who are the central beings of this marriage supper of the Lamb? They are people who have formed a relationship with the love of the True Parents on earth.
Then, what must I know in order to attend the True Parents and receive their love? I must know the 2,000-year providential history of Jesus Christ until now.
Jesus Christ came to this earth on behalf of the whole universe and humankind and has been carrying out the work to pay by indemnity the debt that humankind has shouldered until now. Therefore, after you have passed through this position of all things, the position of children, and the position of bridegroom and bride, you must face a time when you can attend the True Parents centering on Jesus. Thus, only when the mission of attending the True Parents is completed can the love of the True Parents, who are in the place of the eternal God, appear on earth, and at that time, the mission of Jesus will finally end. Jesus hoped that the purpose of the providence of restoration in the spiritual world would be substantially fulfilled among all things on this earth. Therefore, if the saints who believe in the resurrected Jesus today do not greet on this earth a day when they can repay the debt of the bridegroom and bride that Jesus had to repay, and at the same time, fulfill the purpose of the True Parents that Jesus had to accomplish on earth, and offer a prayer of restoration to God on behalf of all people, we have no way to repay the eternal debt of God's love.
For this reason, Jesus was also in the position of a debtor for 2,000 years. This was because the responsibility remained to repay, on behalf of all people, this debt incurred by not being able to completely fulfill the will of the True Parents. However, that responsibility does not end with spiritual responsibility. The purpose of the 2,000-year historical course of Jesus Christ is concluded only when a family is formed in place of the True Parents, who can sing and worship the love of the eternal God amidst all things in the universe, centering on the eternal life of God, by restoring the position of the original Adam and Eve who had not fallen, combining spirit and body.
In the hope of fulfilling this one purpose, Jesus has prayed to God for 2,000 years with an earnest heart. Thus, he tried to complete the first standard by which the original world of God, who created heaven, earth, and all things, could be found.
If they had not fallen, they could have formed a relationship with their spouse, children, and all things, with the love of the True Parents as the origin. However, because human beings fell, God is carrying out the providence of pulling them up in reverse. In this way, the world where all things, children, and couples form a relationship, and centering on Jesus who appeared as the True Parents, and centering on the standard of the bridegroom and bride, all the myriad creations can respond to the words of the True Parents and appear before God, is the eternal world (無窮世) spoken of in Christianity.

<Sermon> The title of the message I would like to give at this time, centering on the Bible passage that was read,

is "Let Us Restore God's Dominion." I will speak for a short while on this topic.
Finding God, the Lord of Dominion
All things of creation that God made in six days have remained in a sad and difficult position, not yet having been able to attend God as the Lord of dominion. This remains as a destiny that we must absolutely resolve in the course of restoration. Therefore, if we as individuals wish to stand as offerings who can make a pledge before Heaven and be victorious, we must complete the restoration of the dominion that God desires. If we cannot do so, we can by no means stand as offerings of victory. The reason such a course lies before human beings is that after the fall, a world of Satan's dominion, which no one wanted, came into being.
God, who created all things of creation to experience joy through Adam and Eve, lost everything He had created due to their fall. He lost Adam and Eve, and He lost all things. And Satan, who was never even considered, has been dominating all things, taking the position of God the Creator. This is God's sorrow, and it remains as the sorrow of the conscientious people and saints who, in the course of the history of restoration until now, have been praying to Heaven to resemble God's heart.
If you were to set up a created being and ask what its wish is, how would that created being answer? It would reply, "The wish of any existing being is to find God, the Lord of dominion." God Himself knows well that what all things in the universe are seeking is God, the true Lord of dominion, but He is in a position where He cannot directly dominate these things, even if He wants to. You must know that this is Heaven's sorrow.
Now, what is the hope that we human beings today, as one of the created beings who have lost God, the Lord of dominion, desire with our bodies and minds? It is for God the Creator, who used to have dominion as all of creation hoped and idealized, to directly

dominate us once again.
Today, we have the mission to fulfill this hope and will, and we are receiving the calling to accomplish that work. Therefore, we must restore God's dominion, and along with it, we must also restore our dominion as the owners of all things. And we must return the glory of gratitude for the grace of God's dominion. You must know that this responsibility lies not with all things, nor with the heavenly hosts and angels, but with us, who may seem like nothing today.
Therefore, if we fail to fulfill our responsibility even once, we lose the dominion of the entire Heaven, and if we lose the original Heaven, we lose all the hopes of all things. For that reason, if we fail to fulfill the responsibility on behalf of that historical destiny through our lives and through our life, we will not be able to stand before God, nor can we appear before all things as the lords of creation.
And now, you must know that the course that I, as an individual, created as the center of the entire created world and as the center of the internal world with God's creativity, must walk is not one that remains in my individual self of today.
If, in your life of living for the sake of the heavenly law, you live a life thinking only of yourself, God's creative dominion will be cut off because of you. You must know that the hope of all things that desire you to have dominion over them will also be cut off.
Therefore, you as an individual must now reveal the value of representing the position where Heaven dominates the whole and representing the Lord of dominion over all things. Thus, you must be able to say with your own mouth, "I have fulfilled the will of being established as the one being You seek, the original Lord of dominion who represents the whole. Therefore, God, please give the command." The one being who can stand in such a position is the being that God has been seeking and desiring while providentially working for 6,000 years. Therefore, it is our collective duty to fight against hardship and adversity in God's 6,000-year history of the providence, defeat the enemy Satan, and restore human beings.

When we think about the authority of dominion that we, as individuals representing the whole, must find, what specifically must we find today?
Human beings lost God, who has dominion over the whole, due to the fall. They lost God, who has dominion over the whole and is the origin of the whole. Therefore, what we as individuals must find today is God, who created the heavens, the earth, and all things. Thus, you must become people who possess God's dominion as your own.
The Result of Losing God
Then, what is our sorrow today? What is our sadness, and what is our lamentation? What was the earnest wish hidden in the course of the 6,000-year history of restoration until now? It was for me, for all people, for the entire universe, and for heaven and earth to find the God we had lost. God is the substance of the hope we must find and the substance of glory representing the value of the whole. Therefore, for you to restore God's overall dominion today, you must be able to possess God within yourselves. You must become people who can receive God.
Then, what kind of being is that God? You must know that He is the God who created the myriad things of the universe, and He is the God who has been toiling for restoration in order to exercise overall dominion over all things. Therefore, if you now possess God, since that God is your God, if He is eternal, you also become eternal, and if He has dominion over the entire created world, you yourselves will also stand in a God-like position with a substantial body and be able to have dominion over all things. If you cannot find and establish yourselves as such beings, you cannot say that you possess God.
All the sorrow and death on this earth today are, in fact, due to having lost God. And because of losing God, Satan came to act as the master. When viewed from the perspective of the original principle of creation, human beings were created beings who were supposed to attend God as their one master, but due to the fall, they came to have Satan as their master instead of God.
Now, the destined responsibility to repossess the God of love remains with you, but who is it that blocks that path? In this created world, who is it that opposes the will to attend God as the one protagonist? It is Satan, who makes you harbor sin today.
Therefore, if you do not uproot the source of sin that has penetrated your hearts and, on behalf of all people, subjugate Satan, who has been fighting against Heaven for 6,000 years until today, and establish God's world, you cannot exercise God's dominion on this earth.
Then, you are seeking freedom in your minds, but what kind of freedom are you seeking? If you do not find God, you become servants of Satan. Therefore, if you possess Satan instead of possessing God, you become traitors who oppose the heavenly principle. You must know this.
To Possess God
Then, what is the reason God taught the laws of the heavenly way? It was to teach the method to find God, the method to know God. And the course He has been leading the providence to teach that method has been the 6,000-year historical course.
Today, through faith, you know the fact that God is real, and all our members know well that God's original nature is manifested as the central character of all created things. However, that God whom you know must become yours. You must form a relationship with God that can never be severed, no matter how much you try.
If you do so, whether you run to the east or to the west, to the north or to the south, or whatever course you may be in, as long as God does not change, your right of ownership over God will not change. If you cannot stand in such a position, God's demand and hope for you will remain incomplete until then, and you will be in an unprepared state. You must know that if that happens, a condition for Satan to accuse you will remain, and God's sorrow will remain.
What is the work that we human beings, who are in this position, must do today? First, we must escape Satan's accusation. Thus, you must greet the day when you can be testified to, just like Jesus, as "You are truly a son of God, you are qualified to possess God, and you are a son of God who has formed a relationship of oneness with God." If you cannot restore such a day, you must know that you cannot stand before God, who has dominion over all created things, as the protagonists of all things.
By falling, human beings lost God, and at the same time, what did they lose? They lost the original mind of creation. And when I analyze myself, I lost God and, at the same time, I lost the original mind. What you must rely on is your mind. If you cannot control your own mind as you wish, you cannot possess God, and God cannot form a relationship with you.
When your mind establishes an eternal give and take with God, you can possess God, and God will have dominion over your mind as He wishes. Therefore, just as the minds of God and Jesus became one, you today must enter into a position of oneness with the mind of Jesus and stand in a position where you have formed a relationship of oneness with God's mind. If you cannot stand in such a position, a condition for Satan's accusation will remain in your mind.
Originally, human beings were supposed to stand in the position of a second God by living according to the purpose their minds desired within the will that God required, thereby representing God's overall ideal. However, by losing the mind of such a nature due to the fall, human beings today have been left with the condition of having to find this mind of nature while feeling sorrowful, the condition of having to walk a sad course of destiny.
Therefore, we must purify our minds through Jesus Christ. Thus, although our minds are captured by sorrow, when we face the heavenly law, we must raise a new mind and establish a mind of nature that can break through the darkness. By doing so, we must find and establish a form of mind that can connect with the heart of God in heaven and even form a relationship with the minds of human beings engulfed in the realm of death, and raise them up. If you cannot become such people, you must at least repent, knowing that you do not have a mind that God can possess eternally.
In offering our whole heart to God, we should not live a life of offering devotion only at a specific time or season. Just as God is unchanging, you must establish an unchanging heart toward Heaven in the course of your own life; that is, you must establish a foundation of mind that cannot be invaded by any condition of Satan. From now on, that must be established as an unchanging system, and it must become the fundamental principle for advancing toward the path of the heavenly law.
You must know that if you do not possess a mind that God can be proud of, God cannot place you in a position where He can feel pity for you.

<Sermon> The title of the sermon I want to give you at this hour is "The Responsibility of Those Who Have Become Roots." If you look at the scripture in Isaiah chapter 6, verse 11 and onward, it is written, "And though a tenth remain in it, it will be burned again, like a terebinth or an oak, whose stump remains when it is felled. The holy seed is its stump." Here, God is repeatedly saying that if there is a remaining root, He will cause a new shoot to sprout from that root and begin a new history.
Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humankind, were to become the one eternally unchanging root of heaven and earth and fulfill the hope and ideal of all people. However, you know well that because of the Fall, that fundamental root was cut down, pulled out, and transplanted into the satanic world.

The Center of God's Providence

Therefore, the central point of God's providence, which has been carried out to this day, has been to find and re-establish the fundamental root that He intended to establish through Adam and Eve—the root that could have been the root of human happiness, the root of the ideal, the root of life, and the root of love in the Garden of Eden.

Therefore, although the many prophets and saints throughout the course of history who upheld the will of the providence did not know the details of the heavenly way, their labor for the will was to lay the foundation to receive the lost root, which had to be fulfilled as the purpose of the providence, as an unchanging substantial being.

Thus, 4,000 years after the beginning of the history of the providence, the one who was established to find and re-establish the root that was lost in the Garden of Eden was none other than Jesus Christ, in whom you believe.

Therefore, the mission of Jesus Christ, who came to this earth, was to become an eternal root that God could take and, based on this root, re-establish on the fallen earth a form like a vineyard that He could manage as He pleased. This was the very purpose for which God sent Jesus Christ to this earth.

You must know that from the start of Heaven's providence until the appearance of Jesus 4,000 years later, there was a path of toil where numerous prophets and saints shed tears of blood centering on the heavenly will.

That is, there was a providential will representing the clan, a providential will on behalf of the nation and state, and the world, and a providential will on behalf of history. You must not forget that until they passed through that one region, if it was a region, or that one environment, if it was an environment, on behalf of the providential will centered on the clan and history, there was a foundation of labor from countless prophets and saints who could become the elements of the root.


014138

The Responsibility of Those Who Became the Root

And the one who was sent as the substantial being to complete the root that could be established as an individual, to complete it as the root that could be established as a nation, and further to complete it as the root that could be established as the world, was Jesus.

What we who believe in Jesus today must know is that the toil of Jesus' thirty-some years of life and all the toil of the 2,000 years of history since his passing were toil on behalf of the world. And you must know the toil of the prophets and saints who, as a hidden root in the background, fought against the enemy, acting on behalf of the difficult turning points of history until Jesus was established before God as one completed root.

Abraham, Who Lived a Life of Hidden Toil

Who was the historical figure in the background who enabled Jesus to be established as such a completed being? It was Abraham.

Abraham was the owner of a hidden character who did not betray Heaven even in a position where he could betray the heavenly will, being captured in the enemy's country within the satanic realm, in an environment where others did not recognize him. In this way, Abraham, who was like a hidden root, did not avoid but overcame all such circumstances, even if the age was evil, history was in turmoil, and the environment was chaotic. Rather, he appealed with a sorrowful heart toward the collapsing Sodom and Gomorrah.

It is the attribute of human beings to want to boast if they have something, no matter how bad or evil it may be. Yet Abraham, while holding the great providential will promised in his heart for a long time to uphold God's will, did not reveal this fact. In hope, solely as one established root, he was one who lived and passed on after a life of hidden toil, enduring and overcoming in the midst of all kinds of persecution and humiliation to lay an unshakable, immovable standard, no matter who touched or tried to pull it out.

In this way, Abraham was a person who had a sorrowful heart, vowing that on the day he established an unchanging foundation of hope for all the people of the earth, and at the same time, to turn even the evil nations back to Heaven, with his own sacrificial life becoming a sown seed, he would hold onto this standard and not change, in addition to establishing his own unchanging standard of hope before Heaven.


014139

The city of Sodom and Gomorrah was a place deserving of the punishment of judgment from God, and it was a region that had no connection or relationship with where Abraham was. However, Abraham was a person who had no concern whether the city of Sodom and Gomorrah knew the will of Heaven or not, or what would happen to that nation. Yet, not only because he had a providential sense of mission before Heaven, but because he felt a responsibility that he could not but bear, he was anxious and worried about the city of Sodom and Gomorrah day and night. The words written here are what express Abraham's internal heart.

Today, as we face the time of the conclusion of the 6,000-year history, the fact that you sleep comfortably, wear good clothes, and eat delicious food is not because you are great. If you think that way, you are in big trouble.

The reason the world is sustained even like this today is because people you do not know are becoming hidden roots in the background and are building altars of tearful appeal. You have a mission to let all people know this fact.

If there had been a group in the city of Sodom and Gomorrah who knew the fact that Abraham's earnest prayer was reaching the heavens and he was in a dialogue with God, and if there had been even a few righteous people among that group who recognized Abraham, Abraham would have earnestly appealed to Heaven and presented a condition to avert the judgment that was to befall Sodom and Gomorrah. If there had been even a few righteous people, no matter how evil the city of Sodom and Gomorrah was, Abraham could have used the fact that there were righteous people there as a condition and appealed to God, saying, "Father, who judges and passes sentence with righteousness, is it not Your will to judge the righteous and the wicked together with fire?"

However, you must know that when he felt that he alone was praying on behalf of Sodom and Gomorrah, Abraham's sorrow was immeasurably great.


014140

The Responsibility of Those Who Became the Root

Then, do you know the reason why Abram became Abraham?

You must not forget the fact that Abraham had a hidden standard of having appealed for his clan, risking his life, rather than looking after his own happiness and his own well-being.

The Reason Abraham Could Become the Father of Faith

The reason Jesus could appear as the fruit of faith was that someone like Abraham was established before the providence of Heaven and played the role of a hidden root that did not appear on earth. In other words, you must know that even if everything else in the course of providential history was broken, because there was someone like Abraham who could prove an eternally unchanging, immutable faith toward the heavens and played the role of the root of faith, Jesus Christ could be born on that foundation.

Rather than the fact itself that Abram (translated as "great father") from an individual position was decided to become Abraham (translated as "father of a multitude of nations"), the father of faith, if he went through a path of great toil that others did not know, we should look at today's history, place ourselves and Abraham in a one-to-one position, compare, and reflect on ourselves. And we must experience Abraham's position.

Just as Abraham built an altar of a hidden root for the city of Sodom and Gomorrah, you yourselves must have the burning heart of Abraham who earnestly appealed and prayed for the region where he lived and its residents. You must never forget that you must inherit the foundation of faith that was established through the course of Abraham's toil, the standard like a hidden root.

The family of Abraham, the father of faith, received the promise of an organ of blessing. This formed a national form through Isaac and Jacob, and through Moses, and was expanded to a worldwide scope through Jesus.


014141

If it had not been for Abraham's loyalty and faith that reached Heaven, a single bond that could connect with Heaven could not have emerged on this earth.

Today, all people try to show off if they have something good. They try to reveal it and boast about it. However, a person who tries to reveal and let others know in this way may fulfill the responsibility of a branch, but cannot fulfill the responsibility of a root.

Do you know what the hidden secret was that enabled Abraham to become the father of faith? It was because his heart of longing for Heaven and his heart for the earth were so extreme that he could have a broad and deep foothold of connection with Heavenly Father and could become the father of faith.

Moses, Who Became the Leader of the Nation

It is the same with Moses. Until Moses himself was established before the nation, there was a period of 40 years of toil in the palace of Pharaoh where he lived as a hidden root. During his stay in the splendid palace of Pharaoh, Moses did not live a life of wearing glorious clothes, eating, and overflowing with joy. During his stay in the palace, there was not a single moment in his life of eating, dressing, and sleeping that he did not worry about the people of Israel.

Among the people of Israel in Egypt, only Moses' loyalty to Heaven remained unchanged, whether his people knew it or not.

While in the bosom of the enemy, as an unchanging core being, Moses pledged and pledged again that he would not change, no matter what environment oppressed him or what there was that blocked his heart toward the will of the heavenly law. Because Moses had this 40-year period of an unchanging heart and devotion toward Heaven, the power of his love for the nation could later explode.

To you, Moses may seem like a man full of vigor, but in fact, that is not the case. Moses' righteous indignation, which led him to strike and kill an Egyptian when he saw an Egyptian and an Israelite fighting, was not something that arose from the shock of that moment.


014142

The Responsibility of Those Who Became the Root

When he saw that scene, the internal heart of sorrow with which Moses had appealed for his people with a sorrowful heart toward Heaven for 40 years exploded. That is, seeing the chosen people of Israel being treated unjustly, an uncontrollable righteous indignation welled up, and he struck and killed the Egyptian. In this way, love for the people of Israel and righteous indignation toward Egypt were the internal causes of Moses' action. And there was a providential will contained in Moses' action.

Moses struck and killed the Egyptian, unable to overcome his anger, from the position of being concerned about and responsible for the fate of the people of Israel. And since that was trivial compared to the sin of the Egyptians persecuting the people of Israel, God established Moses, who was more concerned for the people than anyone else, as the leader of the nation. However, the people of Israel misunderstood Moses and exposed the fact that he had struck and killed the Egyptian. Knowing that his action had been revealed, Moses had no choice but to flee to the wilderness of Midian.

Moses, who lived in the wilderness of Midian, was ashamed of having lived luxuriously in the palace of Pharaoh and forgot all the wealth and glory of the past days when he lived in a free environment where the daughter of Pharaoh could grant all his requests for him. And although he was in the position of an unknown shepherd who wore shepherd's clothes and herded flocks of sheep, he looked at the flocks and longed for the land of Canaan that had been promised to his ancestor Abraham.

He was a Moses who appealed to Heaven with a heartfelt desire that although he was herding flocks of sheep now, someday he would lead his people and enter the land of Canaan, just as he was leading the flocks. Whether he ate or starved, whether he was awake or asleep, with all his heart and soul, Moses worried and prayed for his people, just as Abraham had prayed for the people of Sodom and Gomorrah without their knowledge.

When Moses looked at the people of Israel suffering from hard labor under the persecution and misery of Egypt, he felt a sorrow as if his bones were melting, and he appealed to Heaven, saying, "O Jehovah! Look upon me and have mercy on this people."

Therefore, God established Moses, whose devotion in appeal was so great, as the leader to lead the 600,000 people out of the land of Egypt. And He had Moses, who was living the life of a mere shepherd in the wilderness of Midian, which seemed like nothing to others, inherit the integrity of the hidden root passed down from his ancestors and established him as the representative of the nation.


014143

And He enabled the people of Israel to become one with this Moses and enter the land of Canaan.

The Jewish People Who Did Not Know the Foundation of Moses' Hidden Devotion
When Moses received the promise permitted by Heaven and was about to enter Egypt, he was overcome with joy. However, Moses was by no means satisfied with that joy alone. Although the will he had appealed for before Heaven—to dedicate his life to leading his people to the land of Canaan—was fulfilled and he had pioneered a way for his people to live, he was not satisfied with such joy alone. Instead, he came to have a sense of mission and responsibility to faithfully fulfill a second responsibility from that point on.
From that time, Moses did not act centered on himself, and there was not a single thing, whether small or great, that he carried out without connecting it to God.
In this way, Moses entered the court of the tyrannical Pharaoh and performed more than ten miracles and signs before their gods, leading the people of Israel out into the harsh wilderness. Here, the people of Israel had to become one with Moses. In other words, for the people of Israel who had escaped to a free environment, though it was a harsh wilderness, the heart of Moses had to become their own heart as they journeyed toward the blessed land of Canaan. Their hearts should not have been different from that of Moses, who had rescued them from the court of Pharaoh. However, because they failed to become one with Moses, they went against the heavenly law and were destroyed. So, what was the cause of their destruction?
They did not know of the foundation of hidden devotion that Moses had appealed for before Heaven in the process of becoming the leader of the people. And although Moses had suffered all kinds of difficulties for them from the day he led them out of Egypt, they did not recognize his toil and hardship. Therefore, they and Moses were divided in the wilderness, and in the end, they met their fate of perishing in the wilderness.

Responsibilities of Those Who Have Become Roots

This historical fact of the Israelites' disbelief in Moses is reappearing today among the saints of the last days.
Saints of the Last Days Who Must Awaken
Although Jesus Christ came to this earth and toiled for all humanity for some thirty years, and for two thousand years since his passing has sought out human beings and worked through love and grace, people are not truly attending him in their daily lives.
And a fearful thing, like the fact that Moses could not completely uphold God's will to lead the people of Israel to the land of Canaan because of their disbelief, may also happen to the saints of the last days. When faced with the fact that he and the people of Israel could not become one, Moses, before rebuking the unbelieving people, appealed to Heaven about his own shortcomings. That is, he went up on Mount Sinai and, while fasting and praying for forty days, he appealed, saying, "Father, why is it that this people cannot enter the land you have permitted, even though it is before their eyes? Whose responsibility is it? The responsibility is mine. It is because I have failed in my responsibility. Therefore, please take me as a sacrifice and block the path of this people's destruction." You must know that there was this period of Moses' hidden devotion.
If the people of Israel had known that Moses' fasting with a sorrowful heart unknown to others was not for himself but for them, they would not have engaged in the faithless act of making and worshiping a golden calf during Moses' forty-day fast. Also, if they had sympathized with Moses' heart and worried about his toil when he was about to be offered before Heaven as a hidden sacrifice on behalf of the people's blessing, and if they could have shed tears with Moses on Mount Sinai and appealed to Heaven, they would not have left God's bosom.
Just as Moses walked a lonely path representing the people by himself, Jesus also walked such a path. That is, Jesus Christ, who was established as the center of the world through the historical sacrifice of Abraham and the course of Moses' sacrifice representing the people, had to single-handedly block all of Satan's conditions for accusation on behalf of all humanity and lay the foundation of victorious indemnity, just as Abraham had blocked Satan's conditions for accusation representing the family and Moses had blocked them representing the people.
Jesus, the Center of Victory and the Savior of All People
You must know that Jesus had this responsibility. Therefore, until he achieved victory on a worldwide level and established an unchanging foundation, Jesus' own person could not end with just his own person. Therefore, Jesus was more faithful than any central figure of faith who had been loyal to Heaven in the four-thousand-year course of history, and he sacrificed his own person for the sake of the whole.
In this way, through his thirty-some years of life, Jesus formed a central form on behalf of the whole in his field of mission, which no one in history had ever established. You must know that if he had not become such a central figure, Jesus could not have become the vanguard who took responsibility for the worldwide providence.
Today, believing saints believe that Jesus is the one who bore the cross of his time, but you must not believe in such a Jesus alone. Before Jesus' death on the cross, there was the altar of Abraham's toil, and there was also the course of Moses' sacrificial toil. And Jesus, feeling the suffering of the people and all humanity in their hardship and misery, not only appealed to Heaven, saying, "Please lay the burden of their suffering on me and grant them the eternal ideal they desire," but he also could not live a single day in comfort in order to actually take responsibility for their suffering.
In this way, because Jesus was concerned even for those in the bosom of the enemy and lived from the standpoint of taking responsibility for the will of the whole rather than his own joy, he was established as the central being who was victorious in the fight against the satanic world and as the savior of all people.
Then, what must we, the believing saints who are in the last days, realize?
We must reflect on the fact that until now, we have not lived a life of shedding tears, worrying, and praying for the wicked.

Responsibilities of Those Who Have Become Roots

The more people there are who must be judged in the last days, the more we must pray for them. And we must not forget that there is a Jesus who worries and prays for us. If we forget and disbelieve in such a Jesus, we will not be able to escape the judgment of the last days.
Saints of the Last Days Who Must Fulfill the Mission of the Root
If the people of Sodom and Gomorrah in the old days had accepted God's warning of judgment, which was foretold through Abraham and Lot, and had reflected on and repented of their evil deeds, they might have been able to escape judgment. Since historical facts teach us what will happen in the future in a demonstrative way, we too, who are in the last days today, must reflect on and repent of our past lives. Therefore, we must clearly know the fact that just as Moses went up on Mount Sinai and prayed for the unbelieving Jewish people, Jesus is also praying for us at this very hour on the spiritual Mount Sinai.
The heart with which Jesus has been praying for humanity while on the heavenly throne for two thousand years was more than the sorrowful heart with which Moses held onto the unbelieving Jewish people and prayed on Mount Sinai. Therefore, you who are on earth must know this and live according to Jesus' will. In the old days, Abraham prayed to God to spare Sodom and Gomorrah from judgment if there were ten righteous people, but because there were not ten righteous people in Sodom and Gomorrah, they suffered God's judgment.
Therefore, just as Jesus has been in heaven since his death on the cross until today, praying for humanity, and just as Moses prayed on the summit of Mount Sinai, you must experience that sorrowful heart and, in this age, hold on to it and worry and pray in Jesus' stead. And you must not forget to be awake, pray, and seek with devotion, asking where the one whom Heaven has established, who can stand in for Jesus' worldwide will and for the prophets and sages of history, is. If there is not even one person left on this earth in the last days as a root, then just as the people of Israel fell in the wilderness, this land where we live will not be able to escape a fearful judgment when it faces the worldwide end times.
If so, what should we do today? Because you are beings like a hidden bush, you must become beings who respond to the desire of the ancestors who have come through the historical course with the spirit of Christ and have longed for a single central root. And you must become people who can fully feel the heart of Jesus Christ, who has toiled for two thousand years as if it were a single day, looking forward to the one day of the Second Coming. This is the problem. Therefore, you must now place yourselves in a relative position to the historical central figures and examine and analyze yourselves. That is, you must place yourselves in the relative position of Abraham, Moses, and Jesus and analyze whether you have become a self that can say that their heart is your heart, their desire is your desire, and their resentment is your resentment.
Now we must know how to build high the altar of appeal, standing before Heaven with empty hands and negotiating. We must know the heart with which Abraham appealed to Heaven for Sodom and Gomorrah. Abraham's prayer for Sodom and Gomorrah was not for his own sons and daughters or his nephew Lot. However, because Abraham forgot everything and built an altar of hidden devotion, Lot, who was related to Abraham, was able to escape judgment.
Today, those who claim to believe pray, "Please fulfill my will." We must not pray such prayers. Rather, we must pray, "Let God's will be done, rather than my will." When Heaven's will is done, the will that I had longed for is also done. Therefore, we must not pray, "Please fulfill my will." We must now, with all our devotion, say, "Abba, Father, since you have established me, since you have called me, please fulfill the Father's will through this little one."
Then, what you must know now is that the inheritance you have received is not the inheritance of your generation alone, but an inheritance that has come down through Abraham, Moses, and Jesus.

You who live in this age must stand in for all the tribes since Moses, and you must fulfill the will that Heaven demands on behalf of the tribes that Jesus needed. Thus, you must know that even if this land is evil, even if this land is dark, even if this land is perishing, you must become the hidden roots that Heaven has established.
What Heaven Demands of Us in This Age
At this time today, Heaven is demanding that we fulfill the mission of religion based on our individual faith. What is that demand? It is whether we have fulfilled our responsibility as Abraham did. And then, just as Moses strove with a sorrowful heart for the people of Israel, it is whether you, when the thirty million people of Korea were in misery, grieved and strove with all your will and heart like Moses. And they will ask if you have toiled in Jesus' stead for all people with the same will and heart as Jesus did when he toiled to save all people from the beginning of creation until now.
Then, when you are asked in return whether you have lived a life like that of Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, you must become people who can say, "Yes. Do you not know us? The hidden root is not only in us, but also in God."
When you become such people, the will of Abraham, who established the integrity of faith through his own person, will bear fruit through you; the will that Moses pleaded for through the people will be resolved through you; and all the elements of sorrow that Jesus embraced for the world will be resolved through you.
If there is such a person on this earth, the sorrowful heart of Abraham in his time, the sorrowful heart of Moses in his time, and the sorrowful heart that Jesus has had until now will be relieved. Therefore, if there is such a person, you must attend him with all your devotion. You must know that if there is no such person, you must become such a person, and if there is such a person, you must know how to exalt and attend him in place of Abraham, in place of Moses, and in place of Jesus. Thus, you should say, "Please pray more for the people. Please be more active." Furthermore, even if you cannot become a sacrifice to be offered before Heaven, you should at least become a person who builds an altar.
Therefore, today you must call out to God, saying, "Father!" Thus, if you do not truly feel that Father who has not been able to act as the master in the course of history from the creation of heaven and earth until now, you will not receive liberation in your lifetime. Therefore, in place of all that, you must build an altar of prayer, just as Abraham prayed, just as Moses prayed, and just as Jesus prayed. *

Luke 22:14-34

Thus, please allow the universal concept that the Father demands of all humankind in the last days to take deep root in their hearts. We know that the word to be given today is not a word that appeared today, but a word that has come through a long history. We also know that in this word, there was an unforgettable, sad event that was forged between Jesus and his beloved disciples, and that our historical ancestors, thinking of it, went forward without regard for the path of death.


The New Covenant That Must Be Fulfilled

To uphold the new covenant that was left behind, the apostles of Jesus and the saints who have believed in Jesus for the 2,000 years since have fought on, without regard for the path of blood and tears, to fulfill on earth the meaning of the promise that was left, the meaning of the earnest desire. This we know well.
Father, please look upon them with pity. Now, open their hearts and allow them to take the place of the hearts of the apostles who attended Jesus Christ 2,000 years ago. Please set our footsteps to pass through the difficult circumstances in which the apostles of old were placed, so that we may be able to fulfill the entire purpose of the providence remaining in the last days. We earnestly hope and desire this.
Please preside over all things from this point on, and by fulfilling the entire will that You are to accomplish, may You enjoy the glory of greeting a day of gladness. Father, we earnestly hope and desire this. We have prayed all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen.
<The Word> The title I wish to speak on today is "The New Covenant That Must Be Fulfilled." I will speak for a moment on this topic.

The Meaning of the Bread and Wine Jesus Broke and Gave
God, who has carried out the history of salvation for 4,000 years through the providence of resurrection, could not conclude the will of heaven and the will of earth together by the providence of resurrecting Jesus alone. Therefore, He established a new covenant, and through this, He has been carrying out the providence of finding the original garden He promised by uniting the will of heaven and the will of earth. This you should know well.
Here it says that the cup Jesus gave and the bread Jesus broke and gave are the new covenant. Since Jesus came and went, we have received his flesh and blood. You must understand that this represents the entire life that must be fulfilled and, at the same time, the entire truth.
What does it symbolize to receive Jesus' blood and Jesus' flesh? It does not refer to the flesh and blood of Jesus as an individual. Broadly speaking, it means heaven and earth; narrowly speaking, it means the center and the individual. Also, the flesh symbolizes truth, and the blood symbolizes the spirit.


Jesus gave all these things to us unconditionally. The person of Jesus, given in such a way, was of course a matter limited to himself, but you must know that any matter of existence in heaven and on earth connected to him as the center was also entirely his matter.
What is it that blocks the way between God and human beings? The will of heaven should appear on earth, and the entire situation on earth should be brought to a conclusion in the will of heaven and move toward one purpose, but this has been blocked. Thus, Jesus, who was the protagonist of love, has been toiling until now, representing that one will that is to appear on behalf of the victorious glory of heaven.
That God toiled for 4,000 years to establish the one person of Jesus was to represent that He could possess the whole of heaven and the whole of earth. Therefore, a person who believes in Jesus can possess all of heaven and all of earth. However, we are entrusted with the overall providential will to not just conclude what we have possessed as our own, but to possess it and then return it to heaven.
Because Jesus established a new covenant and went away, after he passed away, the condition remained for the spiritual world and the physical world to be connected centering on people, that is, the apostles who followed Jesus. If Jesus had not passed away, heaven and earth would have been connected centering on Jesus, but because he passed away, Jesus came to represent the condition of heaven, and the Holy Spirit came to represent the condition of earth.

The Person Who Represents the Will of Jesus and the Holy Spirit
Then, standing in the intermediate position between heaven and earth, who would be the person who can represent the will of Jesus, the person who can represent the will of the Holy Spirit? You must not forget that it is the apostles, or us, who have believed in the new words of the promise on earth until now.
Where is Jesus' desire? That desire is not in heaven.


Where is the desire of human beings? That, too, is not on earth. Jesus' desire must connect with the will of the earth, and the desire of human beings on earth must connect with the will of heaven. Therefore, centering on heaven, you must become a single offering representing heaven and earth, as the holy body representing the blood and flesh that Jesus himself broke and gave.
If you do not, Jesus and the Holy Spirit can never become one for all eternity. The Holy Spirit will continue its history on earth as the Holy Spirit, and Jesus will have no choice but to continue his history in heaven as Jesus.
What is the meaning of Jesus' words to his disciples, "You eat my blood and eat my flesh"? You must not forget that contained within them is Jesus' earnest heart, saying, "Though I may go, you must take all that has entered the realm of the heavenly providence and fulfill my desire."
The blood the disciples received from Jesus symbolizes Jesus' spiritual aspect, and the flesh symbolizes the physical aspect, which represents the Holy Spirit. Thus, Jesus and the Holy Spirit, through that blood and flesh, desired to form a single holy body and be established as a central being that could advance toward a single purpose. And in that blood and flesh of Jesus, the blood symbolized heaven and the flesh symbolized the earth. Therefore, you must know that Jesus' great hope and ambition were manifested there.
Now, after you have become a holy body through the Holy Spirit, your mind must be connected to the holy body of Jesus. This symbolizes the process of the history of restoration. When creating Adam and Eve, He also made a body and a spirit. It is said that He made the flesh and then breathed life into the nostrils to create Adam and Eve. Just as one person was made by combining the principles of these two conditions, so too in the course of the providence of restoration, because the Holy Spirit centering on Jesus established a new covenant, the connected history of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, who have united heaven and earth, has been continuing ever since.
When you think about this, you must realize how important a responsibility is placed upon us today.
You must know that heaven is swayed by the movements of the insignificant apostles, of us who are insignificant. You who are in the place of the apostles! In you who have received the holy body of Jesus, the life force of Jesus, who can represent God, must appear. The moving history of the Holy Spirit, which can represent heaven, must appear. Thus, when you become one with Jesus' will to restore the entire created world and advance, if you turn left, heaven will also turn left, and if you turn right, heaven will also turn right. As you move, so will heaven move.
If you do not establish and conclude the standard through which heaven can move through human beings, Jesus and the Holy Spirit will appeal to you. The universal mission that Jesus left behind will accuse you. When we think of this today, we must feel that through us, who are nothing and insignificant, Jesus intends to accomplish the great universal will that can sway the heavens and the earth.
Jesus does not have the authority to decide without human beings. The Holy Spirit also does not have the authority to decide. The authority to decide lies solely with us, human beings.

Repaying the Blood and Flesh Received from Jesus
Until now, the history of the New Testament has been a history of "Please do it for us." It was a history within the bounds of asking for the sake of hope. The history of the New Testament was one that remained in a place that could not go beyond a certain limit. We must go beyond the words of that New Testament. We must go beyond the history within those limits and know how to receive the grace of heaven. We must become people who can go forward with the entire value of Jesus, who sought to possess all things in heaven and on earth with his own person, and go beyond the limits of that New Testament and say, "Father! Please give me a new promise."
Today, you must manifest in your lives the appeal of Jesus' blood and the appeal He made while His flesh was being torn on the cross. The human responsibility that must be concluded for us to go to the heavenly world has been promised through Jesus. However, it must not end as a promise. You must know that if you do not possess the entire grace, the entire hope, and the entire life in your one body, and with the ideal of your one life, go beyond that limit and establish on earth the standard to be able to give freely, there is no way to resolve Jesus' resentment.
We are now in the process of fulfilling our hope. We are in the process of looking toward a certain purpose and fulfilling that hope. If you have moved in this process, you must be able to conclude the promise of faith you have established. You must know that a self that has gone beyond such a limit is a being that repays what it received of the Lord's blood and flesh at the final moment.
In this sense, what should I do? I must be able to dare to take the place of the front, back, left, right, top, and bottom of Jesus, the front, back, left, right, top, and bottom of the Holy Spirit, and the front, back, left, right, top, and bottom of God.
You must know that if we cannot establish on earth the day of limitation that is to be concluded through human beings, which is the will of heaven and at the same time the will of the earth, then the will of Jesus and the will of God cannot be fulfilled. And when we think of such a will, we must know that our value, which seems insignificant today, is exceedingly great.
What was the one thing Jesus asked of his disciples after giving them his flesh and blood? It is the word, “And he took a cup, and when he had given thanks he said, ‘Take this, and divide it among yourselves’” (Luke 22:17). You must not forget this. Since we have received this flesh and blood of Jesus, if we take responsibility for the problems of heaven on behalf of Jesus’ mission, God’s will shall be done. This is the hope of heaven.
Today, on the condition that we have received the blood and flesh of Jesus, we have the responsibility of the last days to find the altar of victory by forming relationships among ourselves. You must feel this responsibility of ours keenly.

The Lord’s Will, Who Asked Us to “Love One Another”

The principle that comes down from above does not change. Then who will find this unchanging vertical principle and the horizontal relationship that must be connected? You must find it. Jesus and the Holy Spirit have been heading in one direction as the unchanging center, even as history and the age change.

157

Just as Jesus and the Holy Spirit gave and received, we ourselves must form such a relationship. You must know that if we fail to form such a relationship, an altar on which God can work cannot be established on earth.
Do you know the heart of Jesus as he shared his own blood and flesh? It was a heart of unspeakable sorrow. Even in the world today, those who know the will, those who want to live for the will, try to reveal the will even as they overcome by themselves the ordeal of their bones melting in a sorrowful and wretched place. Therefore, you must know what Jesus’ heart must have been like as he looked upon those who did not feel this, those who did not know how to face this will.
If you do not understand these historical circumstances, you cannot even share the horizontal Holy Communion among yourselves. Therefore, today we need a life that expresses the love of the Holy Body, a life in which we can share among ourselves the heart of love that Jesus shared when he communicated with God and when he communicated with the Holy Spirit.
You must know the meaning of Jesus’ request to “share the heart of love among yourselves” in order to enter into one realm centered on heavenly love in some form, connecting individual to individual, denomination to denomination, and even going beyond denominations.
Today, among you, those who do not have a comrade with whom you can give your whole self and receive their whole self in return, you must know that you are a pitiful person. And the Holy Spirit before Jesus gives and receives with him because even if people change, the Holy Spirit does not change. Therefore, you must fight on behalf of the history of the spiritual world on the standard where you can give and receive with him like that.
The time has now come for us to fulfill the one last hope that Jesus left behind. What must you do to connect this one hope horizontally? First, you must become a person who knows how to serve on the earth. You must become a person who fights and is martyred on the earth. You must know how to serve the righteous on the earth.
Today, you must keep in mind what Jesus said. All

“He who serves all people will be served,” and “He who exalts himself will be humbled.” What is this? It is the center of life that we feel on a horizontal level today. Therefore, we must know how to serve anyone, be a friend to all, and also know how to protect them.

To Fulfill the New Covenant

Now that the new words of the New Testament have been promised, we must feel the internal heart of Jesus as he commanded. And at the same time as we fathom his heart, we must also know how to fathom his ideal and practical aspects. Thus, we must fulfill the will of Jesus and the Holy Spirit on their behalf. If such a will is not fulfilled in us, the history of Jesus and the Holy Spirit will be withdrawn in the last days.
If the history of Jesus and the Holy Spirit is withdrawn, on that day of withdrawal, I must be able to stand alone and know the hope of Jesus and the hope of the Holy Spirit, and be able to go the practical course that Jesus went on his behalf. I must become one who, on behalf of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, has a new ideal and can defend it.
We are the people who have received the blood and flesh of Jesus’ new promise. What is the mission that remains for us? It is to fulfill the new covenant. To do so, my own self must be able to overcome Satan in the last days, even without the cooperation of the Trinity. If so, what is the center of being able to overcome Satan? It is to know how to do the actions that Satan cannot do. You must be able to do the actions that Satan cannot do.
The essence of Satan is arrogance. The essence of Satan is jealousy. The essence of Satan is to be only for oneself. Therefore, the teachings of Jesus and the Holy Spirit are to be meek and humble, to sacrifice, and to become a sacrifice. These are all things that Satan cannot do. For Satan to be meek, he must repent of all his sins before God and turn back. If Satan did not have a jealous heart, this world today would all quickly return to heaven.

159

Therefore, you must equip yourself with the elements that are contrary to Satan. Furthermore, you should not remain within that realm of limitation but go beyond it and enter into the new realm of promise. Thus, when you establish one unchanging center, as those who have received the blood and flesh of Jesus, you will be able to fulfill the will of the new promise.
You must clearly know that if you cannot stand in the position where God can again consult with you about what He could not consult with Jesus, and what Jesus could not share with the Holy Spirit—that is, if you cannot stand as the central being who represents all the standards of heaven and earth—then the will of Jesus’ promise will not be fulfilled, and at the same time, the will of the new promise that God desires cannot be fulfilled either.
Today, even if we do not have anything of the world, we must completely have the body and mind of Jesus. We must be recognized by heaven for a central value that represents heaven and earth. Thus, our recognized value must not remain within a certain realm of limitation. We must become beings of such value that no being in the heavenly world can help but welcome us.
The blood of Jesus and the flesh of Jesus are not only valid on earth. They are not only applicable on earth. Just as the course of faith is applicable in the heavenly world, they are also applicable in heaven. Therefore, if we have completely received the blood and flesh of Jesus, my desire will be fulfilled in the heavenly world and also on the earth. And that which is fulfilled will represent the desire of Jesus in the heavenly world and the desire of the Holy Spirit on the earth.
Thus, the two becoming one, we must take on the work that Jesus and the Holy Spirit were doing, let Jesus and the Holy Spirit rest, and go to the standard where we can make a new promise with God. Only then, you must keep in mind that the new history of God, the overall providential history of heaven, will proceed with the standard of victory through you.
