<Prayer (II)> Beloved Father! Please lead us and create an environment where we can stand in the position of the Israelite people who were placed before the figure of John, who saw the form of Christ manifested on behalf of the will of the heavenly law and cried out to heaven standing by the Jordan River.

Even if our hearts are at a great distance in history, please grant us the grace of emotion to hear again the voice of John the Baptist, who cried out with a sorrowful heart centered on the heavenly law. The words, Behold, the Lamb of God, who takes away the sin of the world! were indeed surprising, fearful, and majestic.

Although numerous people, numerous sages and wise men, have come and gone on this earth, we know that the words of John the Baptist, who testified of Jesus, established a new historical standard of re-creation, as there was no one who boldly stepped forward and cried out that he had taken upon himself the sins of all people. May we know the heart of John the Baptist, who found one being who could bear the sins that all people disliked, and please grant us the grace of joy to entrust all our sins to Jesus Christ and worship toward heaven.


Today, please change our environment to the environment of the Israelite people who received the grace of liberation. Please manifest their heart in our environment. Please allow us to realize that if there is one who has found a central figure to whom he can entrust all his sins, there is no one more blessed than him.

Please allow us to feel the joy of one who possesses Heaven, who can entrust my life and my all and be grateful on my own in a free environment, and allow us to recognize again today that Jesus came to this earth and took on our sins.

Please take on all the sins of those gathered at this hour, and allow only goodness to remain and only goodness to be full. I earnestly hope and desire, beloved Father, that a stimulating impulse may arise from us to entrust all elements of sin to Jesus Christ, to give glory to the Father, and to comfort the sorrow of Christ.

Please look upon the many children gathered today with compassion. Please do not let the heart of the one who speaks and the heart of the one who receives be two. Please grant us the power of resurrection that can revive us, and work with the word of re-creation that can bring us back to life. Please grant us the grace of joy to be restored to our original form by breaking the chains of sin and relying on the word of re-creation. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.

I have entrusted everything, so please grant it according to Your will. I have prayed in the beloved name of the Lord. Amen.

<Sermon> The title I want to speak on this evening is Why Did Jesus Become the Lamb Who Takes Away the Sin of the World? I will speak for a moment on this title, Why Did Jesus Become the Lamb Who Takes Away the Sin of the World?

The Background of Jesus' Advent

God created human beings as a central being through whom He could feel His internal ideal in substance. Therefore, through them, He intended to create a world of joy without any gap at any time, by achieving the hidden beauty of heaven, the hidden love of heaven, and the hidden glory of heaven through the life of Adam and Eve, through their lifetime, and through their course of eternal life.

Due to the human fall, this original will that God intended was fundamentally severed, and human beings came to dwell within the dominion of Satan, whom they had not wanted, in place of God. Human beings, who should have lived a life of attending God and returning glory and joy to Him, have instead been repeating a history of humiliation, centering on Satan in place of God and attending and following him. This is something you all know well.

And God has been carrying out His providence until now because there remains glory to be found centered on people, a will to love centered on people, and a work of exhortation to be done centered on people. On the contrary, you also know well the fact that Satan has been continuing the fight to destroy God's glory, the fight to destroy God's love, the fight to destroy heaven's life, and the fight to bind today's human beings in his grasp and not hand them over to God's side.

Therefore, God must now establish a person and set up a condition to resent Satan, establish a person and set up a condition to protest against Satan centered on the glory that should be returned to God, and establish a condition to protest against Satan who is receiving love from human beings on behalf of God. Also, since Satan has the authority over all life on behalf of God, God must establish a person who can protest this as well. This responsibility remains with God.

If a central figure, the original human being whom God seeks to find, who can attack Satan, does not emerge, there is no way to return glory to God again, no way to return love, and no way to return life.

To establish this one central being, God toiled and carried out His providence for 4,000 years. And so, the one who was finally established to testify to God's glory, to testify to God's love, and to testify to God's life, as the center of faith, the representative center of humankind, whom God sought to find before all people, was none other than Jesus Christ.

Jesus' Responsibility

Then, what was the responsibility that Jesus Christ had to fulfill when he came to this earth? He had to restore God's glory, restore God's love, and restore God's life. But what was blocking this was sin.

Sin prevented all people from returning glory to God, from feeling God's love as love, and from feeling heaven's life as life, thus preventing the establishment of a center of eternal life. What is the reason for that? It is because, due to the fall, hereditary sin and personal sin have permeated all of creation, centering on human beings.

Therefore, the responsibility that Jesus Christ had to first carry out when he came to this earth was to fight to uproot the root of sin that permeated all people and all of creation before restoring God's glory, before restoring God's love, and before restoring God's life.

So, Jesus Christ came to this earth and took upon himself the sins of all people to uproot this sin.

Then, for what reason did Jesus have to take on the sins? It was because human beings had sin. And furthermore, it was because human beings did not know the truth.

Jesus Christ came to this earth with God's glory, God's love, and God's eternal life to save all people, but there was one condition blocking his path, and what was it? It was the sin that was woven like a wire fence between this person and that person, this group and that group, this society and that society, this nation and that nation.

Unless this sin is voluntarily liquidated, God's glory cannot be seen on this earth, God's love cannot be seen, and God's life cannot be seen.


God has been having human beings liquidate this sin. When human beings liquidate this sin, He can thereby bestow upon them God's glory, bestow upon them God's life, and bestow upon them God's love. From the human standpoint, the reason God had human beings liquidate this sin was for the purpose of making human beings themselves know the protagonist whom they had not known until now.

Therefore, if we can serve that protagonist on behalf of heaven's glory, serve him on behalf of heaven's love, and serve him on behalf of heaven's life, if we become such people, there is no power that can sever the relationship between us and Jesus Christ, whom heaven has established as the center.

However, because of the fall, until this world comes to an end, there remains a burden of sin between me, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit that must be eliminated. This burden of sin remains in the family, society, nation, world, and heaven and earth, centered on the individual. The news that one being is coming who can take on the burden of sin of this entire world, heaven and earth, is more joyful than anything else, and it is the gospel of salvation and victory.

Then, have we ourselves entrusted our sins to Jesus Christ today? Has our family entrusted its sins to Jesus Christ? Has our society, our nation, entrusted its sins to Jesus Christ? Has this world we live in entrusted its sins to Jesus Christ? The problem is how many saints remain on this earth within the realm of unliberated sin.

What You Must Do in Your Daily Life of Faith

What you yourselves must do in your daily life of faith is to entrust all your sins to Jesus. Have you handed over all your sins to Jesus? You must ask yourselves this. In reality, a being must emerge on this earth who can say, Father! I cannot resolve the sins that remain in me by myself. I entrust my sins to the Father. Otherwise, the ideal of Jesus Christ will not be fulfilled.


If the burden of sin still remains in me, if the burden of sin still remains in my family, and if the element of lamentation due to sin still remains in our society, our nation, our world, and heaven and earth, then the suffering of the cross of Jesus Christ is extended.

You must know the fact that even at this hour, you are repeating the act of extending the suffering of the cross of Jesus Christ.

Today, we must offer a prayer of repentance, saying, Jesus, please take all my sins.
we must do. We must say, “Lord! Please take responsibility for my sins.”
Unless we unite our mind and body, unite the mind and body of Jesus, carry the bundle of sins entrusted to Jesus, pass through Jesus’ hands and my hands, and go through a revolutionary course that can pierce through to the very bottom of sin, we cannot say that we are people who have completely liquidated our sins before the Holy Spirit and Jesus Christ.
Then what is the meaning of Jesus coming to this earth and saying that he will take responsibility for sins? Because we fell, we lost God, the owner of life, we lost the True Parents, and we lost the one center that could protect and love me. The one who came as this central being was Jesus. Now, after Jesus Christ takes responsibility for all the sins of the world, we will face a time when heaven and earth and Satan will have a final showdown over the one person of Jesus.
If you yourselves do not entrust all your sins to Jesus and entrust them to God, then even if Jesus Christ wants to intervene as your master, he cannot. You must know this.
From a human point of view, Jesus is the most unfortunate of the unfortunate
We must know the heart of Jesus. We must know the heart of Jesus who came to find this world. That heart of Jesus was a heart that wanted to bear the sins of the entire universe. You must know that from a human point of view, Jesus was a pitiful person. You must know that when Jesus came to this earth, there was no one as unfortunate as Jesus. He came to this earth to find and to bestow grace, but there was not a single person who knew Jesus’

170

Why did Jesus become the Lamb who bore the sins of the world?

desire and served him, saying, “Jesus is my eternal ideal and unchanging master.”
He came for the sake of the nation, he came for the sake of the country, he came for the sake of the world, and he came for the sake of heaven and earth, but you must know that Jesus Christ, who was established before humankind, was the most unfortunate of the unfortunate. There was not a single person who believed in the words he spoke and the actions he took when he came to this earth, saying, “Oh, we welcome you!” In this way, from a human point of view, the environment in which Jesus personally found himself was an unspeakably unstable environment.
Jesus, too, as a human being, must have had the same sensibilities as you. However, you must know that Jesus, who bore the sins of humankind, who could not solve the sins of his own body, and who took responsibility for the past and future sins of all humankind, forgot his troubles and stood in a position to comfort each individual who resented his own sins in a lonely place. And we must comfort the internal toil, suffering, and sorrow of Jesus Christ, who came to take responsibility for the sins of humankind.
Of course, we must be sorrowful over our sins. The reason why we must be sorrowful is that this sorrow must not directly pierce heaven. The one who came to comfort this sorrow is the Holy Spirit.
Therefore, we must shed our sins with the cooperation of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Otherwise, the agony of Jesus Christ, who took responsibility for our sins, will not be resolved on this earth and will not be resolved in heaven.
Then what is it that you must know now? The Holy Spirit is in charge of atoning for our sins before heaven. This is because human beings do not have a direct relationship with God or Jesus in the heavenly world. That is why we must receive the cooperation of the Holy Spirit, who works on earth.
And what we must know is that although the way to receive atonement was opened through the cross of Jesus Christ, the one who actually takes responsibility for our sins and toils is the Holy Spirit. You must know that the Holy Spirit is toiling in a middle position for our sake, in place of my pitiful situation as a sinner.

171

What kind of toil is the toil of the Holy Spirit? The toil of Jesus, who died on the cross, was the toil of taking responsibility for our sins, and the toil of the Holy Spirit is the toil of crying with you when you cry and being hung with you when you are hung on the cross. And he is continuing the history of the toil of crossing the pass of the cross for you today. You must know this well.
Thus, when the toil of Jesus Christ and the toil of the Holy Spirit become one with me in the middle and surpass the standard of toil that heaven demands, all the sins we have committed on earth are atoned for.
The human responsibility for the toil of the Holy Spirit
Until now, we thought that only I had toiled to meet Jesus Christ, but we must know that behind me, there is the Holy Spirit who has toiled more than I. What Jesus desires is that because the toil of the Holy Spirit is greater than the toil of human beings, he wants to establish this Holy Spirit to represent the glory of Jesus Christ and to unite human beings. Unless such a day is found, Jesus cannot come to this earth again and stand as the protagonist of all people.
Therefore, when we go out against evil, we must know that because of the sins we have committed, the Holy Spirit has come to toil on earth in our place, and Jesus has come to be hung on the cross. Also, we must know that wherever we go in heaven and earth, we are sinners who have no way to escape the resentment of heaven.
Realizing this sin, we must now offer our entire minds and bodies. Therefore, first, by relying on the toil of the Holy Spirit and filling the measure of the toil of Jesus Christ, we must relieve them of the burden of that toil. In this way, when the toil of the Holy Spirit ends because of me, the toil of Jesus ends, and the toil of God ends, the will of heaven’s providence of restoration, which has toiled to take responsibility for our sins, is concluded. And we ourselves will only then find a single protagonist. You must know this.
Jesus came to this earth as the Son of Man and left. Jesus came to this earth as a human being with a body and left. If you look through the spirit world,

172

Why did Jesus become the Lamb who bore the sins of the world?

Jesus has a body with which he can have a one-on-one conversation with us, so if your spiritual eyes are opened, you can comfort and thank Jesus, who died for us, but you cannot do this for the Holy Spirit. This is because the Holy Spirit does not have a body.
Jesus came to this earth as the protagonist of heaven who wore a substantial body and as the center of the created world. However, because the Holy Spirit has not yet had a body, we cannot directly comfort him for the toil of the Holy Spirit. In order to resolve this resentment, the ideal of the bridegroom and bride was established through the 2,000-year history of toil, but Christians today do not know this.
Then when will the substantial Holy Spirit on earth, who can become the bride before the heavenly Jesus, the bridegroom, appear on this earth?
The crime we committed not only made Jesus Christ cross the pass of death, but it also made the Holy Spirit cross such a pass of toil. However, if I resolve the resentment of that toil through my own self, I can return that joy and glory to Jesus, but I cannot return it to the Holy Spirit.
When we entrust our sins, first the Holy Spirit takes responsibility for our sins. After that, Jesus Christ takes responsibility, and then we receive liquidation from God, but we do not know this well today. If saints who know this work and this mission appear, the work of the inspiration of the Holy Spirit will appear to all humankind through them.
Then, since Jesus Christ came to this earth and left, what should we do now? We must find a bridegroom-type protagonist in the same position as Jesus and a bride-type protagonist in the same position as the Holy Spirit. Therefore, we must receive the grace of atonement. And holding on to the Holy Spirit and Jesus, we must be able to say, “Holy Spirit, Holy Son, and God! Please bless us.” Unless you become like that, the 2,000 years of toil of Jesus Christ and the 2,000 years of toil of the Holy Spirit cannot be completed on this earth.
Why did Jesus take responsibility for the sins of the world? It was for us, so that we could possess freedom. And the reason he had us find the master was to move human beings from the position of being ruled by Satan to the position of being able to rule Satan by having them possess their original form.

173

Therefore, after you have gone through that entire course, you must become children of freedom.
To annihilate Satan and become free from sin
What makes us not free is sin. However, sin itself does not make us not free. Satan makes us not free on the condition of the sins we have committed.
Finding the master is the mission we must fulfill, and shedding sin must also be fought centering on the mind and body, but to find freedom, we must fight against Satan.
When we fight against Satan, I cannot annihilate Satan with my own body alone. The Holy Spirit alone cannot annihilate Satan. And Jesus alone cannot annihilate Satan, and God alone cannot annihilate Satan. If I say this, you may say that it is a contradiction.
However, if God Himself could annihilate Satan, why was the 30-odd years of toil of Jesus Christ and the sacrifice of the cross necessary on this earth?
Now we must wage a fight against Satan. And in waging the fight, we must know well for whom we are fighting. We must know that we are fighting first for the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit, and then for ourselves. We Christians know that we are fighting for heaven, but we are forgetting the fact that we are fighting for ourselves. Then why do we fight for heaven? It is to block the offensive and invasion of Satan.
You must know that heaven is mobilized to enable you as an individual to find a blessed path of heavenly principle. You must know that it is also mobilized on earth. That is, in the heavenly world, God is mobilized, Jesus is mobilized, and the Holy Spirit is mobilized, and on earth, you do not know,

174

Why did Jesus become the Lamb who bore the sins of the world?

but many pioneers are mobilized for you. You must know this.
Therefore, you must know that so many people are mobilized in the heavenly world and on earth and are fighting to grant you freedom, and you must be able to repay them.
At this hour today, many people are toiling to lead your mind and body to a place of freedom. God has been toiling for a long time in the heavenly world, and Jesus and the Holy Spirit are toiling. Not only that, but tens of thousands of saints and tens of thousands of angels are toiling. You must not forget this. Also, you must not forget that there are saints who are fulfilling their responsibilities with the determination to die in order to resolve the dark environment in which human beings are bound.
If we know that toiling while fulfilling the mission of heavenly law on earth is to receive glory in that land, we must be able to save face before heaven.
Now, when the day of judgment comes, you will be required to toil like the toil of Jesus to make you free. You will be required to toil like the toil of the Holy Spirit. And you will be required to toil like the toil of God. Not only that, but you will be required to toil like the toil of the many prophets and sages who toiled to liberate you.
You must not live a life of faith that is satisfied with being comfortable, at ease, and joyful for yourself alone. If you live this kind of life, you may avoid the difficulties that come to your own body, but you will have no way to avoid what the Holy Spirit, Jesus, God, and the tens of thousands of saints who have carried out the history of toil demand.
Then, today, if we are to find freedom, become a body of freedom, and lift up our own body and say, “Father! Thank you,” we must be grateful centering on Jesus. In the heavenly world, the Holy Spirit and the tens of thousands of saints are hoping that you will return the reward for their toil to God. You must know this.

175

The resentment of Jesus must be resolved by all the people on earth, and the purpose of Jesus must be fulfilled by all the people on earth. And human beings have the mission to complete that purpose on earth and at the same time to complete it in heaven.
Repaying those who toiled for the liberation of humankind
If we have received atonement through Jesus and obtained freedom and liberation, we must be able to fulfill what Jesus desires. You must know that it is the hope of heaven to find one person who can do so.
Even if the earth is sinful, the earth is evil, and the earth is rebellious, the heart of God
You must know how to connect with the heart of the heavenly law, the heart of the prophets and saints, and stand proudly before Satan on behalf of humanity. Therefore, you must be able to confront Satan and say, "No matter how violent you are, no matter how strong your power is, I will not lose to you," and attack with confidence. A person must emerge who is equipped with this heart of freedom and can boast before all creation. If such a protagonist does not appear, the glory of Heaven, the love of Heaven, and the life of Heaven will not be connected to us.
Today, because we have failed to create an environment of freedom, the ideal of God, the ideal of Jesus, and the ideal of the Holy Spirit are not connected to us. And if this ideal is not connected, the life of God, the love of God, and the glory of God that move in the heavenly world have no relationship with us.
Then why is it that Christians today, who say they stand in a position of having received the grace of liberation through a free faith, are unable to look toward eternity and move forward? It is because even if they are in an environment of joy and freedom through the Lord of glory, that is not everything. They must receive eternal life. Are you in a position today of lamenting and resenting yourselves for changing with each hour and each season, unable to last even a few years? You must know that if you cannot escape from this position, you will be placed in a position far from God's life of goodness.

176

Why Did Jesus Become the Lamb Who Bore the Sins of the World?

Although you yourselves are precious, before you think of your own precious value, you must first recognize the precious value of God, liberate God, and take responsibility on this earth for establishing the protagonist of Heaven's freedom. If such a protagonist emerges, he or she cannot help but become the unparalleled, top-tier bride before Jesus.
Now, you must fight, transcending time and place, to find and establish the standard of God's internal love. And you must know how to feel a heart of love that wants to give something to others, centering on eternity. Also, in dealing with that true protagonist, you must not stop at just one moment.
Today, around us, there are many people who live for one day's freedom and one day's joy, but you must firmly establish the standard of eternally unchanging joy and freedom on the foundation of your heart. Only when you establish that standard can you participate in eternal life. Only when you achieve not just a standard of eternal life and a one-sided environment, but a four-directional environment, will the love of the Holy Spirit, the love of the Holy Son, and the love of the Holy Father reach you.

The Reason Jesus Took Responsibility for the Sins of the World

What is the reason Jesus took on our own sins and the sins of the world? First, it is for the glory of God. Next, it is for the life of God and the love of God. And it is to share joys and sorrows with you for eternity as the protagonist of humanity, the protagonist of freedom, the protagonist of life, the protagonist of love, and the mediator of harmony.
Therefore, if we believe in and follow Jesus, we will receive the glory of God even while on earth, and we will be able to fulfill God's ideal of creation. And when the ideal of creation is fulfilled through you, God Himself will bless and love you, saying, "You are the eternal victor who has overcome Satan."
<Prayer> Loving Father! We did not know that there were so many gates we had to pass through when Heaven proclaimed such an earnest heart. Today,

Please look into the hearts of the beloved children gathered here today and give them strength. Please strike their bodies.

Let Us Participate in the Glory that God Recognizes

Matthew 11:25-30
<Prayer (I)> Loving Father! Please personally guide your children gathered here. Please do not let them be ones who do not know whether the life they have is truly the life they ought to have. Please do not let them be ones who, having received the great grace you have permitted, do not know how to leave it for the sake of the nation.
Loving Father! On this day, a small group that was walking a lonely path has come to this place and prostrated themselves before you, Father. Please allow them to become one in your love, and please allow your hand of love, which seeks for humanity, to become entangled with us in this one place that represents the 6,000-year history. Thus, connecting heart to heart and body to body, please allow all of us to become one.
The grace of your permission was not our grace alone, but the grace of the whole. Please allow this grace to become a grace that can extend through the nation to all the 2.4 billion people of the world. O Father! Please become the center of our lives, the center of our love, and the center of our hope, and may your hand of grace, which is full, be with us upon our heads forever from this hour. Loving Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.
Father! I know that many people are worshiping you on this day. Wherever they gather, may your hand of love be with them.

Please allow their gathered forms to prostrate themselves before the Father's deep heart on behalf of their entire gathering.
Please convey and reveal your hidden love before them. My Father, I earnestly hope and desire that you will permit the grace of your power at this hour.
On this day, we offer our hearts as they are before the Father's altar. Please remove all unfitting elements, and allow us to be filled only with a heart that can sing of the Father's holiness and a heart of gratitude. My Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.
Thus, among your beloved children who have gathered, let there not be a single life that is not fitting before the Father. If there are sons and daughters who have the mark of sin centered on themselves, O Father! Please reveal the flame-like work of the Holy Spirit so that this may be a time when those who have the traces of sin feel shame and can repent on their own. Thus, please allow us to be remolded into meek and humble offerings that can be offered before the perfect Father on behalf of the people of the four seas. Loving Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.
Father, there are also family members who could not attend on this day. Wherever they may be, please work with the same grace, and please bless the lonely denominations that gather in various places and cry out on behalf of the nation and on behalf of the providence. Father! Through their holy hands, please allow the flames of the beacon to appear before this people, and through those who adore you, Father, please allow your holy will to appear as a joyous will before the entire world. Loving Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.
I have entrusted this entire hour to you. Please let the Holy Trinity preside over it. I have prayed in the name of the Lord, earnestly hoping. Amen.
<Prayer (II)> Please hasten the work of judgment upon the earth. Today,

180

Let Us Participate in the Glory that God Recognizes

Beloved brothers and sisters gathered here, may the Father alone protect you, and may the Father alone take charge and guide you. Please allow this one hour, at least, to be a time when there is nothing centered on myself.
Please allow this to be a time when I know that my life is not my own, my knowledge is not my own, and all my concepts are not my own. As something entrusted to you, please allow me to move when Heaven moves and to be still when Heaven is still.
Father, there are brothers and sisters who have remaining wounds and are pierced by a thirsty heart. O Father, who knows their situation and their circumstances, please allow the flames of eternal life descending from Heaven to be lit in their bodies and minds. Please allow this one hour to be a time when they can return the joy of resuscitation to the Father.
Please allow them to know that no matter how great any worldly concept may be, it cannot compare to the heavenly law, and let them know that the ignorance of the world has permeated this earth, and let them know that the shadow of that sin is connected to the entire world.
Thus, please allow this to be a time when they can realize their own shortcomings, be moved by the movement of the heavenly law, and feel a sense of awe for the whole. Loving Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.

<Sermon> The title of the sermon I would like to give today is Let Us Participate in the Glory that God Recognizes.

I will speak on this topic.
To Be Recognized
Because John the Baptist, who was to testify to the will of Heaven, failed to fulfill his mission before the world, Jesus had to stand at a difficult gateway to fight against Satan. The people of Israel, who should have understood Jesus' situation, failed to do so. While Satan was in a position to hasten the difficult path of suffering that lay before Jesus, Jesus stood alone in a position where no being in all of heaven and earth recognized him, and he tried to convey the will of Heaven to a people who did not know it.
Jesus, feeling the mission to convey what he knew internally to the ignorant people, stood himself before all people and, relying on the one heart that only God recognized, he stepped forward to proclaim a new resolution, a new hope, and a new determination before the nation. Today's sermon is an important one with this content.
A person's happiness comes when he has someone who recognizes him. Furthermore, if he has a friend, a comrade, or a teacher who recognizes his past, his present, and even his future, he will be happy.
And the foundation of a person's rest is formed centering on the embrace of such people, and it is through the environment where such people are that one can feel joy and happiness.
Jesus knew that God in Heaven knew him through history, knew him through his thirty years of life, and knew him through the will of the eternal providence.

184

Let Us Participate in the Glory that God Recognizes

He knew this.
Just as God recognized him, Jesus had to recognize all humankind in the human world through history, through their lives, and through the future. As Jesus, who knew this, felt more and more that he himself was the central being who had to make God known to human beings, he had to testify to God's knowing in some form before the nation.
Jesus, Who Had to Testify to the Nation of God's Recognition
What Jesus first sought to testify was that he was the representative being of a relationship with the providential course of 4,000 years before the will of God, a relationship that could never be severed. Jesus, who felt the responsibility to lead the entire nation of Israel to God, just as God had recognized him through the 4,000-year providence, tried to reveal God's knowing to the nation in the course of his life.
Also, when he realized that in the providential course after his thirty years of life, all humankind had to become one with his future ideal, Jesus felt the responsibility to make known to humankind, through his own person, the ideal world where humankind would recognize him from Heaven.
When thinking about the providential history that extends from the past to the present, from the present to the eternal heavenly world to be fulfilled in the future, the affairs of the earth, and how any existing being, through an infinite period, reaches the one person of Jesus, it was not Jesus' mission alone to make this providence known before Heaven, nor was it his mission alone to make it known before the tens of thousands of saints, nor was it his mission alone to make it known before the historical ancestors.
Jesus, who stood before the will on behalf of the whole, had to recognize the nation on behalf of God, just as God recognized him. He had to let the nation know that just as he represented God, the nation had to represent him. And unless a relationship was formed in which the nation recognized Jesus just as he recognized God, Jesus could not feel the happiness of knowing in his lifetime. You must understand that Jesus could rejoice with God toward Heaven, but he could not help but stand in a position where he could not rejoice toward the earth because people did not recognize him.

185

The words Jesus spoke were not just asking people to recognize Heaven. The gospel he preached was not a gospel for Heaven alone. His words, his labors, and all his difficult battles were for the historical nation and for the future nation that would lead history. However, the people of that time who faced Jesus did not know this fact. If the people on earth had recognized Jesus as he knew God, his life would not have been so entangled with sorrow.
To What Extent God and Jesus Recognized Each Other
Then, to what extent did God recognize Jesus? How did God recognize Jesus? From the origin of the history of creation, through the course of human history, through the ties of history, to the entire real society of that time, and furthermore, He recognized even Jesus' future ideal.
Jesus, who appeared before the ignorant people, received Heaven's command and labored, setting himself up. And he fought, pierced by the sorrowful heart of God who had labored infinitely in the course of history. He also sought to comfort the ancestors who had labored in the course of history and to resolve the sorrow that lingered in the course of history. God established Jesus as such a being.
Jesus had a heart for God, and he had a sorrowful heart that wanted to convey that heart to human beings. As long as this sorrowful heart remained in Jesus, God's heart in dealing with Jesus could not help but be sorrowful. We must know that because human beings failed to fulfill their responsibility, God is in sorrow and sadness.
Then, to what extent did God know Jesus? God knew Jesus as the one who could reveal the glory of the children to the whole world through the ideal of the bridegroom and bride centered on Adam's family.

186

Let Us Participate in the Glory that God Recognizes

Then, how much did Jesus know God? While knowing that God recognized him as a being who represented history, Jesus also knew that God wanted to reveal on earth, through him, the faith of the bridegroom and bride from the family life centered on Mary to the course of his real life, and even to reveal the glory of goodness on earth. That is why his words were words that resolved the resentment of history.
Jesus knew that God knew Mary's obedience. He also knew that God knew Mary's situation. He knew that God wanted the faith of the bridegroom and bride, who had to lay the foundation for their start from a position lower than anyone else. He also knew the fact that God wanted the expectation of goodness from among the myriad creations. If human beings had recognized Jesus' knowledge of God in this way, they could have formed a relationship with the will of love that Jesus had, but the human beings of that time did not know that.
Therefore, Jesus could consult with God, but he became unable to consult with people. Since there was no one to whom he could make known his knowledge, his resentful heart, and the providence of salvation on earth, you must know that Jesus' sorrow was greater than the sorrow of losing the whole world.
Love is Completed Through Three Ages
If love is not completed in one generation, it goes through three ages. First, it goes through the love of Heaven's law, then the love of parents, and then the love of husband and wife. We are going through the course of restoration like this because of the fall and the repeated mistakes of human beings.
Therefore, the period until one becomes an adult in one's lifetime is the period of receiving parental love. After that period, the period of love centered on oneself is the period of the bridegroom and bride. After that comes the period of love for one's children.
Then, in God's 6,000-year history of providence, what kind of period of love was it until Jesus came? It was a period when God, by putting Jesus forward, personally gave love as a parent. After that, the period when Jesus leaves the realm of parental love and builds his own family life is the period of the bridegroom and bride.

187

Then what kind of period is to come now? It is the period of concluding the ideal of the bridegroom and bride on earth. Thus, on earth, Jesus, centering on the internal will of God, must unfold the family-level expectation on earth. To do so, he must first unfold the life of the spiritual bridegroom and bride on earth. He must unfold the spiritual heavenly family life on earth and form a family type that represents history on the earth.
After the 2,000-year history since Jesus, heaven and earth must now unite, the internal form and the external form must be connected to form one substance, and a relationship must be formed with it. You must become the children of new parents, centering on yourselves. In the period of the parents, you must be able to raise new children. And through those new children, you must establish the new ideal of the bridegroom and bride on earth. This ideal remains in the course of history.
The Purpose for Which Jesus Came
Then, what was the purpose for which Jesus came? It was to bring to a total conclusion the internal family form, the external ideal of the bridegroom and bride, and the life of the children. Not only on the external foundation, but by concluding the relative standard through the connection of the internal and external, the fortune of Heaven's law can go through the course of restoration of the historical family form, which can establish a standard from the internal for anyone. Through anyone, not only as a real and historical fact but as a decisive fact, you must establish the family life form up to the time God established Jesus.
If you yourselves do not possess the evidential content of the bridegroom and bride of the course of the 2,000-year providence centered on the New Testament, you will not be able to confidently seek out the standard of the bridegroom and bride.
You must leave on earth a substantial child of goodness who can exist eternally and really, not a child of shame, but a child who has completely escaped the history of sin.

<Sermon> At this time, I will speak on the title, "Let Us Manifest the Value of Restoration," centering on the words of Acts 1:6 and below.

Jesus Who Came with the Mission of World Restoration

Where is God's purpose in trying to save fallen human beings? As you well know, it is to restore to human beings their original state of creation. Numerous prophets and sages who first realized God's will have come through each era, taking responsibility for this purpose of restoration and striving toward this one goal to fulfill that will. That is, the 4,000-year history before Jesus came was such a history, the course of Jesus' 30-odd years of life on this earth was a course to fulfill that purpose, and the history of struggle with the Holy Spirit for 2,000 years after his death was also a course of struggle to fulfill this one purpose.

The purpose for which Jesus came to this earth was for the restoration of history, and



Let Us Manifest the Value of Restoration


he came with the mission of his own restoration and, furthermore, the restoration of the world. Therefore, the words of the gospel that Jesus spoke when he came to this earth were words to restore the history of Israel in the past, words to restore his own 30-odd years of life, and furthermore, words to restore all of humanity.

For this reason, until today, human beings have been going through the course of history, sharing in the providence of restoration through the words that Jesus left behind.

Furthermore, today, centering on the words of the New Testament that Jesus gave 2,000 years ago, you must take on the form of a loyal subject who can pay indemnity for the past 6,000 years of history and represent the eternal life to come, and find the victorious value that can restore your own self, restore history, and restore the future. If you cannot do so, the words of the gospel that Jesus Christ left as words of life to restore all people and as the gospel that represented the 4,000 years of history and his own 30-odd years of life when he came to this earth will not bear any fruit.

Today, you must become children who can resolve the resentment of Jesus, who represented the 4,000 years of history, and you must become children who complete the mission of Jesus' own restoration, who sought to establish a new ideology of restoration before all people through his 30-odd years of life and build a victorious foundation for heaven, and the mission for which he toiled for 2,000 years with the Holy Spirit.

Thus, you must return the glorious restoration of victory to Father from the position of representing history, and you must return glory to Father with a value greater than the value of Jesus' entire life, who went through a victorious life.

Furthermore, just as Jesus has been carrying out the 2,000-year history of the providence of salvation by proclaiming the new words of the gospel, today you must receive new words from heaven again, conclude the great work of the entire restoration, and leave it for all generations to come. You must not forget for a moment that this mission remains for you today.

Did Jesus himself carry out his work by revealing everything before human beings to accomplish God's history of restoration?



No, he did not. We know well through the Principle that until now, Jesus has been carrying out the history of restoration without being able to reveal the concrete content of the providence of restoration.

He has been carrying out the history of restoration to fulfill the will of heaven on this earth through symbolic words of testimony while hiding himself, and he has been carrying out the history of the providence of restoration without revealing all of heaven's glory before human beings. Therefore, we must know the inner heart of Jesus, who promoted the history of restoration without clearly revealing the concrete content of the providence.

The Reason Jesus Could Not Express His Inner Heart

Then, what must you know today to possess the glory of restoration?

First, through your life, you must know the hidden value of restoration that Jesus could not reveal, and next, through your heart, you must know the hidden value of restoration that Jesus could not reveal. Then, you must know the hidden content of the restoration of Jesus, who could not reveal the value of eternal life.

And what must we know when God intends to complete the glory of restoration on behalf of the heavenly law?

We must know what content Jesus kept hidden deep in his heart during his 30-odd years of life and could not speak of or reveal to all people.

If you do not know this content, you will not be able to manifest the value of the entire restoration, representing heaven and earth, from the earth to the heavens.

If we look at the words of the gospel that Jesus revealed today, there is no concrete content of Jesus' life in them. Then, what did Jesus allude to? He alluded to one aspect of his hidden life through a life of service. That is, although he was a son of glory who could be exalted,



Let Us Manifest the Value of Restoration


he lowered his glorious self and entered under the feet of many sinners to serve, thereby revealing one hidden aspect. Also, Jesus revealed a hidden aspect in his heart that he could not tell anyone through a life of silence.

Jesus could not express his inner heart even to his twelve disciples who followed him.

Then why could Jesus not reveal such a secret? It was because Jesus knew that even if he had a heavenly secret in his heart, if he revealed it when there was no one to understand it, he would be played with by Satan, so he could not reveal it. That is, although Jesus had a sad and anxious heart to keep what he had learned from the Father to himself and transfer it to human beings, because there was no one to understand and listen to his heart, he could not reveal the heavenly secret to human beings, and he could not reveal the hidden aspect of his heart to human beings.

Thus, Jesus went to the pinnacle of the cross and was interrogated under the charge of being the self-proclaimed king of the Jews before the teachers of the law and Pilate. At that time, Jesus remained silent, and only when Pilate asked, "Are you the king of the Jews?" did he finally reveal himself.

The good and righteous people on heaven's side should have known it as the glory of their lives to worship Jesus as their king, but Jesus was interrogated in the name of a prisoner before Pilate. When he was thus interrogated by Satan in an unavoidable position, he opened his mouth, which had been silent in a position representing God's sorrow, and confessed the truth as it was.
When we see this, we can know that no matter how much it is the history of heaven, if Satan reveals the facts about the heavenly side and questions them, the heavenly side cannot but reveal its hidden heart, and also on Satan's side, if the saints on God's side expose the hidden secret heart of Satan, they cannot but reveal it and report it directly.

Jesus, having in himself the content of restoration that he could not reveal to anyone, not only promoted the providence of the heavenly law through silent service in his daily life, but also showed the hidden content of restoration by standing in the position of a pioneer more than anyone else in its practical aspect. Therefore, you must be people who can break through the heart of Jesus, which can represent this ideology of restoration, and question, "Isn't your heart like this?"

You must know the secret of the hidden providence with the help of the Holy Spirit

If such a person does not appear, you must know for sure that the secret of the providence hidden in Jesus' heart cannot be revealed on this earth, no matter how much history passes.

And today, you must know the secret of the restoration that Jesus revealed through his life, and you must know the content of the restoration in his heart. Only then can you stand confidently before God and confidently before Satan, that is, you can become one who has completed the restoration of a victorious life.

Jesus indemnified 4,000 years of history through his 30-odd years of life and completed the center of restoration on behalf of all things in heaven and on earth. However, until today, there has been no one who could inherit the completed value of Jesus, that is, the secret of the heart that Jesus held and the value of Jesus' unknown life.

So, who appeared with the internal secret and life secret of Jesus instead? It was the Holy Spirit.

Today, you believe in the words of Jesus' gospel, but you cannot be restored by believing in the words themselves. What is needed there is that the Holy Spirit cooperates with my life and lives with me.

Therefore, just as Jesus went through the course of sacrificial service, you too must go through such a course to the peak of the cross, and only then will the life secret that Jesus had hidden be revealed through Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Also, the internal secret that he had in his heart is revealed in that way.

Let's reveal the value of restoration

In this way, today, with the help of the Holy Spirit, we are in the important process of fulfilling the content of the restoration that was hidden in the life aspect of Jesus and the content of the restoration that was hidden in his heart. Therefore, we who are in such a process must have a standard of forming a trinity centered on Jesus, with the Holy Spirit and I becoming one, just as Jesus and the Holy Spirit became one, in order to create a flat foundation for God's victorious foothold on this earth.

There is still a hidden part of life that God has not revealed through Jesus and the Holy Spirit.

What we need

Then, what state are you in today? You have a heart that wants to love Jesus, but you are not loving him properly. Then, what is needed for us now, who are heading toward the purpose of the providence of life restoration and growth restoration through the course of Jesus' 3-year public life, the course of the cross, and the course of cooperation in which Jesus and the Holy Spirit have worked together for 2,000 years since his ascension? If you cannot become like that, you cannot have a relationship with God's love that can complete the value of the entire life and glory by completing the life restoration, heart restoration, and life restoration.

To have a relationship of love with God

<Sermon> The title of the sermon I would like to give at this time is "Let Us Find and Offer God's Eternal Ideal." I will speak for a short while under this title, "Let Us Find and Offer God's Eternal Ideal."

God's Ideal of Creation
When God Himself began the history of creation on this dark earth, the one standard He established was to establish the ideal form remaining in His own internal heart as one eternal, substantial being. Thus, you are well aware that He began the work of creation to establish this one substantial being and, while feeling that eternal joy, to live with one relative ideal, not two.
Among the created beings that God made through the toil of creation, He established one human being as the center of all ideals. However, because that one person came to stand in a position contrary to the hope that God originally demanded, a long history has passed since then, but they have become human beings who have no relationship with the ideal that God desired.
The historical course of seeking out that person again to achieve that one ideal was the course of providence, the course of salvation, and the course of pioneering.
The one ideal that God hoped for in His internal heart was an ideal that would extend to the whole of all creation, but because of the mistake of one person, that ideal could no longer be found in the whole of creation.
Therefore, what is the one central will that God has been trying to find by establishing the will of providence through the history of pioneering and the history of salvation until now? It is to establish a person and realize the ideal that He longed for in His internal heart, so that not only God Himself may enjoy it, but also that He desires to make that ideal of enjoyment the eternal ideal of human beings and return it as a condition of glory. God is working for this.
Therefore, we must now know that God in heaven is calling each one of you. God in heaven has been toiling until now, hoping that you yourselves will become a central body that realizes His ideal.
However, the ideal that God desires cannot be realized as long as we are in the realm of imperfection, as long as we cannot distinguish between God's will, human will, and Satan's will.
Whether you look to the left or to the right, or up or down, what must be accomplished is God's ideal. Therefore, you are well aware through the Principle that the multitude belonging to the left and the multitude belonging to the right, as well as all beings on earth and even the countless saints in heaven, are unknowingly admiring that one ideal.
On what day will God's new ideal of light appear in this dark world? What hour will that one hour be? When will that time be? While asking this, countless sages and wise men have unknowingly continued to pioneer that unknown path until today.
Therefore, now, after you have passed through the heart of God's bright ideal, you must possess the element of an unchanging, eternal ideal, so that you can say to them, "This is the hope that your heart longed for, and this is the ideal that you were aiming for." Thus, you must establish a foundation of joy that is realized through your heart, through your body, and through your environment. If you cannot establish such a foundation of joy, God's ideal cannot be found and established in the created world.

The Realization of God's Ideal and Human Responsibility
Then, where is the most important problem here? It is not in the created things that were made, nor is it in the spirit world. Also, it is not in the angels in heaven, but in you yourselves, who are the center of the whole, the one standard, the one core, and the protagonists of all things. Therefore, you must know that you yourselves are the center and the standard that determines God's ideal.
We must keep in mind that the joy of the one day when that one standard point, that one central point, appears in this world, which is oppressed by death, is our hope as we go through the historical course today, and it is the will of God's providence as He fights against numerous evil spirits.
Therefore, if I am now to live with a heart that admires God's ideal, I must first establish a self that can be in sympathy and harmony with God's internal heart. Thus, just as nature moves according to the law, our own hearts must move centered on the heavenly heart. And you must know that unless you establish a center of the heart that can connect this to the universal end point of heaven, God's eternal ideal cannot have an eternal relationship with the created world.

Let Us Find and Offer God's Eternal Ideal

Then, when we consider our own hearts and bodies, is there a wall that blocks the way between our hearts and heaven? Is there a wall that blocks the way between my heart and my body? Is there a wall that blocks the way between my body and all things? As long as there is such a wall, the eternal ideal of God has already broken its relationship with you.
Now we must open the doors of our hearts and remove all the sins of our bodies to establish a standard by which we can be in harmony. Thus, we must face God and achieve His ideal by receiving the natural gift of being unable not to feel the heavenly nature and unable not to act upon it.
However, because fallen human beings are at a great distance from that one standard, there is a history of toil to pull them up to that standard, and that is the history of the providence of restoration. We must deeply keep in mind that the history of providence to achieve that will is the history that has been led by sending prophets and saints until now.
Now, you must simply go forward. To do so, you must first possess the value of the body, which was created to symbolize all things, and the value of the heart, which was created as the center of the body on behalf of the heavenly nature. Thus, the internal heart of God, who is the center of all creation, the internal heart of God that springs from the heart of the center of the whole, must be able to appear as a single movement through our hearts, through our bodies, through the stage of our lives, and even to all things in the universe. We must accomplish all these things in our one body.

God and Human Relationship and Satan's Goal of Activity
God has worked for 6,000 years to pull human beings, who fell from God's dominion due to the fall, up to their original position. What was that history like? God created all things as a symbolic substantial object according to the principle of creation, and He created human beings as a figurative substantial object. Therefore, as long as such a single existent being is the ideal standard of our hearts, we have a relationship of oneness, not two, that cannot be separated from God.
Who is the being that blocks the relationships that human beings have and cuts off the path of connection? It is Satan, your enemy, the one you must fight against to establish an eternal victorious bond and bring him to natural subjugation. However, as long as God's ideal garden is not realized today or tomorrow, and as long as the ideal of hope that God desired is not realized throughout the entire cosmos through my mind and body, that Satan will not be eliminated.

However, God has an ideal for our minds, an ideal for our bodies, and an ideal for all things. But Satan is fighting against this. Therefore, a day of hope must appear when we can take responsibility for and subjugate Satan on a worldwide level.

Because there is a condition established by that one Satan, God's ideal has no relationship with us until it is removed. That is why God established a master who could stand against Satan and be victorious in order to realize His own ideal, and that person was Jesus Christ.

However, today the gate that connects from all things to the body, from the body to the mind, and from the mind to the heavens is blocked. The ones who have been carrying out the history of breaking through and connecting the blocked gates of this demanding mind and body, and of the demanding counterpart, are Jesus and the Holy Spirit.

Then, what was the unchanging purpose for which Jesus came to this earth? It was to realize God's ideal, no matter what. First was to restore the human mind and restore the body, and then to restore the world of all things. Jesus came with this overall ideology and overall ideal, but because the chosen people of Israel did not believe, he established only the mind-centered ideal, representing God's mind-like character, and departed.

Therefore, we must know the life and history of Jesus until the time when that mind-centered ideal, that is, the spiritual ideal, is established.

Then, what should we, who are now seeking and trying to realize God's ideal, have today? We must have God's eternal elements. This is because even though the times and ages may change, God's eternal substance does not change.

Now, you must fight today, you must fight tomorrow, and you must fight by dedicating your lives until the day you make that eternal ideal that God desires your own.

Faith, Hope, Love, and Life Established by Jesus

Jesus came to this earth and fought to establish eternal faith on behalf of the unbelieving people of Israel in seeking God's eternal ideal. Throughout the course of history, numerous people have come forward believing in God. However, the limit of their hope and faith was confined to their own individuals. But Jesus alone did not establish faith and hope as his own faith and hope. As long as it was established as God's eternal ideal, he dedicated his life to establishing a faith that could be equipped with the elements of that ideal, that is, eternal faith.

What was the one center that Jesus desired throughout his thirty-some years of life? Until that time, in the 4,000-year course of history, numerous prophets and saints had established standards of faith, but their faith did not go beyond national limits and did not go beyond worldwide limits. Therefore, the center of his life was to go beyond such standards and to realize God's eternal ideal, to establish eternal faith.

Therefore, Jesus' faith was not for the purpose of his own salvation. His own salvation was not the purpose, nor was it the purpose to save only this earth. He knew the heart of God who has been providentially guiding everything from the origin of history, through its course, and to a certain end point in the future, and he intended to restore all of it.

Also, in order to find and establish God's eternal ideal, Jesus first fought with Satan to establish an eternal standard, an eternally unchanging standard, that was unprecedented in history. Because he was such a Jesus, you must know that he was able to establish the condition of eternal faith before God who was seeking the eternal ideal.

Therefore, if you want to hold on to Jesus, you must first know that the will of the entire historical human race is involved in the one person of Jesus. He was the only one who could integrate the faith of the numerous believers in the 4,000-year course of history, or the faith of all humankind at that time. Not only that, but he was the one who came with a single standard, an eternally unchanging center, that could represent the future history for all ages and integrate the faith of all humankind.

Therefore, we must follow the example of Jesus' faith. And you must know that Jesus was the one who spent his thirty-some years on this earth to establish a foothold of an eternally unchanging, firm faith, a standard of God's eternal hope, transcending the individual, transcending society, transcending the nation, transcending the world, and transcending the cosmos. When we believe in Jesus, we must resemble the Jesus who established the standard of eternal faith, which was unprecedented in history.

Next, we must inherit Jesus' hope. Jesus' hope was not his own personal hope. It was a hope that absorbed all the hopes that numerous ancestors of all ages had long hoped for. He also possessed a hope that represented the eternal hope of God that pervaded heaven and earth. Thus, you must know that Jesus was able to represent our hope because he established the center of hope that could realize God's eternal ideal, which no one in history had ever had.

That is not all. Jesus established faith toward heaven, was equipped with hope, and was equipped with the bond of life and the bond of love. Thus, he went through a course of struggle for thirty-some years to establish his hope as an eternal hope and his life as an eternal life.

However, the reason Jesus felt the value of life in the course of his life was because he received the eternal life element of God, who exists eternally and is the center of life, representing the entire created world. Because Jesus was the owner of this eternal life, no action of Satan's power could reach him. Also, the love that Jesus established was not a love that could remain within the limited sphere centered on oneself, like the love that people have today. It was an unchanging love that could die to realize the eternal ideal of God. Therefore, at that time, Jesus' heart of loving God in heaven could represent all people. You must know that Jesus possessed a heart of unchanging love, representing God's mind-centered eternal ideal and all the people of the universe, for the first time in heaven and on earth.

Right Faith in Jesus

Today, we are inheriting the will of the providence that Jesus established with faith, hope, life, and love. We must realize the will of salvation that was established through such a course of toil. We must also follow the example of the course in which he set a standard of redemption by burning his own body with the shield of the cross.

<014217>

Furthermore, we who are in a limited sphere today must think about the life of Jesus who spent thirty-some years sorrowfully, longing for not only faith in the infinite God, but also the infinite God's hope, the infinite God's life, and the infinite God's love. You must know the fact that Jesus, the protagonist of the whole universe, the savior of all people, and the master of the earth, fought with his life at stake to establish the conditions to fulfill God's eternal ideal in all of hope and faith, life, and love.

And you must look at all things with such a heart of Jesus, and you must experience the same feelings that Jesus felt. You must also know that Jesus was one who fought while admiring such aspirations, such hope, and such an ideal. You should not just vaguely think of him as a historical figure who came and went 2,000 years ago. You must feel him as the Jesus who is in your heart and who is walking with you in your daily life today. You must once again re-recognize the life-giving element that can realize the eternal ideal of God. Thus, your faith must be comparable to Jesus' faith, your hope must be comparable to Jesus' great hope, and your life and love must also be comparable to those of Jesus.

You must follow the example of the center of Jesus, which represented all the ideal elements of God. You must inherit and fulfill the central heart with which Jesus fought to establish all of them, whether by faith, by hope, by life, or by love. If there is no one to fulfill that will, the will that Jesus came to this earth to fulfill but could not, due to his death on the cross, cannot be fulfilled. Because the course that Jesus could not walk remains, the will of the providence resides in our daily lives today.

Therefore, we must try to feel the character of Jesus through our bodies and try to feel the character of Jesus through all things. Thus, the character of Jesus and our character must unite and be able to conform to the eternal ideal of God that represents the entire cosmos.

Now, you must know what Jesus' death on the cross foretold.

<014218>

Let Us Find and Offer God's Eternal Ideal

That hill of the cross was a cross that accomplished eternal faith, a cross that made us experience and admonished us about God's eternal hope, and a cross that admonished us to also have God's eternal life and eternal love. And you must know that the way of salvation left behind through the history of redemption by the cross becomes a condition that can pass on to us Jesus' eternal faith, eternal hope, eternal life, and eternal love.

However, because the faith of Jesus, who came on behalf of all the people of the universe, did not appear in its entirety, that is, because the hope that he had hoped for on behalf of all humankind was not realized on a worldwide level, Jesus made a resentful appeal on the cross. It was the same with life and love. If at that time the faith that Jesus desired, the hope that Jesus desired, the life that Jesus desired, and the love that Jesus desired could have appeared, there would have been no resentful appeal on the cross.

What to Equip Through the Cross

Therefore, what is it that we must now equip ourselves with through the cross? We must have the eternal faith that Jesus Christ embraced, the eternal hope that Jesus Christ possessed, the eternal life that Jesus Christ lived, and the eternal love that Jesus Christ longed for. Today, we must not just attribute the eternal faith, eternal hope, eternal life, and eternal love established before the cross to Jesus alone.

We must carry his cross and possess his eternal faith as my faith, his eternal hope as my hope, and his eternal life and love as my life and love. Furthermore, we must have the elements of God's ideal that Jesus passed on, even while carrying the cross for humankind. Next, just as Jesus had a chief disciple to whom he could pass on eternal faith, eternal hope, eternal life, and eternal love, we must also have such a person.

<014219>

If the condition remains that the faith received from Jesus, the hope received from Jesus, and the life and love received from Jesus could not be fulfilled because of you, they will appear as conditions of judgment against you in the last days.

In the last days, God will come to you and the eternal will that Jesus Christ left behind will...
He will ask if you have paid the debt of faith of resentment. He will ask if you have paid the debt of hope, the debt of life, and the debt of love that Jesus Christ left behind. When you find yourselves in that position, you must do as Jesus Christ did when he said on the cross, "It is finished." Today, before Jesus Christ, we must be able to say, "I have fulfilled in my own body the eternal inheritance of God that you left behind." You must know that unless such a person appears on this earth, the ultimate will of God's providence cannot be completed.

In the 4,000-year course of history, Jesus established the central element that the eternal God had envisioned. Jesus and the Holy Spirit have been working until today to expand the spiritual and internal conditions of salvation to a global standard. Therefore, if we today fail to establish the eternal faith, hope, life, and love that can externally fulfill the internal ideal element of the eternal God, the 2,000-year providential will of Jesus Christ will come to nothing. You must know this.

Now you have entered the course of faith, seeking to feel God's heart by following Jesus' example. However, you must reflect on how much you believe. Are you perhaps believing within the realm of your own assertions, established by your own personal concepts? If there is a difference compared to the faith of Jesus Christ, who represented the entire cosmos, that difference will become a condition for judgment at the end of days.

What kind of hope do you have today? The hope you have conceptually is a hope for yourselves. You must testify to the hope of Jesus Christ as your hope. Thus, you must have the hope of Jesus Christ, which went beyond himself and represented God's eternal ideal.

220

Let Us Find God's Eternal Ideal

However, you must know that if your hope differs from the hope of Jesus Christ, that difference will become a condition for judgment at the end of days.

The same is true of life. If we have received life by believing in Jesus today, that life is not for our own survival. It is a life that must restore this nation and bring harmony to the tens of thousands of saints. It is a life that can represent the calm and composed heart of Jesus Christ, who represented God's eternity in the face of the cross and Satan's attacks.

Even when he was in the position of his life being taken on the cross, Jesus did not curse his enemies for their retaliation at all.

Jesus was not the person they thought they knew. He was the one who sought to feel God's eternal love while considering the heart of God who had fought against the enemy for humankind for 4,000 years. When you long for that limitless heart of Jesus, you will feel that it becomes the foundation of your faith.

Therefore, the intensity of Jesus' feeling for Heaven's love was something that could represent God's eternal ideal, which could overcome any criticism and any suffering on earth. You must know the fact that because Jesus stood in such a position, he forgot all about having to go the path of death due to the wrongdoing of his enemies and prayed for humankind.

The Love of the Cross

Today, you who have received God's limitless love and limitless life by believing in Jesus must reflect on what realm that life is in.

Because Jesus knew God's love, that is, the eternal and ideal love of God who created the whole universe and yearned to embrace it, he loved God more than he loved himself, his family, his nation, and the world on this earth.

221

Thus, you should consider that the love of the cross was left behind while feeling the heart that could love humankind and love God, forgetting any difficult things, in order to fulfill the providential will that they could not accomplish, representing all the many prophets and saints who came and went in the course of history, embracing the love of God which is the center of all love.

If there is a judgment at the end of days, when the love of God that flowed from God and was revealed through Jesus Christ reaches you, you must have a foundation of heart in yourselves that can receive that love and keep it eternally. If you do not have such a foundation of heart, you will not be able to stand proudly before God at the time of the final judgment.

Therefore, we must now know that before us lies the great and lofty hope and ideal of Christ. That great and lofty ideal came to appear on earth for the first time through Jesus Christ.

That is why today we believe in Jesus and seek to emulate him.

Even after going to the spirit world, Jesus is fighting against Satan on behalf of the world. In order to fulfill the eternal ideal of God, he is fighting against Satan on our behalf, together with the Holy Spirit and the tens of thousands of angels in heaven.

We must no longer hold the faith that was left to us, the hope that was hoped for us, the life that was demanded of us, and the love that was desired for us as only our love, our life, our hope, and our faith. You must keep in mind that if you hold them as only your own, the eternal ideal of God will have no relationship with you. Beloved Father, please allow us to feel the garden of hope that we long for at this time.
