Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.

Today as well, lonely sons and daughters are scattered in the provinces, fighting with the word, so please be with them there as well. They are building an altar of victory with the spirit that they must fight and win against the final enemies of the 6,000-year history, and they are fighting in obedience to the Father's command for that time when the Father and His sons and daughters can rejoice together. Therefore, Father, please be with them and show Your direct work wherever they stay. I earnestly hope and desire that You will allow it to reach the whole through such an environment.

Now, for this one hour, Father, I earnestly ask You to send down the grace of Your joy and to receive us. I have offered up all my words in prayer in the name of the beloved Lord. Amen.

<Sermon> Today, I would like to speak for a moment on the topic, "Jesus is the Protagonist of the Cosmic Revolution."

God Who Wished for Humankind to Be Completed as the Embodiment of Newness

If you observe the process of something new being created, you can see that it is a revolutionary process. When we look at all the things that were made during the six days, that is, all the creatures from the lowly insects to human beings, God created newer and better beings, and finally, He created human beings. You will all know that the Creator's ideal was that by creating human beings, God would complete His higher internal nature and external form, and that it would have a new and unchanging substance that the Father could eternally be proud of.

In this way, human beings were made as a single form that could be said to be truly beautiful and truly good, representing all things and all creation, and compared to any creature, as the eternal embodiment of newness that God can enjoy. You know that what was made in this way was Adam and Eve, who could have dominion over all things.

They were Adam and Eve, who should have rejoiced in God's original goodness and internal glory through their actual lives. However, because Adam and Eve fell, they did not know that will. Fallen human beings are those who have come to be in a position where they cannot reveal the glory of newness on behalf of all that God created.

However, even though human beings fell, God's will is an unchanging will, and if it is not completed, God cannot maintain His dignity as the Creator and cannot show His authority. Therefore, you know well through the Principle that the history of restoration and the history of salvation are to re-establish this.

Then, when Heaven deals with all things in the universe from this position, when will be the day when a precious being that cannot be found in heaven and on earth, and cannot be found among the creatures, a new embodiment of a higher dimension that can newly reveal the entire character hidden within God, will appear as the protagonist and fulfill God's will? To greet this one moving and shocking day, God has established this one purpose and has been working with ceaseless effort through the providence of restoration until today.

When will that one day come when God will find a new cosmic being after the creation of the world, a being that cannot be exchanged even for all the creatures, and that will allow Him to enjoy a joy that has never existed before? God is eagerly awaiting that one day, that one being.

God has already designed the ideal world of creation where God Himself, human beings, and all things can enjoy, rejoice, and be in harmony together, and He has already conceived of even the ideal aspect of life. Therefore, when we rejoice centered on one protagonist who can rejoice together with the heaven that is made of internal symbols and the earth that is made of external symbols, heaven and earth can rejoice together. You will also know well that Heaven is making efforts to find this one standard.

Then, what is the will that the Father requires?

If there is one single will that cannot be let go of even if all things in heaven and on earth are broken, it is the completed human being. Until a human being is completed, he must become the embodiment of truth through the principled way of creation, but because of the fall, he became an unprincipled embodiment. Therefore, although human beings have the form of a human being, their internal character and external form could not appear as a divided body representing God's eternal substance.

For that reason, fallen human beings have the form of a human being, but they have lost the form of the ideal of creation. God is re-injecting the form of the ideal of creation into these human beings. You also know well the history of Heaven, which is making efforts to find a new embodiment of proof.

Jesus Who Came to Fulfill God's Ideal of Creation

Then, who was the one who came as this one central substance, the being of hope? It was Jesus Christ. God worked for 4,000 years until He sent Jesus Christ.

After the creation, God sent Jesus as a new being with whom He could finally be in harmony, a being that could be shown before all things and all creation. However, human beings did not treat Jesus as the being who was the goal of God's desire, but instead, they once again committed a fallen history of opposing him.

God, who had worked to find the lost standard of goodness, gathered people who were under the accusation of Satan throughout the 4,000-year history and made a national foundation. Therefore, this national foundation should have become a foundation for Jesus, whom God had established as the one protagonist who could represent God and all things and all beings in heaven and on earth. Nevertheless, Jesus went his own way, and the nation went its own way. Here, our mission and God's mission were decided.

You must know the fact that because the Jewish people, who should have embraced Jesus Christ, who was sent as the representative of the whole to re-create the entire universe as a world of newness centered on God, as the protagonist of the whole, failed to do so, Jesus, who had the mission of being the protagonist of the whole, disappeared as Jesus, and the people disappeared as the people, and as a result, God's sorrow was further aggravated.

The words that Jesus himself spoke to the Jewish people at that time and all that he revealed were not for his own will. Whose will was it? It was Heaven's will. Jesus represented the will of God's providence. However, a conflicting debate arose between the people in the realm of the fall, who had to face God's will through Jesus, and Jesus.

The Jewish people at that time did not know that when the word of God appears in this fallen world, if this word appears before a nation, it will be a word that can revolutionize the nation; if it appears to an individual, it will be a word that can revolutionize the individual; if it appears in the world, it will be a word that can revolutionize the world, and also a word that can newly revolutionize heaven and earth.

The people of Israel thought that the law given through Moses for 4,000 years and the covenant made with Jacob could fulfill their ideals and represent the whole. However, God worked to pull them up gradually from the very bottom. The people of Israel did not know that after going through the formation-level Old Testament history, they were going through the history of going through the principled course of the creation of heaven and earth again, going through the growth-level New Testament era to the completion level. Therefore, Jesus' words were words of life that the people of that era could not accept. The people at that time did not know that they were new words that were higher than the Old Testament law, and words for making a connection with a new value that was higher than the conventional one.

What Jesus desired was to fulfill God's entire ideal of creation. Therefore, he came to find it through a continuous revolutionary process to complete the cosmic mission on behalf of heaven and earth. Therefore, you who are in the last days today must know that when Jesus appeared on this earth and went the way of the cosmic will, there was a process of pulling fallen human beings up to their original position, and in that process, there were countless twists and turns of battle and a revolutionary process.

Jesus' Hope and the Unbelief of the Jewish People

Then, to what extent is the hope of this revolutionary Jesus Christ? It is not the kind of hope that you have on this piece of land where you are living today. It is a hope that can be connected beyond the world to the infinite kingdom of God.

This hope is Jesus' hope and at the same time, it is God's hope, who is one with Jesus. Therefore, human beings must know that God placed His hope in Jesus and tried to reveal His will through Jesus.
Then what was the figure of Jesus who appeared before the Jewish people, speaking words and appearing as the substantiation representing God’s entire will? He appeared as the protagonist of a new truth that had never existed in history. Countless people cried out for truth, but it was only truth on an individual level. They may have claimed it to be a truth that could represent nation after nation and all countries, but in reality, it could not become such a truth. Therefore, the one who appeared equipped with a truth that could shine again upon heaven and earth was Jesus Christ. For that reason, the words that Jesus Christ spoke were of the highest value in that age and that world, and they were new and revolutionary.

If the Jewish people, who longed for God’s will, had known these revolutionary words of truth,

Jesus, the Protagonist of a Cosmic Revolution

they would have abandoned their lives up to that point and desired to possess this truth.

Since the one day that the Jewish people, who should have stood in this position, were meant to achieve was broken, we must overcome this. We have the mission to resolve what has been bound. Sacrifice occurs because of the failure to uphold the truth of Jesus Christ.

God established one people and set up a center among that people, intending to reveal His internal heart with words of cosmic truth through that center. However, the people of Israel did not know this fact.

Jesus was to have revealed the words of eternal truth over some thirty years, but due to their disbelief, Jesus was forsaken. For that reason, until the moment they find the substance of the Word, the people of the world must seek the new, cosmic truth that Jesus Christ, on behalf of God’s will and heart, intended to propagate on this earth.

Today, the faithful saints must fulfill the hope of Jesus Christ. The words that Jesus testified should have appeared as national words and also as world-level words in his time. However, because they did not appear as world-level words, Christianity became a religion of suffering.

If the words that Jesus Christ spoke had appeared as the central words that could save the earth at that time, he could have manifested God’s authority. If there had been an individual who followed the individual Jesus, a people who followed the individual Jesus, and a world that followed the individual Jesus, then Jesus, who was responsible for God’s will, would have accomplished that will on this earth. However, there was no such individual, people, or world before Jesus.

And centered on the words of Jesus, the beloved disciples, the beloved family, the beloved denomination, and the beloved nation who were to represent Jesus should have become one with Jesus, experienced God’s heart, and upheld God’s will. However, because they were in a position of dealing with Jesus from their own denominational level with the truth they knew, the words of Jesus went their own way, and they went theirs.

Then what is it that Jesus now asks of you, the saints of the last days? He proclaimed the cosmic truth, hoping that our shameful selves would become cosmic beings.

Jesus came to this earth as an individual, but he was not an ordinary individual; he was one who represented the whole of all creation. He was one who represented the entire truth of the creative principle of the whole world of creation.

What Jesus Asks of Us

Although he came as a being of such value, he could not become the protagonist of value, the protagonist of the universe. That is why you yourselves must accomplish this purpose of cosmic value. Thus, when we believe in Jesus, we ourselves can meet the truth individually through the heart of Jesus. In this way, when you go through a spiritual history and infinite grace descends, you must not know it only as an individual gift. It must pass through being an environmental gift, a denominational gift, and extend to being a worldwide gift. Only then can we return.

When a gift is given to us, we must not think of it as our own gift from a personal perspective. If you have received grace from a personal standpoint and obtained truth through Jesus Christ from a personal standpoint, you must be able to digest it as your own and at the same time take responsibility for this truth and know how to propagate it to the world. If you go forth with the world in this way, it becomes your gift and at the same time the gift of heaven and earth. However, if your view of faith is to save only yourself, you will remain in a personal concept of salvation and end there.

If the grace overflowing in your hearts now remains only as a personal thing, you will commit again the mistake of the Jewish people of old who crucified Jesus Christ.

If the truth I have obtained remains a religion for saving my one life,

Jesus, the Protagonist of a Cosmic Revolution

the hope of Jesus Christ cannot be fulfilled.

The words of Jesus Christ, which are spoken with a central hope that extends through the individual, the family, the society, and the world to the providence of heaven, are to bring about the work of resurrection and rebirth through your personal gifts. The individual, national, state, and worldwide salvation must be done through you.

You must clearly know that individual salvation, national salvation, worldwide salvation, and cosmic salvation remain.

When you give thanks before Heavenly Father, you must know how to offer not only personal thanks but also thanks on the family, social, national, and worldwide levels. Also, if you repent, you must become people who repent from personal repentance to family repentance, national repentance, worldwide repentance, and repentance for heaven and earth.

Now is the time to go beyond the personal concept of salvation, beyond the family concept of salvation, beyond the social and national concept of salvation, and beyond the worldwide concept of salvation. Only then will a worldwide indemnity begin because of you.

If the Jewish people had had a national concept of salvation and had gone as far as a worldwide concept of salvation, Jesus would have saved all humanity through the Jewish people.

The Words of Jesus are the Words of a Cosmic Revolution

The words of the gospel of Jesus Christ, which are the fruit of passing through the course of history, are the words of truth. They were words that could bestow salvation upon you, transcending the entire history and life that your ancestors had passed through. You must realize that these words of Jesus were indeed the words of a cosmic revolution.

When Jesus Christ came to this earth, he raised a standard against all the legalism that had been believed in until then. He proclaimed, “Through me, all the law must see its fulfillment.” Because the people of Israel did not know the meaning of these words of Jesus, which contained a cosmic view of faith, these words of cosmic value, they killed Jesus.

Those words were cosmic words in that age. In terms of love as well, Jesus spoke words of a cosmic revolution.

Jesus said, “He who does not love me more than anyone else is not worthy of me.” And, “If you do not love me more than anyone else, you cannot be my disciple.” Looking at this, we can see that in order to find the truth until a single cosmic whole, which God desired as the ideal of creation, is achieved, one must go through a cosmic course.

What is extremely important in forming relationships between human beings and between human beings and God is cosmic love. However, because human beings could not form a relationship with God with cosmic love, they came to form a relationship with the love of the archangel. Thus, human beings lost the power to break through the gate of love centered on the ideal love with God. To be able to break through this gate of love again, power is needed.

What was the purpose of Jesus saying, “Love me more than anyone else”? It was not for Jesus himself to be loved. It was so that if people believed those words and loved Jesus, Jesus would hold them with a power stronger than the power that held them in the satanic realm, thereby raising them to the position where they could give and receive the original love with God. For that purpose, he said, “Love me more than anyone else.” These words were the words of a prophetic revolution.

In this way, Jesus brought about a revolution of truth, and also, through his death on the cross, he brought about a revolution of heavenly love. This was a love that represented not only the love between individuals, but also family, social, national, and worldwide truth. It was a revolution of love that represented the universe.

However, the love of the world today is a love centered on the self. Or it is a love centered on the nation. Until now, it has been to the extent of loving one’s own country or loving one’s own family. There has been no love that could go beyond the nation, beyond the national sphere.

However, the hope of God and Jesus is not one people, one nation. It is to establish an ideal world where heaven and earth can become one, centered on God. That is why the love that Jesus presented is not a worldly love,

Jesus, the Protagonist of a Cosmic Revolution

a love on the national or state level centered on the self, but a love that goes beyond the world and connects to heaven and earth.

Revolution of Truth, Revolution of Love

Then what was the true path that Jesus established through the words of the gospel? To what extent are you yourselves loving today? Jesus Christ did not stand before the individual. He did not stand before the family or the nation. Therefore, Jesus, the protagonist of cosmic love and the bridegroom, received family persecution and national persecution.

Through Jesus as the origin, all the billions of creatures of heaven and earth, all of creation that had not felt God’s love until then, were to form a relationship of love for the first time. The responsibility to make this relationship possible was on Jesus.

Then what kind of love is the love that Jesus pioneered, found, and established? It is a love that is the complete opposite of worldly love. Human love is, at best, love for one’s country, but the love of Jesus Christ is a cosmic love. That is, it is a love that goes beyond the individual, beyond the people, beyond the nation, beyond the world, and reaches to heaven.

Then what kind of love is God’s love? It is a love that has two aspects. It is not only loving me but also loving even enemies. Therefore, we must become individuals who can love God and at the same time love even our enemies.

What kind of love is the love of Jesus Christ? It is a love that is for the sake of even Satan. Because he knew that God’s love is a love that loves even Satan, Jesus Christ set up this standard and said, “Love your enemies” (Matthew 5:44). Therefore, we must find and establish this standard of cosmic love on this earth. If we cannot accomplish this work by the time we die, we must have the heart to establish this standard even through our descendants.

And now you must live a life of gratitude. You must live a life of gratitude to Christ and to heaven, thinking, “I am living because of the grace and love of Christ, and I am living because of the grace and love of heaven.” It is a grateful thing that I have been saved, but it is also a grateful thing to represent the cosmic mission of Jesus Christ, and it is a grateful thing to live to complete the love of Jesus Christ.

On behalf of the family, on behalf of the clan, embracing the people, you must know the cosmic love with which Jesus Christ forgave and loved his enemies even as he was dying on the cross. And you must know the heart of Jesus who overcame sorrow and looked at his enemies with a heart of love.

When Jesus Christ was dying on the cross, he said, “It is finished” (John 19:30). You must know that until he said those words, Jesus Christ forgot all his own sorrow and his own unfairness and suffered to fulfill the will of heaven. Because the work of finding cosmic life again through his own body was about to be thwarted, Jesus Christ forgot his own pain, forgot his own unfairness, and overcame all kinds of hardships. Therefore, the life of Jesus Christ was not a life to save only himself, but a life to establish the nation of God, not to mention the people and the nation.

Saints of the Last Days Who Must Awaken

Today, you are carrying out a movement to find the life of Jesus Christ, and in the democratic world, a movement is being carried out to resurrect the name of Jesus Christ. A people who have received great grace and bear a great responsibility, or not

예수님 홀로 남게 되었다는 것입니다.

은 개인적인 사랑의 기준, 개인주의를 갖고 살고 있습니다. 옛날의 유대교

니다. 이러한 것이 예수 이후에도 계속되고 있다는 사실을 잘 알아야 하겠
습니다.
이제 우리에게는 하늘땅을 대신할 수 있는 새로운 말씀과 새로운 생명
과 새로운 사랑이 필요합니다. 그런데 이념적인 말씀만 필요한 것이 아니
라 실체화할 수 있는 말씀이 필요한 것입니다.
그러므로 끝날인 오늘날 여러분은 각성해야 되겠습니다. 여러분은 새로
운 진리와 생명과 사랑을 가지고 민족을 구하고 세계를 구하고 하늘땅의
6천년의 원한을 해원해야 되겠습니다. *

희들 오늘, 이 한 성전을 중심삼고 모여 왔사옵나이다. 부복한 저희들의
마음 몸이 하나되어 아버지의 명령을 대신할 수 있게 허락하여 주시옵
소서. 엎드린 저희의 몸이 거룩한 성전이 되지 않으면 안 되겠사옵나이
다.
오랜 기간을 두고 탄식하며 찾아 나온 소망의 모습들이 저희들인 것을
깨닫게 될 때, 아버님은 참으로 불쌍한 자리에 처하여 계심을 알게 되옵니
다. 지금까지 섭리역사를 해 나오시면서 갖은 수모를 받으신 아버지의 사
정도 알게 되옵니다.
갖은 수모를 받으신 아버지이시요, 갖은 고난을 겪으시면서도 소망의 아
들딸을 바라시어 참고 나오신 아버지이신 것을 이 시간 생각하게 될 때,
저희들은 지극히 보잘것없는 것들임을 알게 되옵니다. 하오나 그 뜻 앞에
황공한 마음을 갖고 나왔사옵고, 아버지의 원한을 풀어 드리기 위해 충성
스런 절개를 갖고자 나왔나이다.
그런 연고로 어제도 오늘도 내일도 싸움의 노정을 거쳐가야 할 입장에
놓여 있는 저희들이요, 저희들이 가려는 노정이 오직 아버지의 영광만을
위한 노정인 것을 아버지께서 아실 줄 믿사오니 이 시간 찾아 주시옵소서.

에서 아버지의 명령에 의지하여 이 자리까지 나왔사옵니다. 아버지, 오늘의

시대의 당신의 아들딸들도 불쌍하옵니다.
아버님이시여! 이 시간 염려의 마음을 푸시옵소서. 하늘의 염려가 지극
히 크다는 것을 알고 그 염려를 저희가 대신 붙안고 남아진 복귀의 뜻을
위해 있는 힘을 다하여 싸우기를 원하고 있사오니, 아버님이시여! 저희들
을 보시옵고 위안 받으시옵소서. 민족의 서러움과 교단의 서러움을 저희들
로 말미암아 위로 받으시옵소서.
아버지, 기뻐할 수 있는 한 줄기 생명의 빛을 향하여 나갈 수 있게, 곳
곳에 널려 있는 당신의 아들딸들을 어서 속히 한 곳으로 모으셔서, 승리의
제단과 영광의 제단을, 그리고 의의 제단을 쌓게 허락하여 주시옵소서. 민
족을 통하여, 이 세상 인류를 통하여 아버지의 그 한 뜻을 이루게 허락하
여 주시옵기를, 사랑하는 아버님, 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵나이다.
이 자리에 나온 자녀들 중에 아직까지 사탄의 참소조건에 걸리거나 원
한의 심정을 품고 있는 자녀들이 있사옵니까? 아버님, 그런 자녀들이 없
게 허락하여 주시옵소서. 그런 자녀들이 있다면, 이 시간 능력의 역사로
써, 힘의 역사로써 그들의 마음에 회개할 수 있는 감동의 은사, 부활의 은
사를 이 시간 허락하여 주시옵길, 아버님이시여! 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵
나이다.
남아진 시간을 맡기오니 슬픔을 제하시고 영광으로 저희들을 주관하여
주시옵소서. 당신이 친히 주장할 수 있고 자랑할 수 있는 기쁨의 은사만이
저희들의 머리 위에, 마음 몸에 충만케 허락하여 주시옵길 간절히 바라옵
고 원하옵나이다. 모든 것 맡기었사오니 맡아 주시옵소서. 주의 이름으로
기도하였사옵나이다. 아멘.

<기 도(Ⅲ)> 아버님, 분부하신 말씀에 의해 만민 앞에 넘어야 할 고개
가 남아져 있음을 알게 되옵니다. 오늘날 저희들은 아버지의 완전성 앞에
저희의 불완전성을 제하기 위한 싸움을 해야 할 입장에 있사옵고, 불변의
진리의 원칙 기준을 넘어야 할 운명이 남아 있사옵니다.
이제 만우주 앞에 저희 자신을 내세워야 할 때가 되었사옵고, 완전하신
아버님의 성상을 닮아 피조만물을 주관치 않으면 안 될 역사적인 운명이
저희 각자에게 남아져 있음을 생각하게 될 때, 오늘의 나는 영원하신 아버
지의 탄식을 대신해야 할 나요, 오늘의 나는 영원하신 아버지의 사랑을 증
거해야 할 나요, 오늘의 나는 아버지의 말씀을 어두운 세상에 전파하여 복
귀의 사명을 감당치 않으면 안 될 나임을 알게 되옵니다.
그런데 오늘까지 믿고 나온 저희의 신앙생활은 아버지 앞에 내세울 수
없는 생활이었사오니, 이 시간 스스로 뉘우치는 동시에 회개할 수 있으며
스스로 각성할 수 있게 허락하여 주시옵소서.
이제 저희가 갖고 있는 모든 관념과 주장과 주의를 존엄하신 아버지의
뜻 앞에 내어 놓고 나라는 실존을 완전히 없이 하고, 영원한 실존체인 본
성의 나를 회복하여 완전하신 아버지의 품성을 닮고, 아버지의 영광에 잠
길 수 있는 나를 회복하여야 할 싸움의 노정이 남아 있사오니, 오늘 이 싸
움의 노정에서 퇴보하는 자들이 되지 말게 허락하여 주시옵소서.
하루 하루의 생활을 통하여, 그리고 생애를 통하여 아버지의 즐거움의
영광이 될 수 있고 아버지께서 취하시기에 합당한 아름다운 아들딸들이 되
게 허락하여 주시옵소서. 아버님, 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵나이다.
이때는 복귀의 시기를 반영시키는 때이옵고, 옛날 예수님 당시와 같이
역사적인 심판의 기준을 넘어야 할 시기이옵나이다. 유대교 앞에 새로운
뜻을 제시시키며 요단강가에서의 증거의 역사, 세례를 주던 세례 요한의
역사가 세계적으로 벌어지고 있는 시기인 것을 생각하게 될 때, 세례 요한
의 사명이 후대인 저희들의 사명으로 남아진 것을 알게 되옵니다.
이제 천륜의 안식의 터를 저희 각자들이 갖추어, 세례 요한의 증거함
가운데 예수 그리스도께서 죄와 사탄의 침범이 없는 가운데 아버지 앞에
영광을 돌릴 수 있어야 했던 그 하나의 선의 동산, 저희들이 손에 손을
잡고, 마음에 마음을 합하여 노래 부를 수 있는 하나의 안식의 동산을 건

244

세상 죄를 지고 가신 하나님의 어린양을 보라

설치 않으면 아니 되겠사옵나이다.
이러한 책임을 위하여 오늘 저희들을 불렀사옵고, 이러한 일을 위하여
Having chosen us today, please do not let us become sons and daughters who leave behind sorrow and sadness before the will of your calling.
We know that the resentment of millennia has pervaded history due to the failure of John the Baptist. Now that we have received heaven's calling and heaven's choosing, please allow us today to go before your throne and establish a foundation for the providence that can complete the will of the entire universal providence. Thus, please allow us to fulfill the remaining mission on a complete foundation.
If we are not qualified to bow down before the sacred image of our majestic Father with free hearts and free bodies today, please let us know that we are still filled with the resentment of restoration. When we offer our entire bodies and minds before you and raise our hands to call you Father, O Father! Please hold us with your hand of love and guide us so that we can receive the name of sons and daughters of your glory.
Thus, please allow us to be sons and daughters who can sing of the glory of joy in the garden of delight, sing of the glory of victory of hosanna to the entire universe, and return glory to the coming Lord. I earnestly ask and desire this.
Please allow us to think of Jesus Christ, who came to resolve the sorrow of history, on this day, the day you have permitted. When we realize that the path Jesus Christ walked was not only his path but the model course we must walk in the last days, we cannot help but feel our hearts grow heavy and our bodies submit to our hearts. Please allow us to become your loyal servants who will take on this will, even if we have to struggle on our own before the awesome and precious will. O Father! I earnestly ask and desire that you allow us to become loyal subjects with a heart of devotion to you.
I entrust everything to you, so please allow the heart of the one who speaks and the heart of the one who receives to become one. I fear that Satan will work through the heart of the doubter at this hour, so please first allow that doubt to be broken.
If there is anyone who, without knowing it, is led into darkness because the power of Satan is at work and their heart is not moved by the Lord's commanded word and they are not immersed in the grace of the Holy Spirit, please allow them to repent through the grace of compassion.
Thus, please allow them to be immersed in the ideal of eternal life, pervaded by your love for ages to come. I earnestly ask that at this hour, along with the word, the history of your life, along with the word, the history of your love, and along with the word, the history of your power may appear. I have prayed all these things in the name of the Lord. Amen.
<Sermon> I will speak on the topic, “Behold, the Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world.”
God’s Providential Purpose and the Human Mission
The 4,000-year history from the time of the fall until the coming of Jesus was not a history of goodness but a history of sin. Numerous prophets came to this earth and fought against sin for 4,000 years, upholding the will of the providence, but they could not completely liquidate the remaining sin. Thus, the providence was extended for 4,000 years through repeated failures in the fight against sin.
The purpose of God’s providence is to completely liquidate this sin. Therefore, until the day this sin is completely liquidated, the history of struggle cannot be stopped, and the history of restoration cannot be stopped. And God has no choice but to send his beloved children as workers of the providence.
Therefore, to fulfill his will, God established Noah’s family in place of the fallen Adam’s family. However, because Noah’s family failed again, he established Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob, and then Moses, who represented the nation. After that, he went through King Saul, King David, and King Solomon, and through the four major prophets and twelve minor prophets, he came to John the Baptist.


Behold, the Lamb of God Who Takes Away the Sin of the World

Now, there is a mission remaining for human beings to do before heaven. What is that mission? Because human beings fell, they planted the root of sin, so it is for human beings to subjugate Satan, the root of sin, and return goodness and glory to God. To find and establish such human beings, God has worked for 4,000 years.
The Cause of Jesus Christ’s Suffering—The Unbelief of John the Baptist
Then what was the mission that John the Baptist had to do when he came to this earth? It was to testify to and attend Jesus Christ.
Because Jesus Christ was established in the position of a perfected Adam who had not fallen, he was one who could return glory to heaven from his birth. And he was one through whom God could be pleased. God sent Jesus Christ to boast of him before all humankind and before Satan.
Therefore, Jesus Christ was not one who should have walked a path of suffering from his birth. He was to be a mediator of glory who returned joy to God on behalf of humankind from his birth, a mediator of love, and a mediator of goodness. However, the people of this earth did not uphold such a Jesus Christ.
Therefore, you know well through the Principle that even though his life should have been filled only with goodness and joy, with no relationship or connection to sin, Satan invaded Jesus because John the Baptist did not fulfill his responsibility to him.
Then what mission remains for us today, who are in the last days? The mission to complete the mission of John the Baptist remains. That is, as sons and daughters of glory who have been victorious on behalf of the 4,000-year history before Jesus Christ who came, we must become people of goodness who can rejoice with Jesus. You must not forget that this is our mission.
God’s sorrow was that Satan led Jesus around and tested him.
And you will know that the reason for the 2,000-year fight with Satan after Jesus came and went was because the Jews of that time did not believe, and also because John the Baptist, who came with a new mission of testimony, made a mistake.
Human Beings Must Subjugate Satan and Liquidate Sin
Now, at this time when the end of the age is again at hand, you must fight in opposition to sin. And you must fight Satan, knowing that you are in the position of John the Baptist, who had to fight against Satan, who had fought in opposition to God for 4,000 years. On behalf of the 6,000 years, on behalf of the mission of John the Baptist, you must fight and subjugate Satan. Thus, you must not have any trace of Satan in yourselves. That responsibility remains for you. If you do not become ones who fulfill that responsibility, the Second Coming Lord cannot deal with you.
Originally, the garden of God’s ideal of creation was a garden without any trace of Satan. Therefore, to realize God’s ideal of creation on this earth, we must subjugate Satan and ascend to the level of a perfected Adam who has not fallen. Therefore, if we do not become figures who can represent God’s glory and boast before Satan, we cannot resolve the resentment of Jesus Christ being tested by Satan.
Because human beings fell, Satan has violated human beings and is ruling over the whole earth. To reverse this, it must be done according to the principle of indemnity. Because human beings were violated by Satan, even if Jesus does not help, the Holy Spirit does not help, and God does not help, human beings must be able to subjugate Satan with their own strength. Human beings must be able to overcome the conditions of sin that Satan presents. Only then can they become sons and daughters of victory.
If you do not become sons and daughters who can fight alone against the universal Satan and be victorious, you and Jesus will have no relationship.
This path is a path of destiny that we cannot but go.

Behold, the Lamb of God Who Takes Away the Sin of the World

It is a path of destiny that we must go, even if we die, if we cannot go while living. Jesus Christ, when he could not fulfill the will he had to fulfill while living, has been longing for sons and daughters of glory who can represent his own substance even to this day, 2,000 years after his death, in order to fulfill that will even in death.
When we think about this, we realize that the 6,000-year history was not a history of glory. It was not a history of glory before God. And as long as Jesus and the Holy Spirit are still fighting against Satan, and as long as the sons and daughters who follow the will of Jesus and the Holy Spirit are being tested by Satan, you must know that God’s original ideal of creation cannot be said to have been realized on this earth.
For that reason, the resentment that pervaded the earth remained as God’s resentment, and the new history to resolve the resentment of the earth remained as God’s cross, Jesus Christ’s cross, the Holy Spirit’s cross, and the cross of believers today.
Until now, we have lived under the protection and command of the Holy Spirit, the protection and command of Jesus, and the protection and command of God. From now on, we must become a self that can comfort the Holy Spirit, a self that can comfort Jesus, and a self that can comfort God.
The will of the Holy Spirit, the will of Jesus, and the will of God are not a will for any individual. This will is a will that extends through the individual, through the world, to heaven and earth. Who will be the universal sons and daughters who can comfort the universal heart of heaven on behalf of this will? You must know that heaven has been working in providence to find such sons and daughters.
We must fight today and tomorrow to liquidate the wall of sin that has been established in history. You must set out with a new determination toward the hill of sin that you must cross even by dedicating your lives, that is, by dedicating all your energy and your lives.
Just as Jesus, even when the legalistic Jews and the numerous Jewish people opposed him, did not change his core, testified to heaven, and gave a new baptism, so must we today. Now, in the final stage, we must transcend denominations. And at the same time as transcending denominations, we must become a self that can fight against Satan alone, transcending all the ideologies of the world’s people.
Thus, if you are victorious in the fight against all Satans, the glory of heaven and the joy of heaven will be with you.
We Who Must Fulfill the Mission of John the Baptist
At this hour, the wall of sin is blocking your way. What kind of wall of sin is it? It is the sin of devouring the prophets and saints who loved God for 4,000 years, the wall of sin that put Jesus Christ on the cross. Therefore, if you cannot liquidate that sin in your generation, you will have no relationship with the sinless, good kingdom of heaven. If you cannot tear down that wall of sin, you cannot enter the kingdom of heaven. You must know this.
If you stand today in the position of the universal John the Baptist for the will of God, you must know how to observe universal sin. Thus, you must comfort Jesus Christ, the Holy Spirit, and God, who are still laboring because of sin, by embracing the resentment of God, the resentment of Jesus Christ, and the resentment of the Holy Spirit alone. Thus, if the one figure who can lead to the day of rest does not appear among you, it is of no use even if the Lord comes again to this earth.
We must fight against sin in these last days on behalf of John the Baptist. We must fulfill the mission of the universal John the Baptist on behalf of the 6,000-year history. And in addition, we must experience the course of Jesus Christ’s fight.
What remained after Jesus Christ came and went is the doctrine of the cross. Through the doctrine of baptism, through the doctrine of the death of the cross, he tried to establish a standard of eternal victory, but he could only establish it spiritually.
Today, we have the mission to fulfill the mission of John the Baptist, a universal, heavenly mission, combining spirit and flesh. You must experience the resentful heart of Jesus Christ, who came to this earth and was not glorified by human beings, and resolve that resentment.

Behold, the Lamb of God Who Takes Away the Sin of the World

Because this mission was for human beings, Jesus and the Holy Spirit worked for human beings for 2,000 years. However, the saints who believe today do not know this fact. They have believed in Jesus and the Holy Spirit as mere servants for human beings and have believed in them as messengers.
Then who is Satan? He is the archangel. The fall is that human beings, who were supposed to rule over all things in the Garden of Eden, had their dominion taken away by the archangel and were unable to exercise it. Therefore, in the course of our restoration, we must even rule over Satan.
We must pass through such a position.
Then, what must we do to walk such a path? We must learn to walk the same path as John the Baptist and Jesus Christ, following the example of their lives of testimony.

The path Jesus walked to tear down the wall of sin

Then, what path did Jesus Christ walk to tear down this wall of sin? Today, in the last days, you must cross again the path that Jesus Christ walked in your own life's course.
When Jesus Christ fought against Satan, he did not stand in the position of attacking sin to uproot universal sin. Jesus Christ did not stand in the position of attacking sin in order to eliminate it. In order to eliminate sin, in order to subjugate sin, he stood in the position of taking responsibility for that sin. You must know that this is the spirit of Jesus Christ.
Sin is evil and bad. There is a mind that we have through the original nature of creation, and sin is that which acts in opposition to this. Jesus took on this sin to liquidate it. Furthermore, that Jesus took on sin means that he took on the sin of individuals, families, societies, nations, the world, humanity, and even the spirits in the celestial world. You must know that Jesus Christ was the one who took on the sins of countless spirits throughout the 4,000 years of history since the creation.
He even had to take on the sins of the spirits in hell. This is because

<014251>

Jesus came in the position of the perfected Adam. Because Adam's fall caused resentment to sweep even through the celestial world, Jesus had to pull down and bury everything that arose from the fall.
Therefore, the life of Jesus in pioneering a new course was the opposite of the life of the satanic world. Knowing that the element and essence of the satanic world is hopelessness, he taught the way of meekness and humility in opposition to it. Therefore, the truth of Christianity was a truth that departed from the world. The truth of Christianity is one that rebels against the world.
Jesus lived a difficult life because there was a providential reason why he had to turn his back and take on the sins to come, rather than bearing them from the front. Jesus Christ was a pitiful person who suffered the cross until the time he could take on all universal sin and be victorious. Even today, he is in that other world, but he cannot rest. He desires that someone on earth would take responsibility for all that sin.

Jesus who suffered all kinds of humiliation and hardship

When we think about the life of Jesus Christ, who came to bear the sins of humankind, we can see that he experienced all the difficult circumstances that human beings face during his thirty-some years on this earth until he passed away. To bear the sins of the pitiful, he was in a pitiful position; to bear the sins of the hungry, he was in a hungry position; and to bear the sins of the lonely, he was in a lonely position.
Thus, after standing in a position where he could bear individual sin, Jesus sought to bear familial sin. Therefore, to bear familial sin, he appeared before the family, but that family opposed him. His own loving parents opposed him, and even his younger siblings opposed him.
Furthermore, Jesus was rejected by the Jewish denomination. This was because he had to take on denominational sin at the same time as he took on familial sin. Also, even Pilate and King Herod rejected Jesus. They drove Jesus to the cross, saying that his will was different from their hopes.

<014252>

Behold, the Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world

However, until the day he passed away, Jesus did not resent such enemies, but rather prayed for their blessing. You today must deeply engrave this image of Jesus in your hearts.
Jesus was born in a manger. Jesus started from the lowest, most humble position and went to the highest position, the position of the Son of God. Jesus came for the people on this earth, and he came for the people who believe in God on this earth.
But who were Jesus' friends? When he prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane, even his three beloved disciples fell asleep. When he was heading for the summit of the cross, they were in a position where they should have united their hearts and minds, but the three disciples took a position that had nothing to do with such circumstances.
Jesus realized that he had the mission to take on all the sins of the universe, and he gratefully received it when anyone whipped him, and he gratefully received it when they criticized and mocked him.
You must know that Jesus did not try to eliminate sin by striking and breaking it to liquidate it, but he tried to take on and bear all the universal sins related to Satan himself.
However, because sin has not yet been completely liquidated, Jesus Christ is carrying on the history of liquidating that sin.

We must maintain an unchanging faith even if we are persecuted and abandoned

Since you are people who attend Jesus as your Savior, you must think before the Savior you attend, 
to what extent have I taken on sin? To what extent have I tried to bear sin? And you must know how to place yourselves in the same kind of environment in which Jesus lived.
If you are now in the end-of-the-age destiny where you must bear individual sin and family sin, then someday the time will come when you will be persecuted individually.

<014253>

Also, the time will come when you will be persecuted as a family. Just as Jesus received individual opposition, family opposition, and denominational opposition, so too will Christians today in the last days receive such opposition. Furthermore, a religion will emerge that is opposed by society, by the nation, and by the world.
And the fight of Jesus Christ to liquidate human sin has not yet been completely concluded, but in place of Jesus Christ, a believer will emerge on earth who, in order to take on all universal sin, will be criticized by individuals, families, societies, nations, the world, and even the spirits of the spirit world. Furthermore, he will be criticized by the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit. History is moving toward this one peak. You must know this.
The people who believed in the Old Testament and came forward became enemies before Jesus. Likewise, it is easy for people today who have come to believe in Jesus to stand in the position of an enemy before the new providence of God.
Jesus Christ said on the cross, "My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?" (Matthew 27:46). This was because at the scene of the final judgment, God said that he did not know Jesus Christ.
In the same way, when you today try to offer your one body to take responsibility for all the history of sin up to now, God will say that he does not know you. Even so, you must have the same unchanging faith that Jesus had on the cross. If you think that you have offered your one and only body for the will, then you must think of yourselves as already dead. It is the mission of a Christian to present this kind of revolutionary faith.
Then, are there people who oppose you today? You must be grateful to them. Also, is there a family that opposes you? You must be grateful to that family. And is there a denomination that opposes you? You must be grateful to that denomination. Even if the nation and the world oppose you, you must be grateful.

<014254>

Behold, the Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world

Furthermore, even if the spirit world and the physical world oppose you, and even if heaven says it does not know you, you must have an eternally unchanging heart. You must have the faith that you will not change.
A believer with unchanging faith must emerge, even if Satan, who caused the fall of Adam and Eve, opposes, and even if Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and even God say they do not know him. This is the final mission that remains, but today the 2.4 billion people of humankind, the Christians who believe in Jesus, do not know this for sure. And it is not the end just because you have become an individual with such faith. You must create such a family, society, nation, and world. If you do not become saints with this kind of faith, you will have no relationship whatsoever with God's will. The path for Jesus to come to you as the bridegroom will be blocked.

Digest persecution with love and be victorious

Jesus' love was in place of God's love. And God's love is a love that cannot be broken by the opposition of any being in the universe. You must receive this love of God. To do so, you must become victorious sons and daughters who can bravely digest it and not be overcome by it, even if all the sins of this world are cast upon you and Satan tests you. Otherwise, you will have no relationship with the love of God, who is working as the center of power and the center of existence in this universe.
Therefore, just as Jesus Christ was treated unjustly by the people on this earth, but rather worried about them and shed tears, so in the last days, many such saints must emerge from among the believing saints. If there are many such saints, there can be no division between denominations. Noah, Who Walked the Path of Adventure
Now, let's look back at our ancestors of the past. First, if we look at the life of Noah, it was not a smooth life. What must have been Noah's heart when he received the command from God, "I will judge the world with water in 120 years, so build an ark on the top of Mount Ararat"? It was not ten or twelve days, nor was it 12 years, but 120 years.... The words to build an ark on the top of Mount Ararat were words that could not be reconciled with the reality of that time.

264

God's Providence and Supranatural Adventurism

From Noah's situation of receiving and carrying out such a command from God, he was truly a madman, a person who could not possibly fit into that era. Having received a tremendous command from God, Noah made a firm resolve and determination internally. And for a period of not just one day, but 120 years, he lived steadily looking toward one day. You must know that such a Noah was an adventurous pioneer who stood before Heaven on behalf of the 1,600-year history, something that had not existed in the 1,600-year course of history.
Thus, with a determined heart, whether God would take charge or not, whether the people of the world would curse him or not, for Noah, who believed in the command once given as a promise of the unchanging will, all those conditions were not a problem. The standard from which he had already departed for the sake of the will, the steps he took with his life at stake and his life abandoned, before those steps, all those things were not a problem. And so, Noah silently walked the course of repeated toil for a long period of 120 years.
For such a Noah, there must have been criticism from his family. The criticism from society must have also been great. However, the path that humans did not know, the path that people did not take, the path that no one in the 1,600-year course of history had ever gone, no one could block the steps of Noah who set out to break through the path of heaven alone. You must keep in mind that Noah was an adventurous person who could boldly overcome the social environment of that time and the whole world pushing him away.
Thus, no matter what trials or difficulties came his way, Noah surely overcame them, and after 120 years, he found and established one restored family that the family of Adam had lost. You must know this historical situation of Noah.
Abraham was also the same. For Abraham, who received the command from God to leave Ur of the Chaldees, it was not a simple matter. When God told him to leave Ur of the Chaldees, leaving behind his beloved hometown and abandoning all his relatives and neighbors, Abraham's heart was truly at a loss.

265

Humanly speaking, it was something that could never happen.
However, Abraham, who received God's command, transcended all the circumstances in which he had lived until then. He transcended his family, gave up all the household goods he had lived with so diligently, and set out with his bundle. Such a step by Abraham was truly something that could not have happened in the reality of that time. Even if there were people who felt for the will and thought about the will, who could have stood on Abraham's side and said, "You are right. The path you are taking is just, so please lead me"?
Whether the world recognized him or not, Abraham set out with a single-minded devotion to the will, with the heart of leaving Ur of the Chaldees forever. Thus, as he moved his steps as Heaven led him, no matter what adventurous, steep mountains blocked his way, and no matter what hill of death blocked his way, he endured and broke through them.
Abraham's Supranatural Faith
God took Abraham, the eldest son of Terah, a seller of idols, and established him in such a position. Abraham, who was so established, made a firm resolve, saying, "On the path I am going, even if my beloved parents hold me back, even if my beloved friends hold me back, even if my beloved siblings hold me back, this center of mine cannot change." That was not all. Abraham was commanded to offer Isaac, the son he had obtained at the age of one hundred to fulfill the blessing, as a burnt offering to God, and he obeyed. That command was an adventurous condition that had never existed in history. It was a condition that would determine hundreds of millions of matters, including the affairs of heaven and earth, and the affairs of heaven and earth, and without knowing this, Abraham, after receiving the command to offer Isaac as a sacrifice, was about to offer his son on the altar.
Think of Abraham, who was about to pierce his beloved son with a knife as a sacrifice. This was truly a supranatural consciousness. At that time, who could have acknowledged such faith of Abraham? Abraham's

Moses, Who Walked the Path of Adventure and Revolution
Moses was called by Heaven at a time when the Israelites were going through 400 years of hardship in the land of Egypt, the land of their enemies. Thus, under the fearful oppression of Pharaoh, he was protected by his mother for three months, and then he was taken by Pharaoh's daughter and lived in the palace for 40 years. You may think that Moses' life in Pharaoh's palace was a luxurious and good environment.
However, Moses, who faced the will, was in the Egyptian palace, but he was not an Egyptian. The fact that he was God's chosen people representing Israel became more and more deeply embedded in his heart as the days went by. Thus, when Moses, who had lived for 40 years alone with the integrity of Israel, came out of the palace and saw an Israelite being treated unfairly by an Egyptian, his righteous indignation, which he could not bear, exploded and he beat the Egyptian to death.
After that, he left Pharaoh's palace and began his life as a shepherd in Midian with the will of the blessing of Israel left in his heart. That life was not a comfortable life. No one of that era could understand Moses, who had abandoned the luxurious palace of Pharaoh and was living as a shepherd.

267

However, Moses did not despair and built up a secret altar for Heaven, a hidden altar for Israel. Because he was such a Moses, when he was 80 years old, God chose him and established him as the protagonist who could resolve the resentment of the nation.
After that, all the steps Moses took were adventurous. Because he embraced the center of God's providence that transcended reality, his entire life was also supranatural, and what he looked at and what he fought for were also supranatural.
When Moses went to Pharaoh's palace after receiving God's command, God should have blessed and protected Moses who was going on the path He had told him to go, but instead, God blocked Moses' path and tried to kill him. Why did God block the path of Moses, who was going according to His own command, and try to kill him? Realistically, it was something that could never happen. There is something here that we humans cannot know.
Thinking about it realistically, it was a hill that could never be crossed. However, Moses, who had already made up his mind, crossed the condition of the test where God blocked him and Satan blocked him, with the heart of praying for only one thing, the fulfillment of the will, whether he lived or died. Thus, you must know that Moses, who was convinced of the supranatural existence of God in Pharaoh's palace and performed more than 10 miracles, was a universal, adventurous revolutionary who had never existed in the 4,000-year history. In this way, Moses led the 600,000 Israelites with a supranatural faith in the will, without yielding to anyone's opposition. Seeing this, you must know that Moses' entire life was a course of supranatural adventure.
Jesus, Who Was Prepared for a History of Adventure
The one who came as the messenger for world restoration after Moses, the representative of national restoration, is Jesus. Jesus knew that in the course of the 4,000-year history, numerous prophets and sages had lived supranatural lives to fulfill God's will. And he keenly felt that he himself was the one who had the responsibility to complete the will that the prophets and sages had come for the sake of God's providence but had not been able to achieve.

He was truly determined to walk the supranatural, adventurous course to pioneer the 4,000-year course. You must know that Jesus was a person who had the determination to walk a course that was more than the sum of the adventurous historical courses of numerous prophets and sages.
Because Jesus was burdened with the mission of settling the universal history of adventure, he walked the path of adventure from his birth. His life was also a life of supranatural adventure. And you must know that in the end, even the path of death on the cross was a path of supranatural adventure.
Then, what was Jesus' life based on? It was a life that summed up the 4,000-year history, a life that concluded the adventurous course that had been filled with Heaven's resentment until then, and a life of supranatural victory that did not exist on earth to establish a new foundation of victory.
The Obedience of Mary and Joseph
Now, what you need to know is that Jesus was born through the body of the Virgin Mary. If there had not been a person like the Holy Mother Mary before Jesus, who came with an adventurous life, what would have become of God's will? If there had not been a Virgin Mary like the Holy Mother Mary, that is, a woman of Heaven, Jesus Christ could not have been born. If there had not been a foundation of an adventurous offering like Mary on earth, the birth of Jesus, who had to be born with a new life through an adventurous course, could not have happened.
When an angel appeared to the Virgin Mary and told her, "You will conceive and give birth to a son," Mary asked, "How can this be, since I do not know a man?" The angel replied, "God, with whom nothing is impossible, has chosen you." At that time, Mary replied, "Behold, I am the handmaid of the Lord; let it be to me according to your word."

269

I am your handmaid, so let it be as you will. I am yours whether I die or am ruined, so let it be as you will." In this way, Heaven gave birth to Jesus because there was a substantial, living offering, Mary, on earth.
That's not all. In the life of faith that you believe in and follow today, you
There are many paths of unknown adventure. Joseph, who was informed in a dream that his betrothed, Mary, was with child, considered breaking off his relationship with her due to various humanistic concerns. It was not an easy thing to do. It was a supernatural event.

Jesus, Who Walked a Path of Supernatural Adventure from Birth

People did not recognize Jesus, who stepped forward with the sorrow of 4,000 years of history, resolved to be offered as a sacrifice for the sake of one will, whether he lived or died. They did not know that he was the Messiah, the savior of all people. Seeing this, Jesus’ birth was supernatural from the beginning, and he lived a new, ideal life of adventure. You must know that this remains unfulfilled today as the will required at the time of the Second Advent.

Looking at Jesus’ life, from the time he lived and grew up in the family of Joseph and Mary, there was anxiety and worry about the will. He was also criticized and accused by his younger siblings. Jesus’ life of about 30 years did not turn out as Joseph had first intended for him. Joseph loved his own biological son more than Jesus. Therefore, we must know that Jesus also did not have a family environment that fit the social form of the time.

Thus, all of Jesus’ life, who lived like a stepchild and died on the cross, was a supernatural life. In such an environment, while facing all kinds of family discord, Jesus silently overcame it all. Finally, appearing with the will and testifying that he was the Messiah of all people was also not realistic.

Because Jesus was one who went forth with the new gospel of heaven, beyond the dimension of the law established as the creed of Judaism through a long history, he was never welcomed realistically wherever he went, wherever he stayed. Thus, Jesus was driven out by his family, by John the Baptist, and by Judaism, and stood in a place where he had no one to rely on. However, you must know that even in that place where he had no one to rely on, Jesus was not one who sought a place to comfort himself.

Jesus, who knew God’s will, proclaimed the new gospel of the New Testament. When John the Baptist first testified about Jesus, an environment was prepared where all the priests and scribes of Judaism could recognize him. However, as he went through the three-year public life course, Jesus’ position gradually declined, and in the end, he was in a position where only fishermen and insignificant women followed him.

Before Jesus, who had to establish God’s ideal, there had to be an eternal promise as a promise and an eternal will as a will, but in reality, such things could not be found. You must know that the heart of Jesus who gathered a crowd of over 5,000 in the wilderness and blessed them for them towards heaven, and the heart of Jesus who prayed earnestly before the tomb of Lazarus, was a heart filled with a sorrow that could not be compared to anyone on earth.

Throughout 4,000 years of history, countless prophets and saints fought with a heroic resolve and inner sorrow, living adventurous lives for the sake of God’s will, but it could not compare to the inner sorrow of Jesus. Jesus had to break through the heart of all the resentment of 4,000 years of history and satisfy the heart of God’s inner sorrow.

Those who followed Jesus were not people welcomed by the Jewish people. They were not people recognized by the Jewish saints.

Jesus had to go a way that no one in society or the church welcomed. Jesus was in a position where he could not stay in a free environment wherever he went.

Jesus’ Bitter Heart

When Moses led the 600,000 people of Israel, the Red Sea blocked his front, and Pharaoh’s chariots were coming from behind. Moses, on behalf of the 600,000 people who feared death, confronted that test of death with a creed that could overcome and remain. You must know that it was a way to revive the 600,000 people.

It is the same with Jesus feeding the crowd of over 5,000 with five loaves and two fish. The heart of Jesus as he looked at the numerous crowd scattered in the field as the day was ending was a heart that could not be found in any person on earth in reality. It was truly a heart of a great adventure that had to be found before heaven. Because Jesus cried out to the Father with this heart, he brought about an adventurous history of creation.

We must feel that Jesus was one who was born adventurously from birth, who went the path of adventure while living, and who returned to the adventurous standard even when he was crucified at the end. Seeing this, Jesus’ life was not just an insignificant life that could be or not be. It was not a gentle and cool life.

Now you must re-analyze your believing self and match it to the life course of Jesus. If you have a heart that wants to be the bride of Jesus Christ, you must know the life of Jesus, who went through an adventurous life of 30 years from his birth, through Golgotha, a life of humiliation and adversity, to the path of destiny of being hung on the cross, the path of adventurous death.

Truly, Jesus’ life was a life that started with adventure and ended with adventure. We must feel in our hearts, hour by hour, the bitter heart of Jesus who came as the bridegroom but went the path of death lonely, Jesus who died for me, Jesus who died to save me, a heart that pierces our bones and flesh.

Today, in this end time, if there is a gift you can give to Jesus, what would it be? It is to embrace the anxious heart of Jesus Christ who went through an adventurous course, dedicating his life, and to become a unique, universal, adventurous offering that cannot be found even if the whole heaven and earth are mobilized, an offering more excellent than anyone else before the whole world, before the whole heaven and earth.

Therefore, now you must realize the resentful heart of God who has come through the course of history until now and go up from a lowly position. You should not seek to take on any task in a joyful place. You must live with a heart that can die for the sake of the will. Think about it. If Jesus Christ, who died for the earth, resents the earth, there will be no one who can resent more than that.

However, Jesus did not come for himself. He came first for history, for the Israeli denomination, and for the people of Israel. He came for the disciples who were following him, and furthermore, for the nation, the country, the world, and the cosmos. His life was a life for the nation, the country, the world, and the cosmos, and even his death was not a death for himself.

But who said that this path of Jesus was right? Think of Jesus who was betrayed by his beloved disciples at the pass of death, and who had to take responsibility for everything, left alone! If he were to be resentful and resentful towards humans, even if he beat the ground and cried and cried, he would not be able to resolve the resentment of his 30-year life, and there would be no way to be compensated for the hardships he received during that time. However, Jesus was concerned that humanity at that time would suffer under Satan’s rule, and with a heart of compassion, even at the place of death of being crucified, he prayed for the betrayed nation, the betrayed disciples, and all the betrayed humanity. Because he was a Jesus of sorrow, he could be their friend even if the ancestors of this land appealed with 4,000 years of history, and even if all the people of that time appealed, and he could strike himself for the opposing nation and pray for the enemies who opposed him. This is something that has not happened in the 4,000-year history of mankind. Also, you must know that this was a universal, adventurous event to tear down the wall of sin that had penetrated heaven and earth.

If Jesus is the King of kings, you must believe his promise to become the queen of the King of kings and live, entrusting everything to the will, whether you live or die.

Jesus went this way. Jesus’ life was such a life. Jesus’ hope was to live for the will and die for the will in that way.

We Who Must Follow the Path of Adventure, Following the Example of Our Ancestors and Jesus

Then, what should we do today, and what should we know? We must know Jesus, who blessed humanity even at the place of death, and who went with all the inner sorrow filled with a resentful heart. We must transfer the heart of Jesus, who went the path of adventure, establishing one will on earth, to our hearts, and by realizing the death of Jesus, we must resolve the resentment that has penetrated Jesus’ heart through the path of universal adventure today.

Among those who believe in Jesus, there are many who pray to the Father for blessings. However, before you ask for blessings, you must realize the sorrow that has penetrated Jesus’ heart. Not only that, but you must also know Jesus’ life and the course of the cross. You must know today that there was a sorrow of an adventurous course that only Jesus and God knew, which humans did not know, and you must realize the heart of inner sorrow that Jesus could not speak of.

Thus, you must be able to say, “Lord! We will resolve your resentment and all the historical resentment. Please whip us. Please work so that we can fulfill the will that you sought to achieve through all the historical nations. Thus, please work so that we ourselves do not fall, but can stand as an adventurous offering that represents the universal history and resolves the resentment left by countless prophets and saints.”

Now, the hope we desire is to fulfill the will that Jesus Christ left as a legacy on earth. It is our destiny to re-establish the will of Jesus Christ that has fallen to the extreme. History has flowed through the adventurous course of the individual, through the family, through society, through the nation, and through the world. Therefore, when an individual among Christians tried to fulfill the will, an adventurous course was added to that individual’s path. The family was also the same, society was also the same, the nation was also the same, and the world was also the same. Now you must know that this adventurous gateway is placed before you. Therefore, today you must be able to be offered as an adventurous offering on behalf of the adventure of my own body, the life of my own body, standing before the adventurous crossroads of life and death and the universal judgment seat, on behalf of the life of the nation, and on behalf of the people of the world.

And we must be able to follow the life course that the past prophets and saints walked and the life course that Jesus Christ walked, in any era and in any environment today. Furthermore, no matter who, when, or what conditions are presented, we must have the resolve and courage to establish a supernatural self and appeal to the whole universe, and to step forward as one who represents the will of heaven.

We Who Must Be Offered as an Adventurous Offering

Now, today, when the day of the Second Advent is near, you must carry out one final, universal, and adventurous mission of 6,000 years of history. If that mission is universal, you too must become a relatively universal being. You must know that only by stepping forward with an adventurous inner resolve here can you carry out that mission.

What would happen if God’s will were to be fulfilled differently from the life of faith we are living? Until now, the history of God has progressed through a supernatural, adventurous course.

Only by passing through this universal, adventurous gateway can you hold the final flag of victory and sing the hosanna of triumph before the Father, and become a being who can represent the position of the universal bride. Also, only then will you not be caught by any conditions, and you will be able to become a prince of heaven who sets the standard of supernatural adventure, no matter what persecution and criticism there may be in any environment.

You must know that only those who have the resolve to become such a prince will become the bride of Christ who can finally take responsibility for the will of God’s providence and reveal its glory. Let us pray.
