<Sermon> The title of the sermon I would like to contemplate with you today is “Those Who Will Possess the Kingdom of Heaven of Hope.”
I will speak under the title, “Those Who Will Possess the Kingdom of Heaven of Hope.”
282

Those Who Will Possess the Kingdom of Heaven of Hope

From the perspective of God’s ideal of creation, God hoped for the kingdom of heaven in the incorporeal world as well as
but also desired a concrete kingdom of heaven in the world of substance where you could personally dwell, and so you created all things. This is something you all know well.
In other words, God created the created world to see the glory of the spiritual kingdom of heaven and the substantial kingdom of heaven by establishing the heavenly kingdom and the earthly kingdom centered on God and Adam and Eve.

God's Ideal of Creation and the Result of the Human Fall

However, you also know well the fact that due to human mistakes, that is, the human fall, the heavenly kingdom and the earthly kingdom that God so desired disappeared without a trace. This heavenly kingdom and earthly kingdom were not built for God, but for human beings.
God's purpose of creating the heavens and the earth was to establish the earthly kingdom and the heavenly kingdom so that human beings who lived a heavenly life on earth by establishing the kingdom of heaven on earth centered on Adam and Eve could enter and live in the eternal world of the kingdom of heaven. However, due to the fall of Adam and Eve, the spiritual kingdom of heaven and the substantial earthly kingdom disappeared, and the heavenly world and the earthly world became a world of sorrow where Satan could freely accuse God.
After the fall, Satan's sphere of activity extended not only to the earth but also to the bottom of the heavenly throne. So Satan has been accusing human beings in the spiritual and physical worlds. Believers today do not know well that Satan has been moving with this authority.
You must feel to the bone the fact that the created world, which should have sung and rejoiced in God's glorious ideal of creation centered on Adam and Eve, was completely handed over to Satan due to human error, resulting in bringing sorrow to the Father who created it.
God has been carrying out the providence of salvation, establishing relationships with human beings through the remaining angels in order to restore this defiled land. God has been carrying out the providence of salvation in order to deal again with human beings who are in a position of betraying the holy God due to the fall, human beings who have fallen so completely that they cannot be compared even to all things. God has been working by building a bridge to rule over human beings who are dominated and accused by Satan, passing through the Old Testament era and the New Testament era until now.

Providence in the Old Testament Era

The Old Testament era was an era in which God had to work personally and deal with human beings with His glory. However, since that providence was not completed, He held sorrow and pioneered a way to deal with human beings through angels for the second time, which is the history of providence in the Old Testament era.
In the Old Testament era, God's will was conveyed through Noah and Abraham, who were established as messengers in the position of servants. In order to raise the people of this earth, who were asleep in darkness, to a position where the Father could deal with them, He chose the family of Abraham and established the nation of Israel. Thus, through the nation of Israel, a path was pioneered for human beings to gradually approach God.
Thus, heaven established a single standard by which it could work through angels. And by establishing the standard of having fulfilled God's will for Adam and Eve, He worked for 4,000 years until Jesus came in order to create a victorious foundation where He could directly deal with the Father. You must know this.
Jesus is the one who was established to raise human beings who are in a position to be dealt with by a servant to a position where they can be dealt with by a son, and the gospel given is the New Testament. Therefore, human beings after Jesus came to be in a position where they could deal with God through Jesus. Human beings who should have directly received God's love fell and could not directly receive God's love, so as we have passed through 6,000 years of history, what we have been hoping for until now is to go to a position where we can receive God's love after receiving the son's love.

Those Who Will Possess the Kingdom of Heaven of Hope

By receiving the son's love and fulfilling the ideal of creation, we must become God's sons and daughters who have a substance that can share joys and sorrows with God, who wanted to enjoy centered on love. Not only spiritually, but this body itself must go to a position where God can directly love it. You must know that this mission has remained for us because of the human fall.

Jesus' Mission and the Role of the Holy Spirit

Jesus came to this earth and had to establish human beings in a position where they could receive God's love. He also had to make them receive God's love in the position of a son like Jesus, both spiritually and physically. Jesus came to this earth with this mission, but because people did not believe, Jesus Christ could not complete the mission of establishing human beings in a position to receive God's love both spiritually and physically. He only pioneered a position where we could be called sons and daughters spiritually.
Then what is the ultimate purpose of God's providence of restoration? It is to complete the standard on this earth where people who exist as substances with both spirit and body can live while receiving God's love.
The one who has been working for 2,000 years since Jesus to complete this purpose is the Holy Spirit. Although the Holy Spirit has been working since Jesus' death until now, He is not working by directly establishing a providential foundation on the earth to complete the will of God's ideal of creation, but is playing the role of a bridge so that we can go to heaven through him. You must know this well.
Then what kind of people are those who can live a heavenly life on earth? What kind of spiritual beings are those who can live in the infinite spiritual world, the heavenly kingdom? The earthly kingdom and the eternal heavenly kingdom are places where only those who have received the love of Jesus and the Holy Spirit on earth, and beyond that, have received the Father's love directly, lived with the Father, and become victors of harmony centered on the ideal of love can live. You must know this.

Qualifications of the People of the Kingdom of Heaven

From the standard of God's creation, such a place is the kingdom of heaven of hope. If we acknowledge this, we must think about in which sphere you who are living today are hoping for the kingdom of heaven of hope, which was God's purpose of creation.
In Revelation 14:1, there is a verse that says, "Then I looked, and there before me was the Lamb, standing on Mount Zion, and with him 144,000 who had his name and his Father’s name written on their foreheads."
What standard are the heavenly gifts that Christians in the world today hope for based on? They are based on the gifts of the bridegroom and the bride. They think that this is all there is. However, as it is said, "and with him 144,000 who had his name and his Father’s name written on their foreheads," the Father's name is the problem.
Today, after you believe in Jesus the bridegroom and qualify as a bride, you should not remain only in Jesus' love, but use that love of Jesus as a stepping stone to go to a position where you can receive the love of God, who could not personally love human beings for 6,000 years.
This was the entire purpose of God's providence, and the purpose for which He sent Jesus Christ and worked for 2,000 years, but the saints of today do not know this.
Then when will we, beyond the position of bridegroom and bride, become victorious eternal beings and become substances that can harmonize centered on the Father's love from the earth to the heavens, that is, even in the kingdom of heaven of eternal life? You must have this kind of love relationship. This is the purpose of Jesus Christ and the purpose of God's providence.
Until now, you have believed in the hope of the love of the bridegroom and the bride. Now, holding the hand of Jesus Christ, you must go before the Father and say, "Father! Please treat us as if we have fulfilled the will of the 6,000 years you desired. We know that this is the purpose of God's creation, so Father! Please love us personally!" You must become such people. You must know that God's providence cannot end until such human beings are found not in the spiritual world, but in the world of substance.
Because Jesus Christ came to this earth and created the expectation of being able to acquire the authority of love of spiritual sons and daughters, if the people on earth form a relationship with Jesus Christ, become one, and inherit that authority of love, then the Satans who accused in the spiritual world, the Satans who accused on the earth with human sins as a condition, will have no way to accuse.

Effort for Complete Salvation

Satan took away Adam and Eve, whom God had created, not only their spirits but also their spirits and bodies combined. Therefore, you must keep in mind that on heaven's side, God has established us believers today in order to reclaim Adam and Eve, who are a combination of spirit and body, from Satan and to pioneer a way for God to personally love them.
Jesus Christ came to this earth with this amazing creative center of the universe as a standard. Then where did Jesus Christ set the standard for the final battle? It was in enabling the saints who followed Jesus to receive God's love both spiritually and physically, because they had only received God's spiritual love. Since receiving God's love both spiritually and physically is the hope, Jesus, who only carried out the providence of spiritual salvation, cannot enjoy complete glory in heaven. Even in heaven, he has to pray for us human beings on earth.
In this way, because the hope of Jesus Christ has not yet been completely fulfilled on earth, you must know that the twelve apostles centered on Jesus and the countless spiritual beings in paradise are being fully mobilized with this one hope as a standard.

For us who are in the last days today, the results of the efforts of the angels who cooperated in the course of providence remain. In addition, the results of the efforts of countless apostles remain. We must be responsible for all the results and conditions of these historical efforts today. We must also be able to resolve the grievances of the tens of thousands of saints who worked and cooperated on behalf of God's will of providence in the past, and all the spiritual beings in the spiritual world, including Jesus.
We who are in the last days, when we go before God on behalf of past history, must be recognized by Jesus Christ and the Holy Spirit. And after going through the stage of being recognized by Jesus and the Holy Spirit, the Trinity will decide whether you can go before God. You must know that the New Testament providence is working up to this stage.

Recognition Stage, Decision Stage, Judgment Stage

What is the recognition stage here? It can be said to be the engagement stage before the wedding. What is the decision stage? It can be said to be the stage of qualifying to go to the holy ceremony as a bride. Then what is the final remaining stage? It is the judgment stage. This stage is a day when God sets human beings before Him and says, "This is my beloved, a being who can share joys and sorrows with me forever, a being who can receive God's love as an eternal and unchanging substance that I hoped for and desired as the ideal of creation," and God personally raises His hand and proclaims it before all things. This is the stage of judgment.
Although God has been carrying out His providence for 6,000 years, He has not yet had a universal day of judgment. The judgment that is given with this one day as a standard is the judgment.
You must go through this gate of judgment and inherit the blessing that God gave to Adam when He blessed him, saying, "Rule over all things." Thus, you must be born as a people of the heavenly kingdom and be able to say, "Father! Please love me. Seeing my historical conditions, I have known the will of Christ's hope, the will that the Holy Spirit and God desired, so Father, please bless me."

Those Who Will Possess the Kingdom of Heaven of Hope

You must become such a person. Such a person must appear on the earth in the last days.
Only after judging by setting up such a person will all created things know that they must serve us as God's own sons and daughters. Satan will surrender only after a relationship of God and His own sons and daughters is established.
For you who are facing this history of providence, the problem is to discern yourselves and decide what position you will stand in. First, you must stand in a position to be recognized by Jesus Christ and then by the Holy Spirit. Looking at this in the light of the history of providence, the recognition stage is the Old Testament era, and the decision stage is the New Testament era.
The stage of judgment is the era of the Second Advent.
History up to the present day has descended vertically through numerous courses.
However, the time is now coming when the history that has been descending vertically will unfold horizontally.
We, who are facing the providence of judgment after passing through the providence of recognition and the providence of decision for 6,000 years, must pass through the history that has flowed vertically and the horizontal history of the end of the age.
What does this mean? God's history has been a history of fighting against Satan. For 6,000 years, we have fought against Satan, but the battle has not yet been decided.
Numerous prophets and saints came and labored, but they could not fulfill God's will on earth. Thus, you must face a time when you can fulfill on earth the will of the many prophets and saints who passed away without fulfilling their will.
In these last days, many strange phenomena that you cannot understand will occur. People will appear, saying, “I am Elijah.”
Such a time will come. People will appear, saying, “I am Elijah,” “I am Moses,” “I am Paul,” or even “I am Samuel.”
Why do these phenomena occur? It is because of the principle of indemnity and restoration. In other words, it is because they must complete the restoration through indemnity of the mission they left behind.
Because they fought against Satan centering on the will of God's providence in the course of restoration through indemnity but could not establish the standard of victory, their mission has been extended to later generations.

We earnestly hope and pray, Father, that we will not become those who do not realize that the inner sorrow of Jesus Christ, who had no choice but to say, 'Do not come the way you are coming,' and 'Do not hope for what you hoped for,' because there was nothing to take when He wanted to take, remained in that one self.
Now, may the entire group gathered here be able to respond to the words of Jesus, who said, 'Forsake everything and follow me,' and please allow them to become sons and daughters who can be called there.
When You command us toward the garden of Your desired wish, before the will that Father rejoices in, we can prepare everything without hesitation and step forward without hesitation,
Unless we become the sons and daughters whom Heaven can love and hold onto at this hour,
it will not do.
Therefore, we have the responsibility to take on the historical resentment of 6,000 years and fight against Satan. Please allow us to become victorious champions who can fight with a new determination, a new resolve, a new pledge, an indomitable heart, and a good heart. Father, I earnestly hope and desire this.
Now, as we stand before the grace You have permitted, may this be an hour where we can rejoice through the Word, where the grace of love can dwell, and where glory can appear as a boast. Father, please take charge, and we also desire to entrust ourselves to You. I earnestly ask this and have prayed in the name of the Lord. Amen.

<Sermon> The title I want to contemplate with you is “Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People.” With this content, “Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People,” I will speak for a short while.

God’s Ideal of Creation and the Result of the Human Fall

God, human beings, and all things were all meant to be eternally one centered on a single ideal of creation.

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

However, because human beings, who are in the middle position between heaven and all things, made a mistake, all things were divided as all things, heaven as heaven, and people as people. Therefore, in order to find the original world of creation again, He had no choice but to carry out the history of restoration, starting from all things, then human beings, and finally to heaven. You should not be people who do not know this situation of the Father.

We today, who were born with the fallen lineage, and humanity today, which dwells as a fallen race, must first become people who feel in our minds and bodies the sorrow of God that pierces us.

Although we have all fallen, as long as there is the relationship in which God created us human beings, and as long as there is the Father who is toiling to fulfill the will of the providence, we should not think that we are in a meaningless position.

Even if you yourselves are evil, and even if you are in an evil place, you must first become people who recognize that the tear marks of the Father’s toil, who has been carrying out the providence through the course of history until now, remain on your bodies. Next, you must feel that you carry on your bodies, on behalf of history, the traces of the toil and suffering of the Father who has been carrying out the providence to find and restore us again, that is, the providence of restoration. Furthermore, you must know that the original ideal of creation, the internal desire that remains in God, is with us in the last days.

Then, we must now know that the sorrow of God, who exists as an incorporeal God, pierces my very being, and that the mark of the toil of God, who exists as an incorporeal God and carries out the providence of restoration, remains on my body as a foundation of hope.

And we on this earth must become people who have a sorrow that can substitute for His sorrow by bending our bodies and minds as much as God is sorrowful with His sad heart, as much as the traces of His suffering He has toiled, and as much as the heart of original goodness He has held as a hope. We must also have a heart of suffering that substitutes for God’s toil.

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

We must know that even on this day, He is demanding a form that can reveal the suffering of the invisible God with a visible body. Furthermore, we must know that the Father is seeking one religion of hope that can fulfill His desire by judging all historical religions.

Whether sleeping or awake, sitting or standing, active, in any moment of the process of life or in a fleeting moment, the Father is longing for the appearance on this earth of true saints who can be touched in their hearts and stimulated in their bodies. You who have gathered here today must go to a position where you can experience this with your hearts.

Jesus’ Purpose in Coming and the Unbelief of the Jewish People

Then, the ideal of creation of the incorporeal Father, who made human beings and all things and intended to enjoy joy and glory; the ideology of creation of God, who set human beings before all things and hoped that all would be intoxicated with the ideal of goodness, boast of God’s love, and share joys and sorrows together, remained as a resentment in His heart due to the human fall. The one who came with the mission to resolve this was Jesus. And the one who came to substantively resolve the core of God’s internal resentment on behalf of the 4,000-year history of God’s toil, on behalf of humanity, and on behalf of all things, was Jesus Christ.

Then, where were the beings who had to attend Jesus, the beings who had longed for Jesus, the beings who could have eternally shared joy with Jesus!

The Jewish people of that time had to know that Jesus Christ was the one who represented God’s internal heart, the heart of piercing resentment, and that he came as the substantial image of God, who exists as an incorporeal existent being, and was the one who could substantively resolve God’s resentment.

However, among the people of Israel, there was not a single person who knew the will of God’s internal providence, who sought to be comforted through Jesus Christ, and who could sympathize with God’s heart of hope and attend this Jesus, praising him, saying, “This is the one who can resolve the heart of God who has been sorrowful for 4,000 years, the being of eternal hope whom the Father has been seeking.”

The sorrow of the incorporeal God must be resolved through a corporeal human being. And the one who could represent the sorrow of God and the sorrow of all people was Jesus.

However, Jesus did not have a single day of joy in his entire life. This was because the tears of God’s sorrow shed for 4,000 years were piercing his heart, and even though all people should have become one with Jesus and resolved God’s sorrow, not a single person experienced Jesus’ sorrow and came forward before Jesus. When we look at Jesus’ entire life from beginning to end, there was not a single such person. Therefore, we must keep in mind that the mark of such resentment has been extended down to us today.

For the people of Israel who were hoping for the Messiah, it was a fact that they had never even dreamed that Jesus, who was born as the only-begotten Son of heaven, the crown prince of heaven, would appear in such a sorrowful and haggard form.

That is why Jesus sought for one being who could attend him. He sought, not centered on himself, but on behalf of God’s internal heart. From birth, Jesus sought a being who could participate in God’s sorrow, a being who could represent God’s toil from birth, and a being who could represent God’s hope from birth, but from his birth in a manger, through his thirty-some years of life, until he crossed the hill of the cross, he could not find a single such being.

Then, while all people attend the Jesus who died on the cross, why did no one attend the living Jesus who came with God’s eternal love to transfer that love to human beings? The responsibility for that lies with human beings. Even though Jesus came to resolve God’s sorrow and to remove the course of God’s toil, and even though Jesus came as the substance of God’s hope to build the garden of hope, it was the sin of our ancestors that they did not fulfill their responsibility to embrace the sorrow of that Jesus, to bear his suffering on their own bodies, and to feel his hope and live with it in their hearts.

Then, what is it that Jesus demands of us today? Because the work of trying to resolve all of God’s resentment through the person of Jesus was extended due to our ancestors’ failure to take responsibility, God’s sorrow became Jesus’ sorrow, God’s toil became Jesus’ toil, and God’s hope became Jesus’ hope. Furthermore, all of that has reached the Holy Spirit.

What Jesus Demands of Us Today

Thus, we today have the responsibility to resolve the sorrow of God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit that has been extended through the 2,000-year history. You must feel this.

And a person who can resolve the resentment of the 6,000-year sorrow hidden in God’s heart, a person who can take on the 6,000 years of toil, must appear. A person who will again reveal the 6,000-year hope of God on this earth must appear among us. They must be found among us.

Now, when you come before the amazing grace of the Father, or before the grace of Jesus Christ, you should not think that the day you come forward is the beginning. And when you stand before the Father, it is not you as an individual who is standing. You must have the realization that when you believe, you are not believing with only your own life at stake, but you are believing with the 6,000-year history at stake.

Even when you stand in a position of repenting for your sins before the Father, you must feel that this is not only repentance for yourself, but repentance on behalf of 6,000 years. Also, when you have a heart of gratitude before the grace of the Lord and the love of the Lord, you should not think that you alone are giving thanks within a certain time frame. You must become a person who can give thanks on behalf of the entire providence of the Father that has been carried out for 6,000 years, on behalf of the horizontal and vertical history, and on behalf of a single standard of hope.

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

In this way, Jesus is hoping that a person who will resolve God’s sorrow, a person who can take on God’s toil, and a person who can fulfill God’s hope on his behalf will appear on the earth today.

Jesus, who came to substantively achieve the Father’s will, could not complete that work on this earth, so he passed away with the destiny of having to come again. Therefore, this Jesus will come to you, who are insignificant, with a heart of sorrow that represents the 6,000-year history. He will come to you not only with the sorrow of 4,000 years, but with the sorrow of 2,000 years added to it. Also, he will come to you not only with sorrow, but with the resentment of 2,000 years of toil added to it.

Our Responsibility for the Returning Jesus

When Jesus, who comes with the hope of 6,000 years, appears before us, what is the responsibility that human beings must fulfill? It is to substantively take on the burden of Jesus’ heart, Jesus’ sorrow, and Jesus’ toil.

Jesus, who came before the people of Israel to resolve the 4,000 years of sorrow on behalf of God’s 4,000 years of toil, was not believed by the people of Israel, who opposed him and caused him to die on the cross. In this way, because there was no one among the people of Israel who could know, believe, and attend Jesus as the one who came to resolve the 4,000 years of sorrow on behalf of the Father’s toil and the 4,000-year history, Jesus had no choice but to die on the cross. Therefore, to complete this work, Jesus must return.

We in the last days, who must bring the 6,000-year history to a total conclusion, must stand alone before God, before the Trinity, and have a heart that can say, “Please entrust God’s sorrow to me as my sorrow. Please entrust God’s toil to me as my toil. Please entrust God’s hope to me as my hope.” And although you are individuals, you must become people who prepare for the day of Jesus’ coming with a heart that you can represent heaven and earth. You must become Christians of such a world.

You who must prepare for the second coming of Jesus must retrace once more the life of Jesus Christ who came and went. You must become people who can experience the circumstances of Jesus’ birth, Jesus’ life, and Jesus’ passing as your own circumstances.

You must have the same sense of responsibility that Jesus felt, that he had the responsibility to redeem all people while embracing God’s sad heart, and you must have the heart that you yourselves have lain in the manger of Jesus, who was born on the evil earth and lay alone.

Even though Jesus was the crown prince of heaven, the prince of heaven, what is this about a manger when he was born on this earth? The sorrow of Jesus, who was overwhelmed with sorrow, was sorrowful, but the internal sorrow of God looking at that Jesus was beyond words.

You must feel that sorrow to the bone in light of such facts. Also, you who are in the last days must feel a sense of responsibility that you have taken on alone the mission that Jesus Christ bore.

And even though he came for all people, he was treated poorly and could not speak
We must learn to think of Jesus’ circumstances, who was in an incredibly miserable position, as our own. Jesus was in a situation where if there had been just one worthy person on this earth who could comfort his sorrow, he would have wanted to hold onto that person and pour out all his hopes.
However, the people of Israel, whom God had chosen over 4,000 years, and the Jewish faith, which had been prepared for Jesus Christ, did not know Jesus. They had no connection whatsoever with the Jesus who lay in a manger in the city of Bethlehem. This event once again repeated God’s sorrow. There was no one to side with the Jesus who was born in a stable.
We must now become people who can gather and resolve the resentment of God and the resentment of Jesus who came to this earth and departed. Only then can we remove the conditions for Satan’s invasion from our bodies. And if we know that the returning Lord will appear on this earth representing 6,000 years of history, then…

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

You must not stand in the same position as the people of Israel. Their faith was not centered on Jesus, nor on the Messiah, nor on God; it was self-centered. The Messiah was sure to come, but even knowing that, no one prepared to receive him.
When the wise men from the East came to worship the baby Jesus lying in a manger in Bethlehem and proclaimed it, the entire city of Jerusalem was in an uproar. Astrologers from a foreign land had come to find Jesus. But this commotion was not a joyful event. It was not a joyful event.
Preparation for the Returning Lord
Today, you who believe in Heaven, you who believe on behalf of 6,000 years of history, must not remain in the same position as the Jewish faith that committed a great wrong. You must now be able to prepare for the coming Messiah, and you must not only be able to resolve the sorrow of Jesus at his first coming but also be able to return glory to him. This responsibility lies with you.
Today, if you enter a spiritual stage, a place where you can confer with the Father, many instructions will be given to you, such as “do this” or “do that.”
When the Lord comes to the earth, he will eat, he will wear clothes, he will have a place to stay, and he will be active. But the Jewish people, who longed for the Messiah to come, did not know this and did not wait with preparations to receive him. There was no one who waited with even a single set of clothes prepared for him.
If there had been people who had prepared with such an earnest heart, when the three wise men from the East came to Jerusalem and said such things, when all the Jewish people were in an uproar, they would have followed the wise men to Bethlehem. But on the road, there were only the three wise men.
This act of leaving a mark of sorrow was the sin committed by our ancestors who followed God and claimed to be for God’s will.
Today, you must not stand in such a position. You must be able to prepare to receive the coming Lord in mind and body, inside and out.
Then what is it that we, in the Last Days, and Christians all over the world must be mobilized to do? If the Jewish people who longed for the Messiah had become a people who prepared a place for him to stay when he was born, they would not have laid Jesus in a manger. Likewise, Christians must become people who can prepare a place for the Messiah to stay when he is born.
The Offering for the Coming Lord
You should not think of Jesus being wrapped in swaddling clothes and lying in a manger as a joyful thing. Jesus was someone who should have been laid in a place more glorious than anyone else on this earth, more glorious than anyone in the 4,000 years of history, with all people united. And as the Son of God, he was someone who should have been loved and praised by all people. Furthermore, he was the Jesus who should have been boasted of before Satan.
But what must have been God’s sorrow as He watched the scene of the Jewish people failing to attend Jesus in such a way? You must know this sorrow of God.
Therefore, you must now become people who, on behalf of God’s heart and knowing the sorrowful heart of Jesus 2,000 years ago, secretly prepare an offering internally. Heaven’s offering cannot be shown to Satan. It cannot be shown to people either. That is why, if you look in the Bible, the most precious offerings were never revealed. Why? Because no one should know about it first. The one who should know must know first. If Satan knows first, he will approach it with lingering attachment, so it cannot be.
You yourselves must prepare for the Father, for the Lord who comes for the sake of the world, but you must prepare a precious offering that is not of this earth, an offering that cannot be exchanged for anything on this earth.

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

When the Lord himself is present and active, you must establish a foundation of attendance within your own body so that the Lord does not feel any difficulty, either mentally or physically. Why is this so? Because your body is the most precious thing in this world.
He is such a precious being, a single substantial being who can represent the entire cosmos. Therefore, when the Son of the Father, the only-begotten Son whom the Father loves, comes, you must build a foundation of peace where he can rest for eternity. And with mind and body united, when Jesus comes again, you must become his hands and feet, live his life in his stead, and attend him in comfort. Also, you must become people who can fight the battle that Jesus fought 2,000 years ago in his place.
Jesus Christ fought for 2,000 years, and now you must have the heart to say, “I will take full responsibility for that battle with Satan,” and you must have the heart to say, “My own body will prepare even the shield for that battle.”
And you must fully comprehend Jesus’ situation at the time of his birth, and then you must fully comprehend Jesus’ heart when he lived on the earth.
Jesus’ Tears and Prayer
If you now try to truly seek the Father, if you try to seek the bosom of Jesus’ love, you will shed tears.
God was sorrowful for 4,000 years but could not show that sorrow, but Jesus lived shedding tears in substance. Although it only appears in three or four places in the Bible, there are infinitely many hidden facts of Jesus actually shedding tears.
When he looked at the Jewish people whom God had loved throughout the providential history of several thousand years, there was not a single moment when he did not shed tears.
Jesus shed tears every time he prayed to God. Whenever he faced difficult and lonely situations, Jesus was sorrowful in a way that only the Father knew. However, Jesus could not speak of this sorrow to his disciples.

You must know this situation of Jesus.
It was not just once or twice that Jesus went up to the Mount of Olives and prayed all night. He did not only pray in the Garden of Gethsemane.
While walking a difficult path, the only place he could appeal to about his sorrowful situation was Heaven. However, it was not that he intended to entrust that sorrow to Heaven. Rather, he asked to take on that sorrow himself. “Father! I will take on the sorrow you feel when you look at me, so Father! Please receive comfort by looking at me! I will bear the Father’s sorrow, so please do not be sorrowful,” he pleaded. And he only prayed, “I will take responsibility for the 4,000 years of toil, so Father, do not worry. Since I am here, do not worry that the Father’s hope remains.”
Jesus had sorrow from the time he came of age. Because the people of the world could not attend Jesus, he experienced sorrow from the time he was growing up.
Jesus grew up in Joseph’s family as a stepson. So the whole village said many things about Jesus, but he lived a life of silence. While harboring the unspeakable will of Heaven, a great and amazing will, he grew up as an ordinary child. You should not think that his life of living for 30 years doing carpentry work was a good life. Jesus, who should have stood in a more noble position than anyone in the nation of Israel and lived revealing the Father’s joy and glory, lived holding an adze and a plane to help with Joseph’s livelihood. What does this mean?
Today, if there are sons and daughters who want to uphold God’s will, true sons and daughters who wish to resolve God’s resentful heart, they must know to go by following the life that Jesus walked as an example.
If you want to know the life that Jesus lived, you must sympathize with Jesus’ heart that was in place of amazing grace, experience that heart, and enter into that difficult position. Then you will feel that Jesus’ sorrow was a sorrow that transcended every hour and every aspect of life, and that Jesus’ life was a life in which he could not feel peace for a single moment.

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

However, Jesus, who came for the sake of the earth, was anxious not to turn the sorrow he suffered because of the earth back to Heaven. Today, those who believe in Jesus often try to pass on their own cross and their own sorrow to Heaven. We do not believe in Jesus for that purpose. However, the person who can say, “Heaven’s sorrow is sorrow because of me, so I will bear that sorrow. God, do not worry,” is a person who has passed through one aspect of Jesus’ conviction, of Jesus’ life.
Are You My Friend?
Now, if the footprints of sorrow of Jesus, who lived for some 30 years in tears, remain, you have the responsibility to resolve this.
Jesus lived in sorrow for some 30 years and finally met his fate, shouldering the cross. You must know that at the final moment, he was overcome with the sorrowful heart of having to fulfill the will even while saying, “Eli, Eli, lama sabachthani?” which means, “My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?”
Then today, if you look at the world with the heart that “I am a friend of Jesus,” you will not be able to look at this world without tears. Jesus shed tears every time he took a step, every time he moved his body. There was not a single time when he did not shed tears. Just like this Jesus, if there is a person among the saints who believe today who sheds tears with a sorry heart before Heaven in their daily life, he will become a friend of Jesus.
If there is a person in each church, in each family, who can shed tears for each other, knowing the heart of Jesus and on behalf of God, then infinite life and love will surely be with them without them having to ask God for it. You must know that God is demanding Christians with whom circumstances can be shared, with whom affection can be shared, and with whom content can be shared.
If the Lord comes to this earth today, he will ask, “Are you indeed my friend who has spent some 30 years of hardship?” He will also ask, “To what extent have you embraced God’s sorrowful heart, and how many days and nights have you lived with a worldwide sorrow?”
You must know that because human beings could not uphold the Jesus who came to the earth, they offered Jesus up to Satan as a condition. And you must overcome this condition.
Why are we alive today? It is because before this body dies, before dirt enters these eyes, we must become people who can hold onto the life of Jesus and weep with all our loyalty, and become true people who can raise up what was trampled in Jesus’ life. Therefore, you must fulfill this responsibility while you are alive.
That is why the “I” of today is not a simple “I.” You should not think that you are only as old as you have lived so far. You must feel that each and every one of you is a self who bears the universal mission to bring to fruition in your own body the providence of restoration of God, which is the 4,000 years from Adam and Eve to Jesus, and the 2,000 years from Jesus to the present.
Therefore, just as Jesus was dignified before his enemies, you must also be dignified even if you suffer the tribulation of the cross. Even if you shed tears, do not shed them for yourself, and even if you weep, do not weep for yourself.
If you are to weep, weep for Jesus. Then for you…
How joyous Jesus must be as he thinks of you. And God will understand your circumstances. Even when you shed tears, you should become people who shed them with such a heart. It means that those who shed tears for themselves are not needed. Only those who shed tears and repent for the sake of Jesus, for the sake of God's love, become the sons and daughters of God.

When you face the suffering of the cross, if you truly feel the Father's love and feel for yourselves that you are within the realm of the Father's love, you will not be able to pray. I have felt such things. Even when a heavy burden that felt like a thousand tons was placed on my shoulders, I did not pray, "Father, please make this lighter."

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

I did not pray, saying, "Let us become those who attend the Lord who came for all people." You should not offer such prayers.

Our loving Father knows me well in this situation. If I were to pray to the Father, who is already in a sorrowful position, "Father, I am carrying this kind of burden," it would inflict a second sorrow upon the Father's aching heart.

You must know even these things when you face God and Jesus. If there were only a few people with this kind of heart among the thirty million people of this nation, they would be able to block the sorrow of this nation. We must absolutely not be people who cry because of our own sorrow.

**Jesus, Who Was Anxious to Comfort the Father**

Jesus came to this earth with a universal mission, but he suffered throughout his entire life. However, he did not pray for that sorrow, but rather was anxious to comfort the Father's grieving heart and worries. At the same time, he was a Jesus who looked down at the earth and grieved to forgive the ignorance of human beings. However, Jesus' life did not end with a life of tears for over 30 years. Because he stepped forward to take on God's toil, he lived with a heart to glorify only the Father's will, whether he lived or died. Jesus lived for the will, regardless of whether God or the people on earth recognized him, and regardless of time or place.

Although he was a Jesus who came to completely fulfill the will, he was not a Jesus who agonized or despaired because he was to die on the cross. Even when he went to the place of death, Jesus did not defend himself. As you know, Jesus did not defend himself as he went through Pilate's court, over the hill of Golgotha, and to the place where he was crucified and died. He was the protagonist of no defense. He was a Jesus who could feel that it was his own responsibility that people opposed him so much. We who believe in Jesus Christ must become friends of Jesus who went from the Jesus who was born to the Jesus who lived.

(Page 321)

What did Jesus become a friend of? He was a person who became a friend of death, not of life. In the course of history, countless people have gone the way of death, but Jesus was the only one who became a friend of death on behalf of all people and died on behalf of all people.

Therefore, Christianity is a religion of death and sacrifice, and the truth of Christianity is a truth that overcomes death. And Jesus' activities were to destroy his own body. You must recognize that it was Jesus' path to be able to love without resentment even while doing so.

Because Jesus was a friend of death, he did not mind death even when it was hastened. You must know that he lived a life with the leisure to die for his enemies.

Later, even God said, "I do not know the Jesus on the cross." At that time, Jesus cried out, "My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?" This was not because hope seemed to turn to despair and his entire life seemed to come to nothing. He cried out because he was worried that he could not fulfill the Father's will completely through his death. Jesus did not care whether the Father sent him to heaven or hell because he had fulfilled his responsibility. Jesus, who was in a position to become a friend of death, was satisfied with dying and intended to complete his mission by dying.

Jesus came with universal love, but no one knew it. Although he came with such an amazing gift, he had no lingering attachment once he set out to become a friend of death. Even though he came to fulfill the hope of heaven, he was a Jesus who did not refute or resent even when heaven did not treat him as an object of hope.

There is a final pass on our way to find God. Even if you go with all your sincerity, there will be a time at the end when heaven says it does not know. The reason heaven says it does not know is that a worldwide mission lies before us. That is why Jesus also had to take on a worldwide mission and experienced such things.

(Page 322)

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

Likewise, such things will happen to you. Even if you give all your loyalty and devote your entire life to clinging to the Father, there will be a time when heaven says it does not know.

However, you must be able to say, "It is the Father's will if I die, and it is the Father's will if I live." Also, if you have hope, you must have this one hope of fulfilling the Father's will. You must become the owner of a heart that can say, "It is a joyous thing not to be able to eat and not to be able to wear."

**The Final Pass on the Road to God**

Today, you should not be people who believe in Jesus to go to heaven. Those who believe in Jesus to die will go to heaven. If you believe in Jesus to die well rather than to live well, it will be an extremely precious faith. Where did the twelve apostles, who believed in the hope of living well, all go when Jesus died?

You should not believe for your one life to live well, but you should believe to sacrifice your one life well, that is, to die well. To do so, we must resemble the life of Jesus. We have the responsibility to uphold the life of Jesus on behalf of history. We have the responsibility to take on the life of Jesus. We can have the love of Jesus only when we have the life of Jesus. We can receive the love of Jesus only when we attend Jesus. Also, you must have a religious character that can emulate the 2,000 years of Jesus' toil.

Not only that, but since God's providence has been extended for 6,000 years, you must be able to attend the one who will come to take responsibility on behalf of the 6,000 years of providence. When the Father or the Lord appears to you, you must have time to invite and attend the Lord. That time is not one or two hours, but you must be able to attend him forever.

Then, what must we do to qualify as a bride who can attend the Lord? Above all, we must be able to take responsibility for and comfort the 6,000 years of God's sorrow.

(Page 323)

And before the Lord who has toiled, you must be able to say, "I will do this and that. I will attend you in this and that way. I have prepared in this and that way." You must become a saint who can say, "Lord, come. Lord, appear," with universal preparation. Such a saint cannot perish.

This great mission is before us. However, many people do not know this. And they do not know that the inner heart of Jesus and the inner hope of Jesus are revolving around each one of us today. What will happen to such a person? The person who does not know will perish. The time will come when they will beat their chests.

**To Attend the Coming Lord**

To attend with the heart, to attend with the body, to attend with society, to attend with the world, and to attend with heaven and earth—this is the responsibility of a son. However, today, you yourselves are not even able to attend Jesus with your hearts. You must know that you have not even started to attend Jesus.

By attending with the heart, attending with the body, being attended by society, being attended by the nation, being attended by the world, and being attended by heaven and earth, glory must fill and overflow not only you as individuals, but also your families, societies, nations, the world, and the entire creation. You probably never imagined that you have such a universal mission.

Then, you who have gathered with this mission, unlike others, should not be petty. You should not become cowardly and foolish people. You must be dignified even when you go before countless enemies. You have the responsibility to attend Jesus who comes with universal glory and universal love. You are the ones who must stand in a universal position with your hearts and substance.

However, Christians who are satisfied with offering devotion for themselves and for their families are not needed. Christians who are satisfied with centering on one church are also not needed. Even if all thirty million people of the nation are Christians, we need a Christian who can stand as a representative of the nation, and even if all the people of the world are believers in Jesus, we need a representative Christian who can stand on behalf of the 2.4 billion people.

(Page 324)

Let Us Be Those Who Attend the Lord Who Came for All People

Since we are to become qualified to govern all the angels in the spirit world, we must be able to say proudly before them that we have done such a valuable thing. Who came to do this? Jesus Christ came.

Jesus came to do such a great mission, and we must attend him so sincerely, but how have we lived as we look toward him? We have no face. We are so shameless that it is not enough to shed tears for 6,000 years. It will not be enough to beat our chests in sorrow and wail for 6,000 years. We are in such a position, but we should not become people who are utterly shameless.

Even if you die right now, even if you fall and are trampled upon, you must not change your heart of integrity and your heart of loyalty, and you must be able to proudly reveal it before all things in the universe and establish the dignity of the sons and daughters of heaven.

**Sons and Daughters of Integrity and Loyalty**

You have stood on a difficult path. You have stood on a path of destiny that you cannot but go. You who have stood on this path of destiny must go that way with faith and inner loyalty throughout your lives.

You will have to cry. "I must attend a universal Lord, a cosmic Lord, a Lord who can embrace the eternal ideal world beyond the 6,000 years of history, but I have been a person who rejoiced in attending the Lord of the family, or at most, I have only been able to rejoice in attending the Lord of the nation and the state." You must repent and wail, saying this.

Do you feel that you have a responsibility and mission for this age today?

(Page 325)

Or have you ever thought that you must achieve on behalf of all humanity the ideal that they have hoped for from the beginning of creation to the end when the ideal of creation is completed? Have you ever felt such a universal sense of mission?

Furthermore, you must be able to pray with the余裕 of heart, saying, "I am a person who has the confidence to more than fulfill this mission." When you pray from such a position, you do not need many prayers. If there is someone who stands in such a position, everything will be communicated with a single word, "Father!" It means that no explanation is needed. It means that no logic is needed.

We have stood in a position where we must be qualified to step forward and attend without hesitation due to the intuitive shock of the heart before the words are spoken. We have set out with such a treasure. Now that you have started, are you not caught in any conditions? Are you not stopped at some point in the process? How far have you run in the course of your life? You must start from the individual and run through the family, society, nation, and world to heaven and earth. You must know that you have such a universal mission. Only then can you meet the Lord.

When Jesus Christ finds a true person who can attend him, sheds all the sighs of 6,000 years, holds onto him, and sheds tears of gratitude, saying, "Father, here is the being you desired to find. Father! Be joyful," there must be a day before humanity when the glorious answer, "Yes!" comes from heaven.

You who are fighting with that day as your standard must become people who know how to fight today and fight tomorrow and devote your entire lives. Therefore, you must become pioneers, vanguards, and brides of the universe adorned in the course of eternal life, and you must be able to attend the cosmic...
we must become people who can attend the Lord.
Please bear in mind that we must continue to fight until we receive such glory of victory, Father's love, and eternal life, become the bride who represents all things and the entire cosmos, and become the sons and daughters who can share joys and sorrows with Father for eternity. *

Thus, we earnestly pray and desire, Father, that You allow us to become Your sons and daughters who can clearly reveal before all creation that we are sons and daughters in Your stead, and who can stand in for heaven and earth.
Revealing the words You have permitted on this day, please allow our hearts to connect with each other, and allow spirit to move spirit, so that this may be a time when we can be reshaped before the hand of Your power.
