<Sermon> The topic I would like to consider with you is "The Multitudes Chosen for the Restoration of Heaven." I will speak for a short while on this topic, "The Multitudes Chosen for the Restoration of Heaven."

The Last Day of Providential History When We Must Confirm Our Position

Everyone, today we have reached the last Sunday of this year. You know well through the principle of restoration that if we do not complete the mission entrusted to us this year, we must complete it next year, and if we do not fulfill today's responsibility today, we must by all means fulfill it tomorrow.
The history since the creation has passed through 6,000 years, passing through a day, a year, a long period of time, and amidst changing times and seasons. However, you also know well that the great judgment is now unfolding worldwide on this earth, and the providence of restoration that God must complete must be accomplished through you today, through the 2.4 billion people of humankind.

Therefore, the time has come for us, who are facing the last days of the 6,000-year providential history, who have joined to cooperate with the universal history of restoration, and who have stepped forward to fulfill the Will, to now clearly find our own position where we are standing.
Therefore, each of you must now go beyond the 6,000-year history and reach the standard of Adam and Eve, who are the ideal of the final restoration and the center of creation. Furthermore, your families, societies, and all of humanity in the world must all surpass that standard. Before that standard is surpassed, God's providence will not be concluded on this earth.
In this way, we, the descendants of today, must take responsibility for and accomplish in their stead the tremendous and awesome toil of the providence of restoration, the faults committed by our ancestors, and the parts that our ancestors could not handle and left behind. You must feel at this time that you have such a universal mission.
Because of the fall of Adam and Eve, the ideal of heaven was fundamentally destroyed, and the ideal of heaven that was to be perfected through human beings was mercilessly cast down from heaven. And still, we have not found the kingdom of heaven, we have not found the people to build the kingdom of heaven, we have not found the families to form the people, and we have not found the husband and wife, children, and siblings to form the family.

The Restoration of Heaven and a Person's Right Life

Therefore, what is the one central purpose that God demands? It is the restoration of heaven. And the movement to restore the kingdom of heaven must be done in reverse. From the people of heaven, we must restore the children of heaven, the siblings of heaven, the couples of heaven, and the families of heaven to build the kingdom of heaven. This mission remains for us.
The land we live on today, the world we live in today, is not the land of the kingdom of heaven, nor is it the world of the kingdom of heaven. It is not a world centered on God, but a world centered on Satan, a world that opposes the kingdom of heaven. However, the historic watershed where the world of evil is restored to the heaven of goodness will surely appear at the time of the end of history.
Today, the 2.4 billion people of humankind are crossing the hill of restoration from individual restoration to family restoration, social restoration, national restoration, and world restoration, following God's providence, in order to cross this hill of restoration.
The central purpose of the gospel that Jesus Christ came to this earth and preached was also the restoration of heaven. This standard of the restoration of heaven is not only the restoration of you as an individual, but also the restoration of the family, society, nation, world, and even the cosmos beyond the individual. Therefore, from the day you believed in Jesus and stepped forward, you have been on a path of battle for restoration.
The lives of people in the world today are not lives lived for the sake of the world. They say they live for the nation, but they are not living for the nation. They say they live for the family, but they are not living for the family. And they say they live for themselves, but they are not in a position to truly live for themselves.
All human beings in the world of evil today should live for the world, but they are not living that way. Human beings who should live for the country, for the people, for the tribe, for the family, and for themselves have fundamentally lost that position and are living.
Even when people today live centered on themselves, they are not living centered on their minds. When I look at myself, to what extent have I fallen? I have fallen to the extent that I, who should live centered on my mind, am not able to live centered on my mind. I have become a person who lives centered on the body. I have become a person who lives only for my own physical satisfaction.
In order to restore human beings who have fallen in this way, God has been carrying out a history of establishing the body and making it submit to the mind, establishing the individual and making them submit to the family, establishing the family and making it submit to the nation, establishing the nation and making it submit to the world.
Therefore, in any society, individualistic people have stood in opposition to the revolutionary course of believing in Jesus Christ. Also, people who have come out centered on the family have also stood in opposition.
Because God works according to the progress of history, that is, the individual era, the family era, the national era, and the state era, there have been difficult passes in the process of that progress that human beings could not follow.

The Center We Must Strive For and the Order of Restoration

In this age, which is the last day when the 6,000-year history is concluding, the ideology of Jesus Christ has been established on earth as the ideology of the restoration of the entire world. In other words, the ideology centered on Christianity today is appearing as the central ideology of the entire world. However, here, it is receiving a counterattack from the ideology of the enemy, and these two paths are fighting.
Then, what standard should we, who are in this position today, strive for? Looking through the hope of Jesus Christ, who established the ideology of the restoration of heaven, the ideal garden we must go to is not just this world. The standard of the ideal restoration that God is trying to find is not just this earth. It is a garden of ideology where heaven and earth have united and become one, not two. Therefore, God has been carrying out His providence until now to find one day of glory when we can harmonize and sing centered on heaven.
What is it that we, who are in such a time today, must know? It is that our one body must indemnify and restore all things of the history of sin.
When you believe in Jesus and step forward, an individual battle will unfold. A battle between body and mind will unfold. Those who become dropouts in that battle cannot become people of the kingdom of heaven. When the evil movement centered on the body tries to subjugate the mind, if you cannot subjugate it and win, you cannot become a person of the kingdom of heaven.
Today, we have the mission to restore from the world to the nation, from the nation to the people, from the people to the family, from the family to the couple, and from the couple to the children and siblings.

Because there is this principled standard of God's ideal of heaven, we must first restore ourselves.
"The kingdom of heaven is in your mind," He said, so we must complete the universal kingdom of heaven, but first, we must complete the individual kingdom of heaven. What is that? It means to become a being who can stand before the universe by establishing the relative standard of body and mind.
Therefore, you can now be absorbed into and harmonize with any field of the entire ideal of heaven. To speak of a single tree, Jesus is the vine and we are the branches of the vine, and we must have the form of a branch belonging to any aspect. Thus, for you, the branches, to go through the trunk, this is restoration.

The Stage of Restoration as a Citizen of Heaven

Now, what is the very first stage you must find? It is the stage of becoming a citizen of heaven. The destiny to enter the stage of a citizen of heaven lies before you. You must have a new historical consciousness. My one existence should not be for myself, but I must have the concept of being for the fellow countrymen of the kingdom of heaven, who are the people of heaven. Not only that, but I must have the concept of striving for the siblings of the kingdom of heaven, for the couples of the kingdom of heaven, and for the parents of the kingdom of heaven. That is not a partial concept, but a universal concept. You must have such a universal concept.
Also, if you live belonging to a society today, you must have a social consciousness, and if you live belonging to a nation, you must have a national consciousness. If you live belonging to one nation, you must know how to love the people of that nation.
Today, we must become people who can assert our will with our mind and body before God, who is providing for the construction of the kingdom of heaven. We must know how to love the people of the kingdom of heaven. We must know how to have the recognition that we exist for the construction of the kingdom of heaven, for the restoration of the world, which is the Father's will.

We should not just blindly follow Jesus as people who believe in him, but we must become people who can believe in Jesus by harmonizing with the fortunes of heaven and earth, both internally and externally. God is establishing the ideology of the restoration of heaven centered on the universal providence. We must become the sons and daughters, and the people who can stand there. And we must know how to love our fellow countrymen of the kingdom of heaven.
If there are believing people among the multitudes next to you and around you, you must become people who know how to regard them as siblings and fellow countrymen. Also, you must make all people do so. When you see this, your responsibility is immeasurably great.
Then, what is it that God demands of us today, the last day? It is for the believing saints to be mobilized to build the garden of heaven. Therefore, individuals must unite and peoples must unite to form the fellow countrymen of heaven. You must know this.
Looking at the 6,000-year history vertically, in the Old Testament era, He gathered the people of heaven, and in the New Testament era, He gathered the children of heaven. In this way, history has flowed in reverse.
In the world today, there are people who are trying to build the kingdom of heaven centered on the ideology of the fellow countrymen of heaven. There are also people who are trying to build the kingdom of heaven based on the ideology of the children of heaven, the siblings of heaven, and the couples of heaven.

The Standard of the Law of Heaven and the Standard of Life in Heaven

Now, you must know how to keep the law of heaven in your life. You must know how to keep the law of heaven for the construction of the kingdom of heaven, which heaven demands. Also, at the same time as knowing how to keep the law of heaven, you must know how to live a life in heaven. And at the same time as knowing how to live a life in heaven, you must become one with the love of heaven.
Then, what should we center on to keep the law of heaven as God has been working until now to restore the kingdom of heaven? We must keep the law of heaven centered on the words of the Bible that were transmitted to us through Jesus.
The Word is the law of heaven, so we must live centered on the Word. Your path is here. In particular, you must live keeping the law of heaven centered on the words of the Principle, which testify to the internal facts through the words of the Bible.
Then, how should we live? A life in place of Jesus' 30-some years of life.
we must do. Your life today, in the last days, must be a life that testifies to Jesus Christ. Therefore, you must be able to show your life before all people. You must also live the same kind of life that Jesus showed us.
You should emulate the life of Jesus, who kept the law centered on the word of God, and live a life for Heaven by living a life of harmony.
Therefore, you must now live a life that represents the life of Jesus, centered on the word, which is the law of Heaven. Your hope and ideal must be the love of God. Therefore, in order to connect with God's love, you must establish conditions of harmony. This is what God is demanding of all Christians in the world today.
The sap of one branch flows to other branches. It circulates to every leaf and every branch. Likewise, we must become people who know how to live in harmony with and for each other. Such a person will be able to possess the love of God that remains as an ideal.

Discard the self-centered mindset

Therefore, we Christians must abandon the self-centered concept of the individual and have a new concept that my one self is a being that represents the world and the universe.
Therefore, even when we look at our members, we must know that they are not who they are today. You should feel the fact that they represent 6,000 years of history, the eternal providence, and on a horizontal level, the 2.4 billion people of humanity. In any one person, there is the will of the promise of God's universal love.

That is why you must be a co-worker before such a person. Since you have such a mission, you must be able to see the will of God's providence correctly and become a group that represents that will.
This is also true in your personal and family life. Your own children, your own parents, and your spouse do not exist for you. Your children are not for you, your siblings are not for you, and your parents are the same. They exist for the sake of the cosmos, beyond the nation and the world.
We must know this and know how to treat our children, siblings, and parents from that perspective. If you recognize this fact and feel it in your life, you will not be able to judge anyone with words.
We must not forget that in each of us there is the universal will of God. You must all live a life of unity, knowing that my one existence is not for myself, but for the world, for heaven and earth, a being that represents the mission of restoration.
Today, you who have come out on a so-called different path must now depart from a self-centered life. You must discard the self-centered mindset. Our Unification Church must also discard a view of life centered only on the Unification Church. This is because we are all cells and molecules of the universe.
Today, in the last days, we must feel the historical action, the providential action of the heavenly law, and the action of God's total love. And you must establish your one body and become a victor in the universal battle with Satan. Only then can you become a necessary being in the garden of the kingdom of heaven, and at that time, the kingdom of heaven will have a relationship with you. You must know that Jesus Christ came and went to fulfill this one hope, and that the Trinity of God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit are working together and fighting Satan to accomplish this one hope.
Today, when you try to fight Satan, you must discern whether the thoughts you have, the concepts you have, and all your principles are for yourselves or not.

Those chosen for the restoration of the kingdom of heaven

You will have no way to escape from the realm of Satan.
And we Christians who are advancing toward the world must also go beyond the world's internal historical consciousness. We must go beyond that and become people who can grasp and feel the world with a universal historical consciousness.

Blessed are the peacemakers

Then what will the world for restoration be like? What will the society for restoration, the family for restoration, and I for restoration be like? What is God's will for restoration? You must be people who know and go beyond all these things. To do so, you must live by the word, have the serving heart of Jesus Christ, and be able to bring about harmony with one another. Jesus said, "Blessed are the peacemakers, for they shall be called sons of God" (Matthew 5:9).
Anyone who knows how to make peace wherever they go can draw near to God. You have the responsibility to bring harmony to every individual, the responsibility to bring harmony to the entire nation, the responsibility to bring harmony to the world, and the responsibility to bring harmony to heaven and earth.
If you do not feel this practical responsibility in your living environment, you must feel it in your heart. You must have the heart to become a sacrifice that can bring harmony to each individual, a sacrifice that can bring harmony to each family, a sacrifice that can bring harmony to each society, a sacrifice that can bring harmony to each nation, and a sacrifice that can bring harmony to the entire world. Thus, you must become a person who has a heart that can stand before the Father in opposition to Satan.
If you live in such a relationship, when you see someone doing a good deed, you will feel like bowing your head and honoring them. And when you see someone doing a bad deed, you will feel that it is your job to guide that person. I will take responsibility. If there is a person who lives while experiencing this fact, he does not have to pray for himself. He does not have to pray for his family. If each of you makes a resolution and a vow to build the kingdom of heaven that God has hoped for on this earth, and lives for it, God will be with you.
Therefore, if there is a nation that knows how to build an altar of harmony by holding hands, that nation will start a vigorous new revolution toward the world. The church will also be like that. If there is a group of people who hold hands, follow the example of Christ, and are determined to die to become a sacrifice of harmony, their steps may seem like they will fail and break, but that is not the case. Their steps are firm steps toward the construction of the kingdom of heaven on earth.
Jesus Christ came to this earth shouldering the amazing mission of heaven and earth. In the course of 4,000 years of history, when there was no loyal subject for heaven and no filial son for heaven, Jesus Christ was the one who came to fulfill the mission as the one loyal subject and filial son that heaven required.
Jesus' life of about 30 years was a life for heaven. And it was a worldwide and universal life. Also, his life was a life of a sacrifice for heaven. Therefore, you must emulate Jesus Christ, who came as a filial son for heaven, which was unprecedented in history.
The Father's will is to establish the kingdom of heaven. What is the kingdom of heaven? It is a world where all of humanity holds hands, is in harmony, is reconciled with each other, is entangled in one love, raises their hands together, gives glory to heaven, and lives in gratitude. When we think about this, the life of faith that we have believed in and come out with today has been a very immature life of faith. Now we must liquidate that immature life of faith.

God who aims for the ideology of unification

Now, the era of any denominationalism has passed. The era of any nationalism has passed. The time has come when we must seek a worldwide ideology of restoration, a worldwide ideology of faith.

Those chosen for the restoration of the kingdom of heaven

Today, the Korean people are a pitiful nation. What this pitiful people must know is that God's history is a history of breaking the individual to establish the family, breaking the family to establish society, breaking that society to establish the nation, and breaking the nation to find and establish the world. This is the judgment of heaven.
Humanity has gone through judgment like this, but what is the final problem that remains? It is to completely break the line of Cain out of the two lines of Cain and Abel that have fought in opposition. Therefore, you must become different people centered on the words of Jesus. You must become different people by establishing the words of Jesus as the law. You must all become loyal subjects of heaven and filial sons of heaven who represent the life of Jesus.
Thus, you must be able to go before God, who aims for the ideology of unification, and say, "God, please resolve through me the resentment of not being able to embrace and love the world as one until now." However, Christians today do not know that they have such a great historical, universal, and cosmic mission before them.
Then to what extent have you revealed the love of Jesus Christ today? To what extent have you equipped yourselves with the faith and life that come from Jesus? You must know that limit.
The grace that comes from Jesus is a universal grace. Therefore, today we must live with a consciousness of the kingdom of heaven. You must live with a central heart and concept that "I am a representative of the kingdom of heaven" in all your actions and even all your feelings today.
Even when you are cursed by all people and your anger flares up, you must suppress it with the feeling that if you get angry, all 2.4 billion people will be cursed. Heaven has come until now with that feeling. If you know this fact and still get angry, lose your temper, and disobey God's will, what will happen? All the members must unite and cooperate with each other.
Is someone in difficulty? You must feel that person's difficulty as if you were wounded in your own body. And you must cooperate.

This should not be done only by the Korean people. All of humanity must cooperate.
You must go the way for the restoration of the kingdom of heaven. You must become sons and daughters who live receiving the love of the cosmos. Next, you must know how to attend God, who is the center of the cosmos. The God you are crying out to, the Jesus Christ you are seeking and believing in, is not a God for you alone, nor a Jesus Christ for you alone. However, people who believe in Jesus today do not know that. They know him only as a Jesus for themselves, a God for themselves.
However, that is not God's hope. That is not God's will. God's position is the center of all heaven and earth. Today, you must know how to attend God in that way. However, that will only be possible for those who live a life in the kingdom of heaven.

A correct faith in God

Then what is the reason why God has providentially guided the 6,000-year history? It was to embrace the entire history in His one bosom. Not only on earth but also in the spirit world, He is a God who has longed for the day when the whole would become one in His love. If you want to receive grace from this God, you must pray, "Father! Please call me."
God's love must not stop with you. What you must know today is that the gifts that heaven has given are not for you alone. They are to save you and at the same time to save all of humanity.
However, because people today live centered on themselves, although many people want to seek God, there are almost no people who have received grace. Today, we must break away from this. We must break through this and serve the cosmic God as the cosmic God. We must feel a responsibility that pierces our bodies and minds before this universal God.

Those chosen for the restoration of the kingdom of heaven

The garden of hope that you believe in and hope for is not a garden of hope for you alone. The archangel fell because he tried to seek and believe in God centered on himself.
The God that humanity believes in today is my God and at the same time the God of humanity. He is our God and at the same time the worldwide God, and the worldwide God and at the same time the God of heaven and earth. At the same time, He is the universal Parent.
However, when we look at the faith of people who believe in Jesus today, they are saying, "Be my God," and at most, they have only gone as far as "the God of our family."
Be this. That is what they are saying. Going a little further, they say, 'Be the God of our denomination.' We must not have such a concept.

Today, there are many denominations in the world that cry out to God. However, the God they cry out to within the realm of their denominations is no longer needed. Only when those beings gather who can believe in and call upon that one being as the center of the whole universe, transcending denominations, beings who are qualified to call God their own Father on behalf of the whole, can we attend God on this earth.

Therefore, today, we must make the concepts we feel within ourselves connect to the whole through the family. You who have entered a new path must now cast aside your life until now and make a new historical start toward a universal life concept.

At such a time, what kind of heart should you have? You must have a heart that can attend the universal existence of God. Thus, you must be able to receive God's love and form a relationship where you and God can give and receive. Only then can you conclude the ideal of the universal bride.

Only after concluding the ideal of the universal bride can you go to find the restored world. However, only by restoring the nation, the people, the siblings, and even the children and the couple, can I appear as a bride before the universal existence of God. Only by going to that position can I stand before the universal existence of God, centered on the love of God that emanates from there, and become one with that love.



Thus, the couple that is united is the couple that can rule this earth and live in the kingdom of heaven. Also, only by giving birth to children as such a couple will they build a heavenly family, and only by forming a people with such siblings and children can they finally conclude the providence of restoration and live a life in the kingdom of heaven on earth.

Such a great movement for the restoration of the kingdom of heaven is being presented through you today. Therefore, you must strive even harder to fulfill that will and not be servile before Satan. Just as Jesus Christ fulfilled the duty of a loyal subject and a filial son for the sake of one will, we too must be equipped with the duty of a loyal subject and a filial son.

To Complete the Restoration of the Kingdom of Heaven and Offer the Glory of Victory

And you must clearly know that not only this nation, but all of humanity in the world, and furthermore, all the spirits in the spirit world, must be made to know how to fulfill the duty of loyalty and the duty of a filial son to Heaven, so that you can become a son, a child, a sibling, a family, or a nation that can offer the glory of victory for completing the restoration of the kingdom of heaven before the Father.

<Prayer> Loving Father, today we must now run. We lack strength, but we are facing such a tremendous historical end where we must leap over dozens of stages at once. Even though I stand in a position where I must splendidly overcome the course of judgment, today we are in a deep sleep.

Father, we are intoxicated with the world. We are accompanied by sin. Father, we earnestly hope and desire that you will establish us as a victor who can offer the glory of victory before the Father, who is the center of the universe, after liquidating all these evil elements.



For the Restoration of the Kingdom of Heaven, the Chosen People

All historical circumstances are entangled in our bodies today. Father, we earnestly hope and desire that you will establish us as a body of joy that can worship before the Father, standing in the position of a friend of Jesus Christ, by cutting them off and equipping ourselves with the center of liberation.

We whom you have chosen for the restoration of the kingdom of heaven, please do not let us become those who live by trampling on the heavenly ideal centered on our own selves. Please allow us to go on and on, sacrifice and sacrifice, fight and fight until we achieve that ideal, and please allow us to endure, fight, and win until we can attend you as the universal Father. Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.

Father, please govern our hearts forever. Now, through the new universal standard of life, please allow us to become sons and daughters who can offer thanks and worship before the Father, who is the center of the whole, and who can be immersed in the Father's love. We earnestly ask this, and we have reported all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen. *
